Numis'OM ~ Eye of Metatron: a Cosmic Streaming
Informational Archives

Introduction
Numis'OM is the current name of the 4th dimensional intermediary stage of ascension into the 5th dimensional New Earth Star reality. Numis'OM is a name given to me by my mentor Thoth for this reality zone and it is integrated into the etheric body of Venus, Earth's Guardian. The Numis'OM streaming thus represents an inter-dimensional connection I have which then facilitates a flow of energy from the reality of Numis'OM as we prepare for the LP-40 planetary ascension. From early 2006 through mid-2009 I produced a quaterly ezine by the name "Numis'OM ˜ Eye of Metatron" to facilitate this streaming for others and the planet.

The Numis'OM ˜ Eye of Metatron quarterly ezine subscriptions have now been transformed into our 44:44 Ascension Portal. Access to all the archived issues of the quarterly ezine we produced over 3 years appear in the archives below are available in the 44:44 Ascension Portal.

About This Publication

Please use the NEW "Printer Friendly Version" link in the menu bar on the front cover page above to make a quality print ofthis publication.
We were guided to name this publicationNumis'OM ~ Eye of Metatronby Thoth, and theIllumined Assembly of the Christos'Merkabah of the Host comprised of 12 souls holding open a portal for the the Christ energies on this planet.
The Radiant Ones we are working with encouraged us to bring forth this publication  as a continuance of work that was done byMaia Christianne Nartoomidfrom 1980 through 1999. During this period Maia produced, first, the periodical entitledThe Source[1980-1988], and then later,Temple Doors[1989-1999]. In 1994Simeon Nartoomidjoined her in producing the latter periodical.
In the nearly 7 year respite between the conclusion ofTemple Doorsand  when the first release ofNumis'OM ~ Eye of Metatronbegan, we both  underwent a period of expanded esoteric initiation and deeply personal transformational experiences that have prepeared us for resuming this work at an entirely new octave of experience.
Thoth and the IAC Merkabah of the Host  have requested that we facilitate a specific Program of Light related to the Aramu Temple of Thoth and Numis'OM to help those who feel resonant with this Station of Light [Spirit Heart Sanctuary] to accelerate their Ascension processes and thus to further help the collective soul of humanity approach the gateway of Ascension which Thoth callsLight-Principle Forty, or LP-40 for short. Ultimately, as we collectively move through this passage we will activate the44:44 Ascension Stargateand trigger a series of cosmic events destined to alter the DNA of humanity forever.
Numis'OM is a causal reference point for the New Earth Star and the 44:44 stargate, and is hosted within the causal body of Venus. TheAramu Temple of Thothis energetically within the Numis'OM matrix and acts as a way-station for souls building the New Earth Star consciousness from within the earthen experience. Souls can thus visit Numis'OM and even the New Earth Star if they have proper intent and attunement. It is our goal to provide pathways for this to occur within.
This publication thus sits at the heart of our efforts to facilitate this greater process for the Masters and Illumined Ones that we are working with and to assist souls on earth.   We hope that you will find it a fruitful and friendly path into the Homeward Light.
The lower front cover art on this issue is entitled "Eye of Metatron" by Maia Christianne Nartoomid. The upper front cover banner art is by Simeon Nartoomid.
All of the art that appears on the lower front cover and in the various articles in this issue is  available on theSubscriber's Freebies and Discountspage while this issue is current. After this volume becomes a back issue the art that appears in it will then only be available through ourSpirit StoreIF it has an associated item number.  Click the item number of the art piece to find it there if it no longer appears on the Subscriber's Freebies and Discounts page.

The Golden Lotusby Maia NartoomidARSY-0015STD
Numis'OM, The Temple of Aramuand the Shamballah GatebyMaia Christianne Nartoomid

Numis'OM is the name given to me by Thoth to call earth's double of etheric energy that is the staging ground or outer membrane for the developingNew Earth Starrealm. We are currently building the hologram of the New Earth.
As the hologram develops, so it evolves the "membrane" of the Numis'OM, which in turn, transfers these frequencies and sacred geometries into the developing New Earth Star.
Numis'OM means:gathering of the many aspects of the holy word or tone in one breath, one movement of being.
The merging seed of the blue ray of earth with the violet ray of Numis'OM creates the blue-violet or INDIGO ray/flame of the New Earth Star.
The Temple of Aramu (divine fire bird) and the Numis'OM in Volume 1, 1997 of Temple Doors:
"Thoth asks us to return to the first information he gave me concerning the ‘New Earth Star’. This appeared in Volume 2, 1991 of Temple Doors. Maia had received some understanding of the planet’s movement toward that evolution previously, but in Temple Doors Volume 2, 1991 he gives the name  ‘New Earth Star’ for the first time, and a more detailed description of the actual condition. We reprint that information here for the readers convenience, as it must be read again first to truly understand what Thoth is saying now about that dynamic."
The New Earth Star from Volume 2, 1991 of Temple Doors:
We are approaching a ‘gate of completion’ when the etheric double of this planet which has been developing on the inner planes for some time, will be ready to receive its first major contact-point with its twin world, our elemental Earth. This first revolution of synchronization will occur on January 11, 1992. In Volume 4, 1985 of The Source (original name of Temple Doors), information was given on what was then called ‘Altheria’, Earth's double of etheric energy which the Egyptians referred to as the ‘KA’.
The Egyptians used this term to refer to any etheric double, such as that of humans and animals, not particularly in describing the double of the Earth itself. This etheric image of Earth is growing, like a crystal in a sunlit cave, refracting the light of the planet’s inner harmonics, transforming the pollution and violence as it interacts with the etheric plane, and straining out the bilge of our confused karmic patterns, thus producing the purest elixir of our true Ark of Illumination - the ‘New Earth Star’ (NES). The completion of the New Earth Star will not take place until this elemental earthen sphere merges with its supernal double.
The planet’s KA is no longer Altheria, for it has progressed into a more defined and rarefied state, known now as 'Numis'OM'. When the Blue Ray of our Earth is fully integrated with the Violet Ray of Numis'OM, there will burst forth into a glorious Blue-Violet Flame, the ‘Iris Eye’. This is the bonding flame of the New Earth Star, when our world and its supernal form will join at the apex of the Metatronic Spiral, through the ‘eye of the needle’ - the Iris Eye. Through what Solara of Star-Borne refers to as the "Healing of Orion", we as an inspirited world, will be able to de-polarize our consciousness so that we can enter the Iris-Eye, where all polarities are ONE....
I was allowed to visit this pre-world, and saw rivers of blue substance flowing like curves of taffy, suspended in the air of a blue sky. I was inside what could only be described as a ‘flying van’, with a guide, who glided us through one of these rivers, explaining that it was a semi-fluid / semi-gas of special protein compounds from which properties of the world were being constructed. Below the ‘rivers’ were strips of greenery, like floating terrariums. We then flew through a ‘cloud’ and below suddenly appeared ‘solid’ land. It was a beautiful plain with a few large cliffs near the bluest river I had ever seen. Homes were built alongside the expanse of lapis water. They were widely spaced, giving the impression of a frontier atmosphere. I almost expected to see buffalo thundering upon the horizon at any moment. The buildings, however, were refined and spacious, similar to what might be found in a rustic, upper class residential area.  I saw no people, but rather seemed to feel their presence. I knew that by comparison to a normally inhabited planet, this world had few residents at this time.
The ‘Totemic’ animals of the New Earth Star, who are aiding us to receive that supernal state of Self, are the Dolphin, the Unicorn, and the Dove.
* * * * *
I wish to stress that in Numis'OM as well as the New Earth Star realm completed, all is formed through thought, or really as sense beyond how we "think" in the body. The "houses" I saw were not built with hammer and nails, but through what the physic mediums of the late 18th and early 19th century called "ectoplasm", being gathered and  
      organized through supra-luminal thought forms. Masters of Tibet and India create certain small objects in this fashion here, in this dimension. So can one who is discarnate and within the realms of pure spirit being.
In 2006 I ask of Thoth:
Maia:What is the Temple of Aramu like?
Thoth:It is a pure energy streaming light-divine from the font of Metatron which assumes a specific pattern within my Akasha field. In this "pure streaming" of light-divine, so I set certain forms into place for the souls who are attracted into my Aramu Temple, due to their own soul harmonics which resonate with my field and that which I represent universally. These "forms" (ectoplasmic creations) are basic and will morph into various attitudes and detail for the individual soul interacting with them. However, there is a basic flow and pattern which I present here, which helps to stabilize and open attracted souls to a greater level of their Realization in the Numis’Om.
Maia:I understand that souls who have transitioned the body here in this dimensional earth do sometimes enter Numis’Om (and thus those so attracted, enter into the Aramu Temple). How is this selection made?
Thoth: Souls who transition your earth dimension may be attracted to any of the "astral" worlds of earth, where most dis-incarnate souls go. However, some are indeed "ready" to enter into Numis'OM. One need not be a master being to do so. It is a matter of willingess to surrender to the vibration I call here the lotus stalk. This "stalk" is a funnel, pathway, streaming into Numis'OM. It holds a certain vibration of commitment. When souls feel this pull, many will turn away from it and go elsewhere, as they are simply not yet surrendered to it's potential. Other souls will find that they can surrender and move into the stalk. The "lotus" in this perspective, is the Numis’Om / New Earth Star.  It was also the symbol for Mu, the Motherland of humankind on earth. In the context of Mu / Numis'OM / New Earth Star  is not only symbolic of tranquility, harmony, unfolding love to reach the heart-seed, but is a true living energy form or sacred geometry of HEART LIGHT.
As the soul moves through various stages of the Numis'OM (via the "temples" of the Master Intelligences), so the number of "petals" on the lotus will change and well as the color vibration of the lotus and it's associated pure symbols. The soul will at first dwell inside the lotus and then the lotus will dwell inside the soul.
Maia:Can currently incarnated souls interact with the Numis'OM and the Temple of Aramu and / or other Numis'OM temples of "Master Intelligences"? If so, will this interaction benefit them by preparing their souls to possible choose entry into Numis'OM when they "slip the body" in this life?
Thoth:Yes, this is so. However it is important that the individual realize that wherever their soul ultimately chooses to journey and alight after their current incarnation it will be a loving experience and right for them, if they so BELIEVE and TRUST in the divine balance of the Eternal Love. Even if they do not enter what we are calling here "Numis'OM" after this embodiment, attuning to it's frequencies of LIGHT and LOVE will allow the soul a deeper feeling and embodiment of those frequencies into it's incarnating being, so that the whole process of "alighting" in an astral earth, current earth embodiment, or Numis'OM, will become a more graceful and expanded experience of BEING.Maia:Could you give a procedure or series of procedures to help engender the Numis'OM within the being of the individual incarnate now on this earth? To not only prepare the for their eventual transition from current incarnation, but to aid them in becoming a more aware and light-engendered being in their present life experience?
Thoth:This can be given.
NOTE:As a result of Thoth's affirmative on this question I am currently planning on creating "The Ascension Lotus Loci" Spirit Tool. This tool will offer a means of harmonically infusing your DNA with the key vibrational reference points or "loci" held within Thoth's Temple of Aramu located energetically in the Numis'OM portal for the New Earth Star. This will thus be a serious tool for working with higher level Ascension energetics via the streaming of consciousness offered by my Illumined Mentor, Thoth. This Spirit Tool will be made available to all current subscribers when it is ready.
Thoth:The Iris Eye - Indigo Flame can also be understood as the "Eye of Metatron", for it is the point of synthesis with the Metatronic frequency.
According toThe Shamballah Schoolthe word "Shamballah" 
      refers to "the planetary crown chakra, the 'center where the Will of God is known.'" Simeon received that the "Shamballah Gate" was the portal in the memebrane between this world / universe and what Thoth calls the attasic universe.
According to my receipt from Thoth, the "attasic" is the universe of non-duality, of completion, of Perfection and Light. In this regard, the Shamballah Gate serves a similar purpose to the Numis'OM in it's membrane function to the New Earth Star.
Thoth:The Shamballah Gate actually contains the entry point into the Numis'OM. You could see this "gate" somewhat like a control panel. On the panel there are various buttons / nodes that if pressed / triggered, open specific frequency vectors. One of these vectors is the lotus stalk or streaming into Numis'OM. (mentioned earlier in this article)
In Volume 2, 1991 of Temple Doors I gave the following guided visualization to aid in connecting to the expanding potential and harmonics of the Numis'OM:
(chant five times)LIVING IN GOD'S HEART TOGETHER (L.I.G.H.T.)
(chant three times)WE WORK TOGETHER TO MERGE OUR EARTH OF THE BLUE RAY WITH THE VIOLET RAY OF NUMIS'OM. IN THIS, WE CREATE THE NEW 
      EARTH STAR
(chant seven times)LIVING IN GOD'S HEART TOGETHER (L.I.G.H.T.)As you chant these words, visualize yourself upon the blue sphere of Earth, within a golden spiral, in deep space.
See the many galaxies of stars in the distance, burning as one chorus in the celestial kingdom. Look UP the spiral, above your head.
Here you see the Iris-Eye. You must harmonize the Blue Ray of your natal being - regardless of your star heritage, you are now Earth's child - with the Blue-Violet Flame of the Iris-Eye. Beyond lies Numis'OM, awaiting to become the New Earth Star. Remember, that the New Earth Star cannot ‘BE’ without us, for it is our purest potion that has created the Numis'OM. Those who now exist within this pre-formed planet are the Kindred Ones, many of them having lived on our Earth. They are all truly illumined beings and part of our genetic vine.

Venus Gateby Simeon Nartoomid
Numis'OM and the Venus GatebySimeon Nartoomid

On June 8th of 2004 the collective consciousness of earth entered into what my mentors are referring to as the "Venus Gate."  The Venus Gate spans the space of time which graces the time period between two astronomical Venus Transits.  The first of the current pair of transits which opened the "Venus Gate" occurred on June 8, 2004. The second of these transits will occur on June 6, 2012, somewhat preceding the end of the Mayan Calendar on December 21, 2012.
From theNASA Eclipse website:
"Transits of Venus across the disk of the Sun are among the rarest of planetary alignments. Indeed, only six such events have occurred since the invention of the telescope (1631, 1639, 1761, 1769, 1874 and 1882). . . .Transits show a clear pattern of recurrence at intervals of 8, 121.5, 8 and 105.5 years. The next pair of Venus transits occur over a century from now on 2117 Dec 11 and 2125 Dec 08."
Do all Venus Transits represent a "Venus Gate"? In a sense they do from the standpoint that they always present an energetic opportunity for sentient and conscious beings within the influence of these transits to interact more directly with the powerful archetypal presence of Venus and her animating principleIshkea.
However, I have been made aware by theIAC Merkabah of the Hostthat this particular Venus Gate is somewhat of a "mega" Venus Gate.  They point to the fact that it is occurring at the end of a significant cycle [in the Mayan calendar, a cycle of 13 baktun, or roughly 5,126 years] just preceding the end of the Mayan Calendar. Also indicated was that the collective consciousness of the earth is rapidly approaching a point of critical Light-Quantum which the Venus Gate is facilitating in a very powerful way.
Numis'OM is a portal within an energy membrane which exists between the earth we consciously know today and the ascended reality of the New Earth Star. Numis'OM is also the Metatronic double, or KA, for planet earth. The earth's Metatronic [non-dualistic] "causal double," Numis'OM, is hosted within the causal body of Venus as the guardian of the earth and her closest celestial sister in Light. The earth's Oritronic [dualistic] etheric double or KA is hosted right here in the earth's etheric body.
Knowing that Numis'OM is our Metatronic double and is hosted within the causal body of Venus allows us to understand more clearly that the current Venus Gate has a significant relationship to Numis'OM and what it represents in our earthen human experience.  In exploring this connection further with the Merkabah of the Host they have indicated that the current Venus Gate is ushering in a "Cycle of Divine Grace" and that the development of Numis'OM from its previous "Altheria" vibration was triggered by the precursory energy currents setting up in preparation for the current Venus Gate.
Numis'OM is deepening its violet register during this current eight year Venus Gate and will be shifting its color more towards the indigo vibration of the New Earth Star near the end of this Venus Gate.  The vibration of the current earth is deep sky blue, and as we collectively orient towards Numis'OM that color begins to merge into the currently pure violet frequency of Numis'OM. When this process has reached a specific point of coherence the stage will be set for higher Light dynamics to then trigger what Thoth refers to as Light Principle Forty, or LP-40 for short. This is "Thoth speak" for the collective Ascension of the planetary consciousness and all Light-engendered matter on earth.
The New Earth Star and its intermediary stage, Numis'OM, are thus ultimately the product of a high level alchemy of sorts taking place on a grand cosmic scale that enlists the collective consciousness of humanity to participate as a catalyst. The Universe provides the raw energy materials, but humanity must supply the impetus and right vibrational codes to allow the finest of the human experience to be extracted from the baser substance of our collective history.  This means that the aspects of the human experience throughout time on planet earth which resonate with phi harmonics [Universal Love] must be extracted from the akashic fields of the earth and transported to Numis'Om and finally into the New Earth Star.
In a sense we are taking the best of our human experience with us, and letting the rest go.  The Venus Gate is a powerful energetic dynamic that is greatly facilitating this process. As we are focusing our attention upon the vibrational energies of Numis'OM we would do well to keep the energies of the Venus Gate within our field of conscious perception. These energies will be present regardless, but we can accentuate their vibrational register in our experience by consciously engaging them.
Given that Venus, and the current Venus Gate, are a significant conduit of Divine Grace within this solar system we will do well to consciously work with these dynamics to facilitate our other efforts to transform planet earth.  The transformative process we are all engaged in is first and foremost an inside job.  Love is what ultimately matters, and Venus has been portrayed in association with various forms of love for many millennium for good reason.
While the animating principle or soul of the earth is know most commonly as "Gaia," the soul presence of Venus is "Ishkea."  The planet Venus was named after theRoman Goddess of Loveby the same name and later the Greeks had their own version with Aphrodite.  I have been made aware that the use of the name Venus by the Romans was the first inkling of the planetary mass consciousness connecting more firmly into the Ishkea vibration and attempting to relate to it in the current cycle of consciousness evolution.
Numis'OM, is in a sense the aggregation of all earthen thoughts, feelings and acts of love that register in harmonic with phi. For love to be in resonance with phi it must be operating in an expanded enough field of awareness that little or no short or long term limitations arise from it.  This is a large topic unto itself and could be the topic for a future article in this publication. For now, probably the best way to demonstrate this is with an example. Let's say someone has a friend who is having some sort of great difficulty in their life. So this someone decides to help this friend because they really care about them.  They provide this help to their friend, then many years later when the friend is doing well and they are not, they then discover  a feeling within them that their friend should now be helping them because of the assistance they provided to the friend in the past.
What this example demonstrates is a subtle level of a limited form of love expressing in the human experience. The portion of the love that harbored the expectation that the favor should be returned by the friend at some point, unbeknownst to its bearer until a later time, does not resonate with phi.  In the midst of that limited field of love, however, is also a pure seed of love in phi resonance which can be made stronger if it is recognized.  We can see that Metatronic seed demonstrated in the example by the person's initial impulse to help their friend which was motivated by their true caring for that person.
So this is one of our goals. We need to become aware of the limitations that exist in our love, yet we also need to become more focused upon the pure Metatronic seed within them and give THAT as much energy as possible. By doing so this seed will become the stronger and more powerful form of love in our experience. As we engage this type of conscious activity we are also forming Numis'OM, giving it greater strength in its vibrational register and aligning ourselves and our planet into its embrace.
In conclusion, I would like to make one clarification. Many people would refer to this pure form of love which resonates with phi as "unconditional love."  That is an apt term if it is properly understood. I have, however, found that there is a lot of misconceptions about this term. Unconditional love means nothing more than what the term literally indicates: love given without any conditions placed upon it.  This is often interpreted to mean that we should not in any way receive anything in return, period.  This is actually impossible because through the Universal Law of Return good energies will always return to you when you have truly loved in an expanded manner. As the Master once said: "as you give so shall you receive."
We will do well then to stay open to the bountiful flow of the Universe as we open up our love into more expanded fields of awareness and expression.  As we love in this way we will magnetically draw all that we need to us and should EXPECT that to happen. It is important to also be aware that such return may not necessarily come through the same person or channel we extended our love to originally. We limit ourselves if we place conditions at any level upon the love we give. But this is different than saying we should not expect a Universal return in response to our love. This Universal response will embrace us in Its own time and way. Keep in mind also that these energies may not return into our experience until a "future" life cycle.
Yet, we can clearly experience all of the past and all the future in the sacred NOW.  Numis'OM will most clearly be found there, in your heart, right now, as you elevate your love into higher fields of awareness, intelligence and consciousness. Love guided by these more expanded states of being is a power that cannot be surpassed in all the Universe. This is where you start to realize more of your God nature and clearly enter the realm of Numis'OM.

Star Lionby Maia NartoomidAB-0031STD
Star Lions of Numis'OmbyMaia Christianne Nartoomid

Murry Hope, in her book "The Lion People - Intercosmic Messengers from the Future" writes about the lion-like beings from Sirius. She calls them the Pashat. Through my akashic insights and communion with Thoth, I have written on the Lion-Headed "Sun Lords" of Sirius, who guardian the energetic capstone (Telos.Aarkhara) set over the "Eye of Ra" - a universal locus, which has been exposed to instability since the universal tear, or schism of space-time in this universal eons ago. The Telos.Aarkhara has been created by Universal Intelligences to keep this "eye" or node in balance. The Sun Lords, or a faction of them, use their tremendous energy focus to constantly re-calibrate the capstone.
In the Timbavati region of South Africa sometime over 400 years ago, during the reign of Queen Numbi, there was seen a streaking light in the heavens, falling to earth. Not longer after this, the golden lions of Timbavati began giving birth to pure white offspring. The African Elders call these white lions “Tsimba-vaati”, which in the ancient Shangaan language means “the place where star lions came down from the heavens”. They also refer to them as the "Children of the Sun God."
From the Akasha it has been revealed to me that the "star lions" of Timbavati were seeded into the then-present golden lion population by the Sirian Sun Lords through a cosmic event in the skies over Africa. This event consisted of an merkabah of pure energy coming into contact with the DNA of a specific species of lion already then present in Timbavati.  The resultant white lions are thus a product of human lions and genetically engineered Sirian lions. . . not "Sun Lords", ie lion-human forms, but a true "lion", yet with a bridging crystalline sequence in the DNA that will in the future allow this species to open a path for reunion with the "Pashat" strain or tribe to come once again into our midst. What purpose would this serve?  The Lion Ones are savants of our future worlds who hold a key to our own evolution. Perhaps not as intimately as do the cetaceans (who are actually a branch of our past-future species), but nevertheless the Lion Ones are among us now. . . incarnating as humans and guiding us at key moments in time. In their true forms, they sing to us the song of our future potential  as solar beings beyond our current star-sun.
In the Numis O'm (current evolving level of our futureNew Earth Star) the Lion Ones are present. Their part is to generate energy and maintain stability of the matrix and many grids within it of the evolving world field.
In communion with the Lion-Headed Sun Lord, Idoris, I received the following transmission. Note that all names given are for our benefit, as the communication of the Lion Ones is largely telepathic, keying off of specific guttural (yet strangely melodious) sounds.
Idoris:Our history was born from the flame of Kham, a world in the 5th Universe, according to our matrix. It was on Kham that the leonine forms developed and merged with the human-like beings that were then present there. This merging was part of a greater plan to unite two golden strains of life that had long ago shared one crucible...as it is on your world between the cetaceans and earth humans.
From Khan, we migrated into the realms of Sirius, to the planet Isuma. Not all of our race, which we will call here Ichatua, are "Sun Lords" this title is more appropriate for those of us who guardian and maintain the capstone over theEye of Ra-- theTelos.Aarkhara. As Sun Lords we are reconcilers of the solar emanations as they penetrate planets within our matrix, such as your earth.
If you touch our matrix we may come to you in vision or Dreamtime and feed you from the flame we guardian in the sacred capstone, for we are the Dwellers on the Threshold of your cosmic being.
Maia:How may we touch your matrix?
Idoris:By connecting to the pure flame of the SOL'RA - the solar center of being, the Golden-White Sun.  As you so intend and visualize this center it shall be made known to you.
Maia:Idoris is referring here to the Golden-White Sun of the 144,000 star-suns. As I write in Volume 02, 1996 (TD-9602) of Temple Doors, in the article "Through the Mouth of the Lion":
"...the Golden-White Sun is the embodiment of totality which is defined in the complete harmony of the 144,000 star-suns composing what Thoth calls the 'Divine Body' or Yesuarta Kominghi. This Divine Body contains light codes for the complete template of the Hue-mon Being, the Adam Kadmon. Thoth has spoken of the 'Foundation Stars' previously, which he defines as: 'Those incorporations of Living Lights which were received in divine consecration in the beginning of creation as a foundation stone for the universal temple as it is revealed to the worlds of being within the divine eschaton.'
Yet even the Foundation Stars, so Thoth tells me, are within the Yesuarata Kominghi, which is a greater body, including all components of the Heaven Temple."
Idoris:Our plight, our purpose as Sun Lords is to reflect the Yesuarata Kominghi. The Divine Body is in the understanding of your planetary identification, the "Body of Christ", for it radiates the Pure Flame of the Christic Consciousness through the universe and beyond.
Maia:Why do you choose the leonine partial form to merge with the human body?
Idoris:The leonine form is reflected in your natural world from a larger template of creation. . . that from which we as a race, arise.
Maia:Tell us more about the "star lions" of  Timbavati. Do you, as Sun Lords, work through them in some way on earth?
Idoris:They are part of our Presence. Yet they are animals. . . creatures of the earth, as well. As they hold our  Presence, so we radiate through them a vibration into the planet.
Maia:As I understand it, the star lions were entirely eradicated through hunting from the wild of South Africa. Only now are plans underway to re-introduce them to the wild of the natural homeland in Timbavati. How important it is that this re-introduction take place?
Idoris:It will happen as intended. Just as it was necessary for the star lions to go into the world on humankind, so it is now intended that they return to their seeding ground.
Maia:The archetype Sekhmet, as a Mother-energy being of universal proportions holds the flame of the Lion Ones, for She offers us a portal into their realm, which is really an aspect of our own being. Understand that every creature on this earth is an aspect of our life expression on earth, or it would not be present here with us. It is interesting that Sekhmet was called "The Eye of Ra" by the ancient Egyptians. Her name means "she who is powerful". I have been shown that she is represented in the Black Madonna, as one who waits to be known in the Heart of the Lion.
It was revealed to me in the Akasha that Mu (Lemuria), the Motherland of humankind on earth, the divine feminine was  depicted as "Mu-Lha", The love-light breath of creation. She was seen in several different forms -- each one intended to represent an aspect of her nature. One of these forms was a lion-headed woman, carrying a golden and white sphere in one hand intended to represent the Golden-White Sun or  later to be called the "Eye of Ra". In the other hand she held a dijti, which was an object that looked like a small whip with three strands attached to it. These were the three waves or universal streams that compose our working universal system. As "Tushbah" the Lion One, so Mu-Lha became a builder of world matrices, much like the Sun Lords of Sirius. Tushbah was black in color, with large golden eyes. her blackness was the void before creation and also that which is hidden until LIGHT is brought from the Golden-White Sun of what we would call "Christ Consciousness" to illuminate the All.
Sun Lord Shieldby Maia NartoomidARSY-0016STD
Idoris:I give this symbolic mandala as a contact point for accessing our matrix (see Sun Lord Shield above). Move into the center of the mandala and then out again...back and forth until the Golden-White Sun is visible in your brow (third eye). It is then that you may experience with us that which we offer the human element of earth: insight into the future design that is in actuality, already within you.

The Lunar Gateby Maia NartoomidAP-0015STD
The Moon's GatebyMaia Christianne Nartoomid

The monolithic Stonehenge in England is a matrix for earth energy that was originally a part of a network of structures linking the planet's energy fields together for instantaneous energy transfer from point to point. This energy could be in the form of thought, transportation of matter from one place to another, or materialization from ether into denser substance.
Stonehenge also served as a time portal, through which it's initiates could see and experience all time "pictures" from the past, present and future. Through the door of the Moon's Gate, as Stonehenge was once called, initiates could receive attunements to their purpose here on earth.
Through resonance with the human beings in it's midst, the stones of the Moon's Gate would ring and vibrate, binding the mortals present to the Music of the Spheres, and thereby opening divine channels for cosmic receipt from the angelic Living Lights (stars).
Relax and silently collect yourself. Ask in prayer that all tension be released from your body and mind, and that this occasion be blessed and guided.
Now slowly take a deep breath and exhale.
Begin to focus your attention in the center of your forehead (brow). Keep your third eye / brow chakra peaceful as you do this.
Picture a suffused, sky blue light. Allow your being to become part of this light.The circle of Stonehenge is materializing in your sight. Position yourself above it, so that you will see an aerial view of the structure. You are to visualize it as is was when first constructed. . . in whatever form this appears to you.
As did the initiates of old, all who read this and choose to participate will now take our place in front of the entry point of Moon's Gate - the Eternal Doorway.
See yourself entering into the stone circle and positioning yourself facing out from the center. You will have a stone sentinel on either side of your line of vision and a clear path out to the horizon in front of you.  This is your gate or passageway through time and space.
Feel the earth's current running down this passageway and beneath your feet. You are riding the back of the dragon. From this perspective, look down the passage you are standing on and observe how the rays of the sun fall on the stones to your right and left, and upon you, as a living stone poised at the threshold of Eternity. Like the ancient stone giants around you, so you have become the moon, reflecting the light of the Father Sun.
Take some moments to feel the communion of energies mingle in your being. . . the sun, the light, the space, the stone and you! The very air surrounding you is becoming charged with the vitality of all these life forces responding to and harmonizing with one another.
Be aware that through the ages master beings or Shining Ones have used the energy field of Stonehenge in this manner to enter and leave this dimension. Because Moon's Gate is one of the most sacred of earth temples, you are truly opening your heart to the light of Beauty and Wisdom when you sincerely and with pure spirit, enter this Gate, asking to receive from this blessed font.
You may humbly greet your earth initiator - the guide who is to be your instructor and councilor of the sacred earth initiations, knowledge and wisdom. Take time to see, feel and form a sense of kindredship with this being - male or female - who has come to assist you. Ask that this earth master reveal to you a symbol which you may visualize to summon them to your heart whenever you feel guided to do so. Study the symbol and either draw it or write a description of it, serving to further embed it in your consciousness.
When you feel complete, move upward, above Moon's Gate and back into the sky-blue light.  YOU MAY RETURN HERE WITH YOUR GUIDE AT ANY TIME.
After you have become familiar with this process by using it in its originally intended form as presented above, you can then start to use it to transport into Numis'OM by requesting attunement and adding entry to Numis'OM as your initial intentions. Allow Spirit to guide you and by all means let it unfold naturally.  I would love to hear about your experiences.

Window in the Sky - Rapa NuibyMaia Christianne Nartoomid

Note:parts of this article are excerpted from an original work entitled "Window in the Sky - Easter Island and Codelight 11:11" which was featured in Vol. 01, 1991 of Temple Doors.
The young woman sat in darkness, her body a crystal attached to a matrix of stone. In the womb of the cave she was alone, yet voices ascended hidden stairways in her mind, whispering truths from beyond the tide. Long forgotten stars, swirling in dream-like substance, entered the crown of her head, sending rarified nutrients of knowledge through her cellular being. She had come to the window in the sky, and now she would pass through it. She would become a vessel for the Zumir. Her generations would know her as a grail of the star.
In January of 1991 I began receiving information concerning a 'light coding' of women in the distant past, with a genetic knowledge of origin and gathering. I came to realize that this coding factor was bestowed upon them by a superior intelligence deep within a star system. The coding infusion came to earth through a convergence of 'invisible stars' -- realms of star consciousness which have yet to become visible within our spectrum of light. I was told by my inner-planes sources that this occurrence took place in very ancient times and at certain points upon the earth. The center point was Rapa Nui, what is commonly known as Easter Island in the Pacific Ocean. It was on this remote island that the command function was imprinted, signaling outward to it's primary stations, Uluru (Ayers Rock) in Australia and the Island of the Sun at Lake Titicaca, Peru. From this triangle, the codes are sent out to the minor stations around the planet.
Among the tribes seeded with the 'code', young girls of elect star genetics were selected to become what we might call Grails of the Sun. This meant that their DNA/RNA would be imprinted with a codelight of origin and gathering.  'Origin and gathering' meant that they would contain the memory seeds and guidance from the star beings - the Zumir, to keep the origin in focus through the tribes and in the DNA and would bring about gatherings among the tribes for the purpose of activating the codes at certain times for specific purposes. The were given from the Star Beings, certain songs which when sung, would trigger crystalline patterns in the brain, opening the energy bodies to the Homeward Light of true gnosis of the divine and the path back through the stars.
The Zumir are a branch of the Lion-Headed Ones of Sirius. They are more human-looking than some, but still have leonine features. The statues of Rapa Nui represent the Zumir. They may not appear at first glance very feline-featured, but the stone replicas reveal a 2nd generation of Zumir, who had integrated genetically with the priest caste of the original people of Rapa Nui.
The stone figures of Rapa Nui were created for the purpose of ourambalos. This is the infusion of stone with the properties of Presence.  'Presence' in this sense is the essence of life (not life itself) being imparted into an inanimate object, either to animate it in a limited way or for other 'magical' work. The stone giants of Rapa Nui were endowed by the Zumir with animation and the ability to radiate transformation, healing, projection and protection.
Within the caverns of the island was the huris, the transmitting crystal that grounded and re-calibrated the codelight. In the book,Mysteries of Easter Island, by Francis Maziere, he writes about having been allowed inside one of the sacred caves of the Lost Race - the Long Ears (aka the 2nd generation Zumir or Toltak). He speaks of the outer things of the world being but a manifestation of spirit with certain things being specifically charged with power.
Maziere explains that the natives told him the sacred objects in the cave were not made by their ancestors -- that is, the Polynesians. Many of these objects reflect an anthropomorphic view. . . bird-men, lizard-men, whale-men, etc. Perhaps lion-men as well? Maziere speculates that extraterrestrial contact having charged the island could not be
One of the most interesting revelations inMysteries of Easter Islandis the circular "watch" created by the monoliths as they scan the horizion. Maziere has in his book a circular diagram of how the statues are positioned to look out from the island with a combined 360 degree view. When he asked the natives if perhaps, like Stonehenge, the positioning of the statues formed some kind of star chart, they responded with an emphatic 'no'. They told him that the Rano-Raraku moai (giant statues):
"look at a part of the world over which he has power and for which he is answerable; that is why this land was called the Navel of the World."
It was futher explained to Maziere that the moai looking toward the south are different from the rest. They are workers of the Arctic winds, sending their powers to a large red rock that demarks the lower end of the triangle of thePacific Isles.
It is of interest that on the geomantic globe of earth created by EarthStar and distributed by Conservative Technology, the earth is displayed as a crystal of 30 equal-sided diamonds. The grid-lines of telluric power that compose the edges of these diamonds come together from nine directions, converging either aproximately or exactly on Rapa Nui (difficult to tell from the small EarthStar globe in my possession). This nine-pointed star eerily resembles Maziere's diagram of the directions the Watchers face as they look out to sea.
Also, could it be that the"huge red volcanic rock"to which the giants of the south transmit is Uluru in Australia?
At some point in time the power of Rapa Nui was abused and the Zumir withdrew the sacred powers from the island. Yet it is not entirely gone. . . some of it still sleeps within. There will come a time when the code is re-awakened at the Navel of the World and the New Earth Hologram will spill forth through Grail Star maidens and into the vessels of the Kindred, bidding all the tribes of humanity to gather once again as human crop circles in the starry fields of earth.
rapa nui - navel of the world

Cindy writes of the photo above entitled"a view to the sea":
A view of the cliff the young men would jump off of to swim to the island Motu Nui which you can't see in the picture as it was raining that day. . . it is past the small island you do see. . . . At this time we now have 12 tribes, little resources, and once a year the tribes would meet on this ceremonial ground where one man from each tribe would jump off the cliff, swim to Motu Nui, retrieve the egg of the Manutara bird, swim back and climb the cliffs. Star Lion Shieldby Maia Christianne NartoomidARSY-0022STD
This is the continuation of the topic of the Star Lions which I began in Volume 01, 2006 Numis'OM. I would suggest that you readThe Star Lions of Numis'OMbefore proceeding with reading the following article if you haven't already done so.
Walking With the Star Lions~ 
    a Shamanic Journey ~byMaia Christianne Nartoomid


fromMystery of the White Lions, Children of the Sun Godby Linda Tucker:
Because we are Stars, we must walk the sky. . .
- a traditional song of  Bushmen Lion Shamanism

In her masterful book,Mystery of the White Lions, Children of the Sun God, Linda Tucker relates the incredible story of the white lions of Timbavati, in South Africa. As I wrote in my first article on this subject:
In the Timbavati region of South Africa sometime over 400 years ago, during the reign of Queen 	Numbi, there was seen a streaking light in the heavens, falling to earth. Not longer after this, the 	golden lions of Timbavati began giving birth to pure white offspring. The African Elders call these 	white lions “Tsimba-vaati”, which in the ancient Shangaan language means “the place where star 	lions came down from the heavens”. They also refer to them as the "Children of the Sun God."
The lion priest Mutwa revealed to Linda Tucker the meaning of the name Timbavati - "the place of coming down." He then proceeded to tell Linda the story, which the bushmen of Timbavati consider to be authentic history, of Queen Numbi's encounter with the star object and the Shining One. Numbi, a Rain Queen of her people, was prostrate from illness in her hut one night, when a blazing object streaked across the sky and came to earth only miles from her village. She instructed her women to help her to walk, and slowly the traversed the distance to where the object sat upon the earth. It was  spherical light,"sitting like a newborn sun upon the ground."From it emitted a humming synchronicity.
After awhile, a "God" emerged from the bluish light. He was like the shining light, so she could not see his facial features, seeing only the outline of his body.  The being raised his hand in salutation to her, and she approached him, leaving her servant women cowering behind her. She was taken into the light with the being. The spherical "star" then rose into the sky and accelerated into the heavens. It is said that at a later time, Queen Numbi did return to her people, with great wisdom to share.
Many years after the star object had landed, in this very region of Africa white animals began to be born. These were not albinos, but true genetically white creatures - among them antelope, impala and eland. Some of these with only one horn instead of two, and with blue eyes. There were some white elephants, baboons and leopards as well and. . . the white lions, many with blue eyes! While the other "White Ones" eventually disappeared, the White Lions continued to be born.  More recently, it has been discovered that the Timbavati is especially high in radioactivity. It is postulated by Linda Tucker and others that the "star sphere" having landed there may have emitted a strong radioactive field.
When I wrote my first article on the Star Lions, I had not yet read Linda Tucker's book, having only seen her website at the time. I had very much wanted a copy, however, and then a friend let me know that she had a copy of this book (not knowing I even knew about it), and offered to  let me borrow it! An intended synchronicity, no doubt.
I have written on the Sun Lords of  the Telos.Aarkhara  as beings with the body of a human and the head of a lion. The lion shaman told Linda Tucker that their "highest gods" possessed the head of a lion and the body of a human being. As Linda points out in her book, the Sphinx has the head of a man and the body of a lion. I find this significant, as the Companions of Horus whom I know of as theNefer'Ratemare the Guardians of the Sphinx and the grid it anchors in the earth. From my akashic perspective, the sphinx holds one "charge" of a field of light, which is anchored at the other end in the Timbavati. Linda Tucker suggests something similar inThe Mystery of the White Lions.
The lion priest Mutwa spoke to Linda Tucker about the Abangafi Bapakade - the Shining Ones, who are brilliant leonine ones helping to bring love, light and truth to the humans of our earth.
These, I believe, are what Thoth calls the "Sirian Sun Lords" - the Lion-Headed Ones of the Telos.Aarkhara. Mutwa's own guide and guardian is a being whom I believe is probably an aspect of Sekhmet. Mutwa describes her to Linda as one of the eternal ones working with the evolution of this planet.
The white lions are understood by the indigenous people of the Timbavati as custodians and messengers of the Shining Ones. These white creatures are indeed shining ones themselves, for they are over lighted and animated by the "Gods" of the stars. Although a relatively new (some 400 years ago) presence in the Timbavati, the white lions are referred to by the lion priest Mutwa as being very ancient beings that are as"old as life itself."
Not far from Timbavati are the ruins of the ancient city ofGreat Zimbabwe. In her book, Linda Tucker writes about the connection between the Star Lions and the master builder of Zimbabwe. She entitles this chapter "Great Zimbabwe: Resting Place of the Lion."  The lion shaman Mutwa revealed to Linda that thedesign of the Great Zimbabwe complexwas an astronomically correlated to the Sirian star system. This certainly aligns with Thoth's revelations to me on the Sirian Sun Lords.
In conclusion to Linda Tucker's chapter on the Resting Place of the Lion, she writes that both Timbavati and Zimbabwe were laid out on precisely the same degree of longitude. . . the same longitude as the Great Sphinx of Giza at 31'14' east.
I was especially interested in the chapter in Linda's book entitled "Lion Priests and Eagle Shamans."  To the Bushmen, the eagle is venerated alongside the lion. The Zulu would never kill an eagle or a lion, believing them both to be divine creatures of the heavens. Thoth has opened the akashic scroll for me in the past about the "Stareagles" race, whom he also calls the "Shepherds". These are a branch of the "Solarians" of the Sun Bow Klan.
Here we have a lot of titles that could be confusing and it is not the purpose of this particular article to delve into separating it all out. For the sake of what I am pursuing here, I will simply say that the "Stareagles" are a star race who were the primary Seeders of this planet. They worked in tandem with the Sirian Sun Lords in anchoring the temples of LIGHT (the grids of divine assemblage) on earth, and genetically opening pathways to strengthen and re-generate a "lost" code of humanity, easing it back toward it's true nature. When I use the word "lost" here, it is only meant to infer a stage of an intended process of divine experience for souls, for nothing is truly lost or fallen or forgotten. As an aside, many years ago I was given by Thoth the totemic name of "Star Eagle."
Mutwa told Linda Tucker that he was descended from a "select priesthood" that had its origins with beings of a divine nature named Wandau [lion] and Ntswana [eagle or hawk].
Mutwa referred to these beings as being"imbued with stellar powers."
Mutwa spoke of the four steps of initiation for the lion shaman, the fourth stage being the evolution into the lion-eagle/hawk-man-serpent identity, the "Guardian of Sacred Knowledge" known mythologically as the 'gryphon'. To the indigenous Africans it is the Npenvu - the Beast of Truth.
Thoth refers to the gryphon as a "morphic creature." Such a being, so he tells me, is created through eons of souls in this dimension or higher realms, focusing certain specific lines of creation energy into a cauldron of etheric malleability. . . a "soup" of new form and dimension. From this amalgam of energies emerges the morphic creatures, their purpose being to bring together specific force fields of creative power and strength as a means to transform, enlighten and sustain the cosmic SEED of generation in the worlds of the universes of LIGHT. The gryphon/Npenvu Thoth refers to by it's even more ancient aloii name of Amsk'Adii. The Lemurians communed with these beings in their temples and some priests even rode upon their back in states of what the Eastern traditions call 'samadhi.'
On page 242 ofMystery of the Star LionsLinda Tucker writes about the "Vitruvian Man" as drawn by DaVinci. She states that this image may have been originally connected to the concept of star gods. I find this interesting, as Thoth guided me to use the Vitruvian Man in the medallion I created from my article on theNefer'Ratem.
The wanton "canned" hunting of the White Lions of Timbavati had eliminated them from the wild until recently. Thanks to Linda Tucker and her colleagues, they are now being re-introduced into protected areas.
Linda Tucker summarizes my own akashic perceptions when she writes inMystery of the White Lionsthat the white lions are truly radiant beings of light incarnated in lion form that embody the solar logos.
The "light fields" of Numis’OM are what Thoth calls the etheric webbing holding together the moving streams of ether into which the New Earth Star, and thus Numis'OM is building, creating, shifting and constantly renewing it's dimension and substance. In the electro-magnetic realm of our current earth, the "webbing" is much denser and more magnetic. This creates a certain stability in what "is" and what "isn't". For instance, if you set an apple down on the table, you can be reasonably certain that when you return to it five minutes later, it will still be an apple and not an orange!
In such realms as Numis'Om and our own "inner earth", apples may shift to oranges quite easily, just as an ocean current will take away a palm frond from the beach and replace it with a shell. However, beings who dwell in these realms are equipped with certain crystalline packets in the brain and DNA which allow them to access these changes and move with them in a way that is coherent and productive. This will be a whole topic for an article in the future, but enough said for now, just impart an idea about the light fields of Numis'OM.
As the light fields dance. . . expanding, contracting and re-locating, so they create splendorous auroras in the skies of Numis'OM. Beneath these heavenly light shows are sweeping plains surrounded by high mountains. This "reality" is a first level being generated by the light fields. A second or third level would look quite differently. You do not get from the first to the second level by moving through space-time from one point to another. You shift the crystalline patterns in your body. . . and there you are!
The first level of the light fields is the region that is guardianed by the White Lions. It is the entry point of Numis'OM. The White Star Lions in the ascended state (of Numis'OM) are truly "Shining Ones" - their whiteness beyond the brilliance we know on earth. Then, all the colors and contrasts of Light in Numis'OM are exceedingly luminous and vivid.
I am especially moved to learn from Idoris, the Lion - Headed Sun Lord, that the White Lions who are being massacred for profit in Timbavati are assuming ascended states in Numis'OM as a distinct tribe of Light Beings, working to assist the natural realm of earth in it's re-genesis. This special "tribe" Idoris calls "Kimbaza." Among the Kimbaza are those Lion-Ones who incarnated as golden lions carrying the white gene, being also true "Star Lions" under the flesh.
The Kimbaza Star Lions hold like a flaming wand, the light of COMPASSION for humanity. . . they who were killed by humans for profit. . . indeed, bred and raised to be released into regions specifically to be killed by the highest bidder. Thoth further enlightened me that this is their CHRISTIC MISSION. . . not only to forgive, but to ENLIGHTEN those souls who partake in such unconscious murder. Just how do the Kimbaza enlighten them? Thoth replied to me that this comes through the dreamstate and through presenting these individuals with life scenarios, while perhaps not pleasant, will nevertheless be instructive! Star Lion Priestessby Maia Christianne NartoomidAB-0032STD
In Numis'OM there is a Temple of the Lion in which priests and priestesses who maintained such a temple structure in Lemuria and later Egypt, continue this connection to Spirit through the High Deva of the Lion Being.
Their ceremonies and rituals are very much attuned to the rhythms and cycles of the Rigel Sun-Star (the sun of the New Earth / Numis'OM), as the Lion IS the natural embodiment of the Solar Logos. The indigenous African name for  the Star Lions is "Tsau", which means "Star Beast". Thoth tells me that this word is actually ancient Aloii (Lemurian) in origin, and was used to mean both "lion" and "star". In her book, Mystery of the Star Lions, Linda Tucker tells of a Bushman mother holding her newborn up to the heavens and saying "Tsau, Tsau", asking the stars to bless her baby with the heart of a lion.
Linda Tucker writes that the Lion Priest Mutwa told her that one of the stars in the Belt of Orion was called by his people the "Lion Star". The constellation of Leo was called the "Exiled Lion." Thoth relates that the star Denebula in the constellation of Leo is a portal star to the Golden Star of Mazuriel in the attasic (greater, non-dualistic) universe. Mazuriel is the ultimate "Christ Star", as it radiates the uniting force of this entire universe, drawing it BACK toward and eventually into, the "Higher Heaven" of the attasic.
The Temple of the Lion on Numis'OM holds the star grids in it's light field for the various stars and grouping of stars in the universe which contain the radiating frequencies of the Divine Logos. This "Divine Logos" is contained with the Solar Logos, thus all these stars that are "Lion Stars" are one and the same as being "Christ Stars".
While the Star Lions hold the vibration of the Christic Solar Logos, the unicorns vibrate at the capstone of the Christ Star summit. The LION is the FOUNDATION and the UNICORN is the CAPSTONE. Together they form a powerful union of Christic Spirit for the new light ascension hologram now being evolved on earth -- that which Thoth calls the "New Earth Star Hologram." As Linda Tucker mentions in her book, thelion and the unicornare often seen together the medieval tapestries and heraldry.
Place yourself in a relaxed, meditative state and ask to be escorted through a visionary journey with the Star Lions into Numis'OM.  You may conduct this journey any way you choose, but below I offer some guidelines.
Focusing through your third eye, imagine a beautiful, diamond-shaped clear crystal. It is set in the midst of a pale lavender sky.
The diamond begins a pulsing blue-to-violet flash, the cycle of the pulses starting slowly and then gradually increasing in frequency until the moment in between flashes are so brief, the flashing seems more like a brilliant flickering.
Now concentrate just on the flash /flicker itself, tuning out everything else. Feel yourself MOVE INSIDE THE LIGHT AND INTO THE CENTER OF THE DIAMOND CRYSTAL.
The blue and violet light becomes golden, then pure WHITE RADIANCE!
As the whiteness seems to dissipate you now see that you are in a field of tall grasses and exquisite flowers, with hazy, blue green mountains in the distance. The sky is a deep lapis. You notice tiny pin-points of light amidst pink and golden clouds. The air smells so clean and pure and tinged with the perfume of the flowers around you.
As you gaze about, suddenly you see two "flowers" become two blue eyes, framed by the massive bushy head of a white male lion. Instead of fear, you feel a strong sense of kinship. His strong stare softens a bit. He raises his head into the breeze and you see his mate beside him stir and rise, standing shoulder-deep in the grass. She is Sekhmet personified. Her eyes a deeper blue than the male, she seems to arrest time and space with her intense focus upon you.  Caught in the snare of that suspended moment, you notice that the male is now standing as well.
He takes the first tentative step toward you. He is not fearful, but merely respectful of your sensitivity and need to adjust to his presence.
He awaits your encouragement, and then his eyes brighten as he walks with a sure and regal step toward you, stopping within a foot from your reach. The lioness follows suit, only she comes right up to you and rubs her large and majestic head against your chest, circles you once and then lies down at your feet.
Spend some time with these beings. I know them as White Flame (male) and Moon Star (female).
After your heart-speaking with these two incredible Star Lions, ask them to take you deeper into Numis'OM, beginning with the Temple of the Lion. There you will meet priestess Tii'La'Kai and explore your own lion-being.

Aura Healing Garden ~ Inner Earthby Maia Christianne NartoomidOR-0006STD
Divine Grace, Avalon, Numis'OM,and Para PrakritibySimeon Nartoomid

In the western mystery traditions the earth's higher dimensional and/or parallel state of reality is often referred to as Avalon.  There have been many descriptions put forth as to what Avalon truly is. Many of them are embedded within very symbological and mythological interpretations.
I have been recently brought into an expanded awareness of how Avalon relates to Numis'OM, the New Earth Star [NES], and wisdom that issues forth from the Hindu scriptures.  In his book, "The Second Coming of Christ," Paramahansa Yogananda relates that in the Baghavad Gita there are three levels or domains of nature defined. There isapara prakriti, a state of impure or unbalanced nature which is the nature we know here on earth.  Then there ispara prakriti, a state of pure or balanced nature and which is what the realm of Avalon resides within.  Finally there ismaha prakritior super nature.  Maha prakriti is where what we term the New Earth Star [NES] resides. What is termed "miracles" can emanate from either para prakriti or maha prakriti and inter-penetrate apara prakriti.
Much of what my partner, friend, and wife Maia has written about through the years has been concerned with reality systems that reside within para prakriti, or pure nature.  The inner earth realities she relates in some of her writings wherein the lion and the lamb lie peacefully together so to speak, are relating the state of beingness which exists within pure nature or para prakriti.  In her writings about the New Earth Star [NES] she touches into the qualities and attributes of maha prakriti as well.
Numis'OM is a stepping stone to, and a portal of access for, the NES ascended earth reality. Ultimately the NES lies within the harmonic zone of maha prakriti.  The NES will reveal itself as a gradual unfoldment within the awareness of the souls embracing its potential.  Herein lies the purpose of Numis'OM, which is the Metatronic or full-light spectrum causal double of the earth, and is hosted within the causal body of the planet Venus [readNumis'OM and the Venus Gatefor further info].
Therefore Numis'OM spans the frequency spectrum between para prakriti [pure nature] and maha prakriti [super nature].  Numis'OM was created through an invocation of the Law of Divine Grace by the Illumined Master Intelligences that are here to guide the earth's humanity through the Great Transition we are now navigating.  Through Numis'OM we are given the opportunity to receive a measure of Divine Grace in our efforts to align ourselves to the New Earth Star within maha prakriti, or super nature.
Stations of Light such as Spirit Heart Sanctuary are also created under the Law of Divine Grace as a bridge between apara prakriti [impure or imbalanced nature] and para prakrtiti [pure or balanced nature].  Because such Stations of Light must have contact with the limited and unbalanced states of nature, human beings who are also part of that realm must create them.  This activity must be commissioned and overseen by the Illumined Ones to be effective.  This has been our objective, and in fact it was these Illumined Beings which originally founded this Station of Light through my partner Maia, which I then later helped her develop to what it is today.  As I have often said in the past, all of the good that has come about through this Station of Light has happened in spite of our limitations, not because of our greatness.  It is the greatness of God-Spirit-Source and the Illumined Ones who have continued to be able to offset our own personal limitations in ways which often surprise us.
This speaks to a very important spiritual principle: that we, as a limited humanconsciousawareness, can in fact join our efforts with beings of much greater Illumination and awareness than our own to create something that is not limited by our own personal limitations in the same way that other creations of our own would otherwise be.
This leads me to commenting briefly on the concept of self-mastery.  Herein I am defining self-mastery as our conscious personal efforts and achievements to transcend self.  Many of us have been accustomed to thinking in terms of self-mastery as a path to transcendence.  This is well and good and is serving a Divine Purpose in that it has helped us to experience a sense of our spiritual power expressing in the world of form.  It has also helped us to break free from some of the denser aspects of human existence on earth. Yet, self-mastery can in time become yet another prison we must eventually liberate ourselves from.  I have been made aware that we are now collectively entering a time where this will be become increasingly more obvious as the carefully woven fabric of our hard earned self-mastery begins to break down.  I have been experiencing this for quite some time as of this writing.
I will also clarify here that I am not knocking anything or anyone who provides assistance in the effort towards self-mastery or who is on that path, in a sense we all still are. Self-mastery is a very necessary step. It is also important to get a sense of what lies beyond our current efforts. We are additionally multi-dimensional beings so there may be parts of our being working in multiple dynamics simultaneously at any given moment in linear time.
This evolutionary consciousness movement I am speaking to herein ultimately embodies a transition from self-mastery to self-realization.  All parts of our being will pass through this acceleration before we will realize the pleroma, or fullness of the God-Self within our human experience. In the domain of self-mastery we learn to gain control over the more limited aspects of ourselves and to deal with the shadow self to bring it evermore into accord with our expanded self.  In the domain of self-realization we come to know the God within -- the God-Self, Atma, Magna-Soul, Monad, I AM Presence.  The culmination of the self-realization movement in consciousness is a state wherein we are so completely anchored within the domain of the God-Self that we never leave that state of being regardless of what occurs externally in the circumstantial world around us.
The necessity and activity of self-mastery resides primarily within the domain of apara prakriti [impure or imbalanced nature]. Self-realization takes us fully into para prakriti [pure or balanced nature] and sets us like an arrow upon God's Golden Bow with the string drawn back waiting to shoot its arrow into maha prakriti.  The tension building on the bowstring is tangible and can be felt by anyone who is sensitive to subtle energies.
While it is possible for a being to reach this point and initiate the release of their arrow from the Golden Bow on their own, I have been made aware that the Master Program of Light most of us are currently working in with the Illumined Ones is meant to elicit this as a collective movement rather than an individual one.  There are exceptions, but they are few and far between according to my sources.
So God's Golden Bow will eventually release a shower comprised of multitudes of illumined Light-Arrows sending the leading edge of the collective consciousness of earth into the NES within maha prakriti.  Each time anyone one of us moves our awareness and consciousness into a greater harmonic attunement with super nature, the NES draws closer as a realized potential for ALL of humanity.  There will need to be a critical mass of beings strung in God's Golden Bow waiting to be shot into maha prakriti and the NES before that can happen.
The concept of the 144,000 comes into play here as it does in some other dynamics. The Illumined Ones I commune with have indicated that this is primarily a symbolic number and that it actually represents a specific measure of light quantum and not the actual number of beings/arrows ready to be shot from God's Golden Bow.  This "measure" is not something that we can currently accomplish with existing scientific instruments.  Master Intelligences register this "measurement" upon the plane of theiratoma. They are able to sense the very fine gradations of resonance between the baseline phi energies within the planetary field and those within the Great Central Sun -- the Heart-Mind of God-Spirit-Source. They are able to sense these refined resonances because of their own ultra-clarity. In this manner they become the sensing instrument and its operator all rolled into one.
We can also learn to start to sense this light quantum in many ways as well. An excellent practice along these lines is to learn to view the circumstances of our lives and world news and events from a higher perspective.  It is important to learn to perceive these circumstances and events from the perspective that they all serve a Divine Purpose in the end. If such purpose does not reveal itself to you affirm it as an article of faith and you will soon start to catch glimmers of portions of that purpose. Once you do, then align yourself with that larger sense of purpose.  Also keep in mind that with our limited human awareness we will not be able to apprehend nor understand the entirety of the Divine Purpose and Plan behind all difficult circumstances and events. We can, however, get a good sense of that greater purpose and as we progress we become increasingly able to see an ever-increasing scope to it all.
Another way to get a sense of this expanding light quantum is of course through prayer and meditation, asking to be brought into a higher awareness of this light quantum.  Ask Spirit to bring it to you in a way that makes sense to you.  Start to look for signs of this light quantum everywhere you go and in everything you witness.  Doing so will shift your reality towards the light quantum you seek to perceive and thus will build upon it in the process. As you grow in your capacity to perceive the light quantum you will fan its Divine Flame into a full-blown torch of liberation for all.
If you feel attuned to Avalon as many people familiar with the Western Mysteries do, you can use this to your advantage and strengthen your conscious connection between Avalon and Numis'OM within your mind and inner experience.  This will help you to take advantage of what you already have going in your favor. Just consciously realizing that they both exist within the realm of para prakriti opens the door to much deeper and more expansive inner revelations!
As Thoth related to us many years ago, the planetary ascension "through" the portal membrane of Numis'OM and into the NES will be dependent upon what he termed the "Heart Ascension."  When asked how we would know if we had completed the Heart Ascension Thoth explained that once this had occurred the individual would no longer have any desire to be anyplace other than where they are in the moment because the ascended reality would reside within them fully enough that the external circumstances of the world would no longer adversely affect the individual's inner experience.  This would in turn enable the individual to serve in a far more expanded scope of endeavor here in the un-ascended earth.  This in turn accelerates the collective process of ascension for the collective soul of humanity.
So there is our yardstick.  We only need to look honestly where we are within this field of greater potential without judging ourselves for being where we are now, and strive to move more fully into it.  As I am writing, theIAC Merkabah of the Hostis gently saying to me that they and many other Illumined Beings are there for us and that this can NOT be fully accomplished through our own personal efforts alone.  Because we are working within a Program of Light that has collective unification as its primary directive at this time we must learn to work with the parts of the collective that are more advanced than we to achieve our goal.
This means that we must at some point be willing to release our need for self-accomplishment [self-mastery] and come to a greater realization that the forces we have to deal with are much larger than any of us individually and thus require a larger collective and Illumined effort to transform and transcend them. In other words there must be a Greater Power brought to bear upon these energies than any of us personally can muster or wield alone.
Many people get caught in the trap of trying to deal with the difficult planetary energies which their soul has brought into their space to be dealt with using the approach of personal self-mastery.  This will not work once an individual crosses a certain initiatic threshold wherein they are then opened up to being more of a planetary surrogate for the benefit of all.  Energy from the limited mass consciousness starts to pour into their energy bodies and often causes great difficulty, particularly at first.  Once the individual learns that they are now being opened up to experiencing a greater degree of the planetary dross so they can give it passage to into the Divine Light as a surrogate, they then will also naturally seek Divine Assistance in this endeavor because they will realize that what they are dealing with is much larger than they are.
As Thoth related to us years ago it is not our responsibility to transmute all the dross in our space. It IS our responsibility to reveal it -- become aware it is in our space and what its nature and character is -- and then to offer it up to the High Host and God-Spirit-Source to be transmuted. It is VERY important that we become proficient in accomplishing this.  It is an extremely effective tool, it is very fast, and its activity operates under the auspices of the Law of Divine Grace. We thus move ourselves more fully under the action of Divine Grace when we use this tool. We are then empowered to experience what I call "Quantum Transformation."  I will be writing more on this in the future.  I also teach people to become more proficient in its use in thesessionsI do.
Once we receive Divine Grace, in order to keep the envelope of that energy expanding within our experience, we also must be open and aware enough to allow ourselves to likewise become vessels of Divine Grace for others.  The opportunity to do so presents itself to us many, many times each day. Most of these opportunities are seemingly so insignificant that we may miss them.  But no act of becoming a vessel of Divine Grace for another being is insignificant.  The spiritual power and radiance that you build within your energy bodies and the planetary energy bodies is far greater than you may realize with even the smallest of such acts of love, kindness, caring and compassion that resonate with phi [Divine Love].
David Hawkins in his book "Power vs Force" describes how a couple of loving thoughts, feelings and actions at the end of a very negative day can offset all the negativity that transpired during the day.  Along this same line of thinking he then also relates that one person calibrating at the level of 700 on hisMap of Consciousness[I highly recommend this book and the map] can offset the negativity of 70 million individuals calibrating at less then 200. His chart on page 234 shows that even one individual calibrating at 300 will offset the negativity of 90,000 persons below 200.  The power of love is truly beyond what the human mind can imagine possible.  When we extend love and kindness to another being, especially when they may be mistreating us in some way, we invoke the Law of Love AND the Law of Divine Grace and negativity is transmuted for us, the other being, and the planet. THAT is quantum Light-Love work!
It is the aggregation of many such acts which ultimately place us into harmonic accord with Numis'OM and the NES.  The more often we can elicit this awareness and consciousness in our lives, open ourselves to Divine Grace, and also be a vehicle for it to transmit to others, the more easily and quickly we will find ourselves advancing towards completing the Heart Ascension process. This will in turn expand our experience towards living more completely within the states of reality known as Avalon, para prakriti and ultimately maha prakriti as we enter the New Earth Star as the leading edge of a collective exodus to broader Metatronic horizons.  This we are destinined to experience while we are still here in the current earth and we will become living examples for others to see what lies ahead.  THAT will initiate a major acceleration for all other beings on the planet as they suddenly realize what they are missing!
