Ascension Ankhby Maia Christianne NartoomidARSY-0021STD
The Ascension Ankh

You can be so filled with gratitude that God’s will is being done, regardless of conditions or appearances, that you, by this very devotion, can transform and completely glorify, any earthly circumstance or condition.
As you are thankful in all things, all things in your world that have not seemingly expressed total harmony can be immediately transmuted, transformed or translated into conditions of harmonious self-empowerment for ever and ever.
What a wonderful life of glorious synergy!
~ excerpted with permission fromThe Bible for Translating from Physical to Spirit, by Terry Livingood [highly recommended]
I received this Ascension Ankh as a vision I had while Simeon and I were praying for my health, and the health of ALL beings on this planet.
Later, I requested more information about it from Thoth. He revealed to me that the Ascension Ankh is a NEW PURE SYMBOL for the ascension of the energy bodies as they are integrated into the New Earth Star vibration of Numis'OM.
The Egyptian Ankh represents basically, life. However, it is intended to mean much more than that. In her book,Mystery of the White Lions - Children of the Sun God, author Linda Tucker states categorically that the ankh did not originate in Egypt. She believes it's origin to have come from sub-Saharan Africa where it was known as the"Knot of Life - the symbol of the one-legged sun god Mvelinqangi."
My akashic insights reveal that the ankh is in the shape of  a device brought to Mu (Lemuria) from Venus by the original Lord Melchezidek. When held and moved just above the body, it regenerated and re-aligned all the energy bodies. It is a symbol of Eternal Life, which encompasses the physica,l but is far more universal and dimensional in scope.The Ascension Ankh has it's loop open to reflect the movement outward and upward of the life waves of creation. The crescent is the womb releasing, giving birth to the egg, depicted here by a fire opal - a fire and water stone (star suns and life-giving fluidium). Over the fire opal is the Seed of Life Symbol, which is the first stage in creating the Flower of Life. The Seed of Life is that beginning strand of BEING that arises from the Azoth, or ether of "First Form," to create the pattern, the expression of life seen in the Flower of Life.
Both the Seed of Life and the Flower of Life were engraved by the ancient Egyptians on the walls of the Osiris Temple at Abydos. The Seed of Life symbol was drawn upon the body of initiates in the Temple of the Risen One (Great Pyramid), indicating their readiness in mind, body and heart-light for the ascension process.
Understand that in the Egypt of Thoth's day, "ascension" meant to walk the earth as an Illumined One - a Solar Lord,  liken unto  the Thoth, Raismes of Aphra. Such a being does not have to leave the planet or go to another dimension of it to be "ascended". The Master Yeshua (Jesus) embodied full ascension as he walked the slums and towns in the Holy Land.
The light green stone is meant to represent moldavite - the heavenly stone - and is placed at the heart of the universal body. It is the ascended heart being that must be present before any other aspect of self may ascend.
I believe that the Ascension Ankh was given to me to share with the Numis'OM subscribers as a symbol to meditate upon for integrating the energy bodies in preparation for ascension. We have therefore made it available forfreeto Numis'OM subscribers. You may place the Ascension Ankh on your desktop and send it to others if you wish. I request that if you send the Ascension Ankh to anyone, please include thislink.
The Ascension Ankh is also available through our Spirit Store as item#ARSY-0021STD.

Thoth and the IAC Merkabah of the Host  have requested that we facilitate a specific Program of Light related to the Aramu Temple of Thoth and Numis'OM to help those who feel resonant with this Station of Light (Spirit Heart Sanctuary) to accelerate their Ascension processes and thus to further help the collective soul of humanity approach the gateway of Ascension which Thoth callsLight-Principle Forty, or LP-40 for short. Ultimately, as we collectively move through this passage we will activate the44:44 Ascension Stargateand trigger a series of cosmic events destined to alter the DNA of humanity forever.
Numis'OM is a causal reference point for the New Earth Star and the 44:44 stargate, and is hosted within the causal body of Venus. TheAramu Temple of Thothis energetically within the Numis'OM matrix and acts as a way-station for souls building the New Earth Star consciousness from within the earthen experience. Souls can thus visit Numis'OM and even the New Earth Star if they have proper intent and attunement. It is our goal to provide pathways for this to occur within.
This publication thus sits at the heart of our efforts to facilitate this greater process for the Masters and Illumined Ones that we are working with and to assist souls on earth.   We hope that you will find it a fruitful and friendly path into the Homeward Light.

Children of the Divine Rayshipby Maia Christianne NartoomidARSY-0025STD
The New WorldbyMaia Christianne Nartoomid

Please note that the first four articles in this issue are all interconnected subsections of a larger body of information.
In my articleNumis 'OM, The Temple of Aramu and the Shamballah Gate inVolume 01, 2006of this periodical, it is stated that Numis'OM and indeed all of the New Earth Star as it forms, is much like any of the astral and higher spiritual worlds - more in the category of the higher spiritual - that one crosses to after having left this earthly level of existence. There are distinct differences though. I will highlight the main ones here:
1)Numis'OM contains specific master temples dedicated to integrating souls into building the "New Earth Star." Other astral and higher spiritual realms certainly have "temples" and integration processes, but those related to Numis'OM are specific to creating a NEW dimensional helix and not an extension of one already in existence. This is really a difficult thing to write or speak about, as saying that the New Earth Star is NOT already in existence is limiting it to a time line, which it is not. Perhaps more accurately, we might say that the New Earth Star is not yet a part of our "consensual reality" as souls, therefore "not in existence fully" for our soul evolution from the perspective of our current point of reference. A mouthful! So best not to dwell on it too much. We might simply just realize that we are definitely on a "New Frontier" with Numis'OM, as the New Earth Star is "becoming" out of it from the spinning of our consciousness as our being accelerates more rapidly into greater PRESENCE.
2)The BIG difference and definitely the most important, between Numis'OM / New Earth Star and other higher spiritual realms of what we call the "non-physical" of this planet can perhaps best be viewed in the following way:
World systems such as our current planet's are ones in which a soul is incarnate in a body, lives for awhile and then discards the body to go to a "non-physical" state of that world system. It will then at some point likely return into the same physical state of that world again - what we will call here the "base level" - to learn more, and help the mass consciousness progress through the individual soul's experience there. The soul will then leave that body behind, returning to a non-physical state of the planet. This can go on and on for the soul for some time. If not THAT soul, then other souls from the same world system.
However, at some point, the world system of that planet will be ready to absorb it's current base level.
Our base level is where we live, grow old or sick, or have accidents which maim or destroy our bodies. Then we must leave that body and state of existence to return to the spirit realm. . . and usually COME BACK AGAIN for more of the same, only with new or more advanced processing to do!
But what happens when the world system is ready to absorb it's base level? IF that base level is "physical" - meaning that it can be damaged or "destroyed" in it's physical form, when it is absorbed into the next stage, it will ascend it's matter. The molecules of  it's dense physical are translated into LIGHT particles and go WITH the souls then on the physical planet, into the next stage - the first level of non-physical available to it in the "daisy chain" of that world system. So this means that the daisy chain is intentionally BROKEN and that little "link" which was the "physical" is gone! Now the base level of that world system is non-physical. Not only that, but all the little astral pockets collecting around the physical disappear in a puff of smoke, as they were totally dependant on the base line physical world's lower akashic record to keep it supplied with "reality." A lot of souls in this world are and have been for centuries, crossing over from this "life" into the astral pockets where to some extent, they re-create rather small existences based on the limited thoughts, beliefs and desires they had while in physical embodiment in their last incarnation.
Numis'OM still accommodates the soul's need to see and experience individuality, and symbols and pictures of reality that allow it to open more fully to Spirit on the level they are then ready to receive. But it is not an "astral" world. It is a "higher spiritual" plane, so it is open-ended in drawing the soul ever-deeper into pure being a step at a time. One can live in a house, have conversations sitting under giant trees in beautiful gardens with friends. Unicorns, mermaids, "friendly" dragons - all energies waiting to manifest with love and wisdom to offer you are there. More and more you soul will be drawn DEEPER into the New Earth Star, building it as you go - creating less "things" and more pure light gnosis. This process is gentle - there is no rush. There is no time. It is all in accord, balance and beauty.
Numis'OM / New Earth Star is the starting point of a NEW WORLD SYSTEM.  Our  planet as we now know it is the very last pearl on a connecting strand. When it is absorbed into the one above it, this world system of which we are a part will become free from it's anchor in the "physical." Then it enters a whole new category of "world systems" - inside categories of universal systems (but we won't even go there in this article!).
To help us with the idea of world systems, Thoth has given us a scale-context to place it in.  The Lemurians called a world system a "NA" or a fluid (progressive) cell. There are 29 "NA" in one "ATA" - i.e. a knot or binding unit. To put things into perspective, we are currently at "NA 1." The New Earth Star will eventually take "us" through to the next ATA, where it will then become. . . something else. Again, let's not go there. We have enough on our plate just trying to wrap our minds around the next NA! We could also call this upcoming NA "World System II."
Numis'OM as it is "now" (in our now) is the first membrane or staging ground for the New Earth Star. It is what you might say, "betwixt and between" at the moment, as our physical earth is still attached to the strand. It will not become a true base line for a World System II until the physical base line is translated, i.e. ascended into the New Earth Star. But if we go beyond this "time" limitation we set for ourselves with linear consciousness, we can see Numis'OM as already the base line for a World System II! IF we do this - if we imagine this, we create it in OUR reality via what Thoth calls the "New Earth Hologram."
The potential for progressing this planet through it's current "bumpy ride" toward the finish gate for NA 1 is potent. IT IS REAL, and it is within our grasp. Semantics don't matter here. They are just fancy handles on doors that can be opened many ways. One does not have to read or believe in terms like "New Earth Star" or "Numis'OM" to "be there" in vibrational intention. There are other ways. . . there are always other ways. Spirit is never, ever limited. However, those of us who may feel aligned to and resonate with this terminology and way of seeing the picture can come together in vibration to create a strong focus toward bringing the "future" world system into the "current" one, via encoding it into the New Earth Hologram.

The Star "Eagles" and Hawks" are non-physical beings who choose the appearance of humans, or sometimes they appear as eagle or hawk-headed, but they are relations to our genetic vine.

When you leave the denser "body" behind you then find yourself in the next layer of your "onion-skin," which is far more subtle. Thus, DNA exists in the "subtle" or what we would call non-physical. It simply is more diverse on that level.
The Eagle and Hawk Star Beings are in very subtle states of particlulation. The particles that form their outer shell energy are very tiny and fast-moving. Ours, by comparison are large and slow-moving.
There is another aspect we need to address at this point about these beings. At a point in our distant past, some of them entered the physical birth into this planet. So many of "us" have this "cousin" DNA within us at a very subtle level. Thoth refers to these persons or rather "tribe" as the "Star Eagles" and "Star Hawks".

Our physical heart-organ would quantum into such a high frequency it's current physical exterior would explode. In fact, even in Numis'OM, AJANU is seen only by the Illumined Ones and Angelics.

The Nine Divine Rays of Numis'OM:

The "hawks" are especially in the thick of it, while the "eagles" are more effective in overview positions. For instance, one Star Hawk is Nelson Mandela, while Mother Teresa was a Star Eagle. The Star Hawks make the changes through difficult and exacting means yet usually with a high degree of grace, while the Star Eagles supply the healing and to some degree, enlightment concerning the interior plight - not the external battle.
Ghandi was a Star Hawk, while the current Dali Lama is a Star Eagle. Certainly both had their share of oppositional struggle and both radiated enlightenment, but Ghandi remained in the thick of it, while the Dali Lama was destined to be at the apex of the overview.
Since the main threshold of the Eagle and Hawk Star Beings is Rigel in Orion, we see then that what Thoth is calling the "Children of the Divine Rayship" have been since the beginning of earth, Blue Star Rigel souls.  Yet not all Rigelian souls are "Children of the Divine Rayship." At some point in their soul journey they can choose this position, but once chosen, they are in until the "finish" - meaning until World Ascension.
Yet now, in the 21st century, some souls from other star thresholds are being born among the Children of the Divine Rayship. They are not of the Star Eagle or Star Hawk tribes. They are nevertheless entering this ancient matrix of Ray re-balancing and weaving. The gate is widening for more star families to enter this task, for it is great and the "time" as we perceive it, is near at hand.

Grail Round Tableby Maia Christianne NartoomidMAN-0027STD
The Power of Pure BeingbySimeon Nartoomid

Have you ever contemplated the difference between human beingness and pure beingness? I have and it is a very interesting investigation to have engaged! In fact I still engage in this exploration regularly.
One reason I enjoy this so much is because subtle-planes observation, investigation, and study is very harmonic with who I AM and what I AM here to do. The other reason I do this is because it always seems to lead to a feeling of expansiveness and liberation from the confines of the limited vehicle in which I AM traveling while here on earth.
I have worked with quite a few people over the years that have difficulty with embracing the aspect of their being which resides in Pure Being. I have learned that what often times happens is once an individual gets in touch with that level of their being they then find their limited human self intolerable and that leads them into deeper engagements with self-judgement which in turn obstructs their path.
There also seems to be a programmed mechanism built into many of us human beings that makes us believe judgment of ourselves is somehow better than judging others. From a social standpoint that is largely true, you won't have many friends if you go around judging others all the time. From a higher perspective though it is energetically the same. You cannot judge your self without also judging others and vice versa. We are all part of One Being after all.
Pure Being is our most natural state of being. Humanity has largely come to believe that their mind is their subtle self, the part of them that they cannot experience with any of the five senses but only through their thoughts. This leads people to believe that their mind is all powerful. Yet leading edge science being conducted at places like theInstitute of HeartMathtells us that the heart as an organ in the body has an electromagnetic energy field that is 5,000 times greater than that of the brain in our head and an electrical energy field that is 40-60 times greater than that produced by our head brain. Hmmm.
Our physiology thus does not support the concept that the mind is all powerful. Given that I AM naturally resonant with many of the basic perspectives found in Maha Buddhism (many previous incarnations there) this posed a bit of paradox for me. The point I AM getting to here is that Pure Being is also not the mind. So how the heck are we going to connect with this place called Pure Being if we cannot sense it with the five senses and it cannot be located in the mind? The answer is through expanding our awareness.
Many people feel that awareness is also a function of the mind. There is some truth to this if we are considering the type of temporal awareness that we use to function in the dance of human life. This would be awareness of material objects and concepts related to skills we acquire or need and so forth. However, the type of awareness that I AM speaking of here is not that type of awareness. It is an awareness of being and comes from your total being. It is an awareness of the nature of love in its most rarified form BEFORE it takes motion and moves from being noun to verb. Its first motion? Acceptance of all things and beings and their right to exist.
I have had profound insights that this type of awareness is actually rooted in a memory of states of Pure Being which existed prior to what is being called the Big Bang. We all share in this memory, it is holographic and exists within every aspect of the Universe. It is that original state of awareness that preceded everything that currently exists in the Universe; both energy and matter, which are but different expressions of the same primal substance. Now this makes total sense to my mind as well because the Big Bang represents the first moment of differentiation. In a sense the Big Bang is really not over yet. We are still in it as things continue to differentiate; continually changing, dividing, subdividing and also mutating into entirely new forms that never existed before.
So by now you may be thinking that if this is where Pure Being lies it may be impossible to access for most people. Its not. In fact this makes it even easier. Space and time have no bearing on this level of reality. If an experience of the state of Pure Being was somehow to be granted by the complexity of the differentiated Universe then we would truly have a very difficult time locating this state of awareness within the labyrinthine mosaic of interwoven strands we generally experience as reality.
Contemplate this for a bit. To access this state of Pure Being does not even require consciousness! In fact consciousness can get in the way. The Big Bang preceded the development of consciousness, and thus that state of being cannot be accessed using consciousness either. Experiencing ourselves as pure consciousness is a great primer for the real show, but we have deluded ourselves into believing that everything is consciousness. Rather, everything is energy and that is very different indeed.
In terms of beingness relative to the temporal human experience there is sentient beingness, there is intellectual beingness, and there is consciousness beingness. Rudolph Steiner skirted upon this concept with his revolutionary revelations about the three levels of collective soul evolution that humanity is going to traverse in the earth Alpha through Omega. These were the Sentient Soul evolution, the Intellectual Soul evolution, and the Consciousness Soul evolution. We have recently entered into the latter.
So what is the difference between these three types of beingness? Sentience is awareness moving from a point outward, in other words awareness of the other. Intellectual awareness is but a transitory state of beingness that is meant to develop consciousness out of sentience. Consciousness states of beingness are what happens when a ray of awareness is bent back upon itself closing the circle so to speak. When this happens you then have a self-aware system and that is consciousness. It is the development of the intellectual capacities that allows us to become self-aware, to bend that ray of sentient awareness back upon itself.  The faculty of intellect has so many other intriguing capabilities that we have been merrily experimenting with the creative potential of those possibilities as we travel the road of soul experience through the realm of earth.
It is now time to recognize that we have become over-enamored with our intellectual faculty and to see what its true purpose in our design really is. We each need to understand how we best can bend that ray of our sentient awareness back upon itself. This will be different for each of us, but it is happening all the time. You do something in the world without awareness of what may really be going in you (i.e. unconsciously), then the flow of life gives you feedback about it so you can become more self-aware. Its not a punishment, really. It is the way the Universe works and this mechanism is born of Infinite Love calling everything home.
When I use the term love herein I AM not referring to the human version of it. I AM referring to a powerful energy, a monopole if you will, a TRUE UNIVERSAL POWER, that not only holds all of the Universe together, but which also draws all aspects of it back together towards their point of maximum unification post-differentiation. So, it really does boil down to what Joseph Campbell said years ago about following our bliss! When we follow that which we find the highest resonance with we are on auto-pilot heading into an experience of the state of Pure Being.
One problem often encountered is that we may think that following our bliss means avoiding everything that seems as though it might be difficult or challenging. Quite to the contrary, any bliss we might be able to experience with this strategy would quickly vanish because we are designed to be creatively engaged, which brings challenge and difficulty as part of the package. Rather, following your bliss truly means to listen to your guidance and to follow it IMPLICITLY. When you do, you will find that sense of exhilaration that living on the edge brings. Lets face it, living 100% according to our guidance is living on the edge - the edge of uncertainty. That is the ultimate bliss!
Fear of the uncertainty is what kills this process for many people. There is a pervading misunderstanding in the metaphysical, spiritual and holistic communities that guidance should be able to inform us of the details of the future in order to eliminate the uncertainty. How boring would that be!  The Universe just does not work like that. It is true that we are traveling in a vehicle of our own design and that the vehicle knows exactly where it is going and will take us there with Godspeed if we don't interfere with the vehicle or its driver and that guidance occassionally lets us have a peek at what's ahead. However, if we as backseat riders were to know all the details of the journey and destination then what would be the point of the journey?
The journey is about discovery. The journey is about learning to read the roadmap of limited experience as unlimited beings. The journey is about the development of consciousness from pure sentience. The journey is about remembering our nature in Pure Being while simultaneously being able to experience a more limited nature in the realms of manifestation, which includes the "Worlds of Pure Light."
The purpose for all of this? To expand the beauty, textures, colors and radiance of love in the Universal Heart. Every time we give expression to the Being of Love that we are, it makes an imprint upon the Universal Heart Crystal. Each imprint is unique, like a fingerprint or snowflake, no two are quite the same.  The journey through differentiation is what elicits the opportunities needed to give expression to the Beings of Love that we are. This occurs within an ever-changing environment ensuring that the beauty, textures, colors and radiance of love emanating from the Universal Heart Crystal will grow infinitely, forever, without end.
As for Pure Being, it is therefore not a place or a space. It is a memory and a state of awareness. It is within you, always there just waiting for a moment when the energies of your human being make an opening for that universal memory to transport you into an awareness beyond all the mundanity and differentiation of your life wherein you can see it all in a different context afterward.  We all experience these moments spontaneously every so often and cherish them deeply. What we seek is to be able to access Pure Being at will.  Many spiritual traditions have attempted to formulate systems to teach us how to do this. For me, none of these have worked to any great degree.
Instead, I have found over the years that simply accepting what I AM now as a human being, limitations and all, opens that gateway more profoundly than anything else.  I have come to realize that in order to unconditionally accept ourselves, we must access this part of our being, so there it is every time we do. In order to help me accept myself (and others) in the full glory of all our struggles and limitations I find that the power of the heart is the key.
I am going to share a simple exercise that is based on the tools developed and taught by theInstitute of HeartMath. It was scientifically developed. I can attest to its effectiveness from my own experience and that of many others I have taught it to. I can also say that its effectiveness in changing the Heart Rate Variability (HRV) waveform and the hormonal balance in the body has been proven in many laboratory settings. I also have a biofeedback device and software which allows me to see these changes in real time right on screen. Its undeniable both scientifically and experientially. Here are the simple basic steps.
1)Place your focus of attention on your heart chakra. You may find it easier at first to place your finger there to help you focus on that part of the body.
Keep in mind the objective is to focus your attention there which is different than thinking about it. If you can recall a time when you were in a park or at a lake or some other beautiful place in nature where you were looking at something where you had your attention on it, but you were not thinking about it, but rather just taking it in. This is focusing your attention on something without thinking about it.
2)Gently, slowly and rhythmically start breathing in and out through your heart chakra.
3)Be aware of any sensations you may feel in the heart chakra or elsewhere in the body as you do this. These will be your specific signals or keys that let you know you are starting to become more coherent and thus are expanding your state of awareness. Also, focusing on the sensations in the heart chakra can help to intensify the energy effect.
4)Continue this heart-breathing process until you feel a sense of peace coming over you.
You can keep going after this, the longer the better. But just reaching this state is powerful enough. It is from the place of inner peace that comes over you when you do this simple practice that you can more easily accept yourself and others. When you engage the activity of unconditional acceptance of self and other, also be aware of what you are feeling and experiencing inwardly. This practice can bring you rather easefully into a state of Pure Being if you are willing and able to surrender in that direction fully enough. This practice is wonderfully effective for dealing with the fear of uncertainty!
Some people have called this state of being I am calling Pure Being the Void.  It really does feel like that at first, so that is understandable. Yet, the more I visit this state of being the more I realize it is not a void at all. I do not really have any words to describe what is there that negates the idea of the Void other than to say it is the most rarified form of love one can ever experience. It's a pure power that is beyond human imagining and its available to all. In fact, it IS all! It is us and everything around us. Everything has its origin in this state of being and owes its existence to it. The Power of Pure Being is thus synonymous with the Power of Pure Love, they are one and the same.
To the degree that we align ourselves to the Power of Pure Love we are increasingly drawn into states of Pure Being thus amplifying that awareness within the collective consciousness of humanity.  When we focus on Numis'OM and the New Earth Star we would do well to remember these are realities which are way stations along the collective journey into Pure Being. The linear time cycles and meta sciences involved boggle the mind. However, when we realize that all of it is here now just waiting to be experienced by each of us individually prior to the larger collective events the heart lightens considerably! In fact, the heart gets downright effervescent and bubbly when we realize that to experience this ahead of the collective curve IS part of why we are even here! It is the Power of Pure Being and Love that are ultimately our road, our vehicle and our fuel. Have a blessed journey!
I AM currently offeringRadiant Heart Initiationsif you would like to invite me to be a qualified facilitator on your journey.

Thoth Raismes of Aphraby Maia Christianne NartoomidAB-0003STD
Heart-Speak from Thoth

Atu Tehuti, Ati Hatu	--"in the rising of the breath I greet you, in the release of the breath I embrace you"
Giselle:The esoteric society known as the Rosicrucians (I guess some of you have heard or read about them) states our evolution works as double spiral (or a helix, just like the DNA).
First off, we are what they call "Virginal Spirits" and dwell in the high realms, although we are not individual souls and therefore, have no a developed conscience. We're only part of an "innocent", "unexperienced" or "virginal" Spirit.
The Spirit begins its journey through a spiral that "goes down". As it goes down, it incarnates in many different forms of increasing "individual conscience", such as minerals, plants, animals and finally humans. As we "go down" in the spiral, we acquire a soul, we become more conscious or "wise" individuals. Rosicrucians state that human beings dwell in the bottom of the double helix. As we become even more conscious, we begin our journey up into the second spiral, until we become Spirit once again, but not a "virginal" one, but a conscience Spirit who is also formed of individual wise souls, such as God Father.
The Rosicrucians also say going "up" or "down" the helix is not "right" or "wrong"; it's simply a necessary road for evolution, for the Supreme Energy to discover itself. We are the way God gets to know himself. Therefore, although human beings are below the helix and virginal Spirits are above, we are "wiser" (NOT "better") because we have already experienced individuality.
Everything in the universe works in cycles within cycles: we experience similar states, but with an increasing level of complexity or conscience - such as a student that reviews geometry in highschool, but with more difficult concepts that those he learned when he was in junior high. Therefore, evolution is not in the form of a circle that repeats itself, but a spiral: a circle that moves into different levels and therefore brings infinite wisdom to the soul.
An example of this: although we are currently experiencing the human state, within it we are still experiencing a reptilian conscience - conscience of low emotions, impulsive behavior lead by instincts and not reason, etc. After the so called "Earth's Ascension", we'll be experiencing a mammal-human conscience, and then a human-human conscience and so on.
The Rosicrucian conception deals with current mankind, but perhaps, it's not the same for everyone. For example, fairies: I understand they follow a different path and therefore haven't been in 3D bodies, like us. Is it possible that there are many evolutionary paths?
Thoth:Think of the whole of BEING as a many-faceted crystal. Each facet gives off a unique angle of reflection and yet contains the whole picture within it. "Evolution" is a man-made concept, although I use this term at times, as it is understood by humanity in their application of it. There is really only the ALL. As souls in various modalities of being reflect aspects of the "ALL," so they see this reflection as a path or evolutionary line that moves toward the ALL and expands to include more of it as it moves forward. In actuality, evolution is a product of time and time is a perception only. Yes, this perception can be measured and it can be warped - speeded up and slowed down. . . as “perception” creates subjective "realities." Thus evolution is bound within the same perception - that there is a timeline which it faithfully follows to an ultimate completion.
Yet human beings and whole worlds of beings do expand AWARENESS. At first through an expansion of perception and then jettisoning perception altogether to become Awareness. It is then that awareness is no longer an action but a place that is all-inclusive. Expansion of awareness, however, is not the result of spiritual evolution but of simply turning loose of EVERYTHING to become NOTHING.
This does not mean that evolution is an illusion. It does exist - but as a working concept within a specific consensual agreement of expression among the Many. This "Many" cuts to the cellular and even DNA level. . .so long as the original concept is in place within the self-created and sustained program of the Many.
Nature Spirits go along with the program of the natural world which the "Many" have put into place. But unlike currently incarnated souls on this planet, Nature Spirits are far more sentient than they are conscious. This means that they don't self-reflect as humans do, and so are less caught in the snares created by the paradigm: "I think, therefor I am."
Giselle:I read or already know that human beings dwell within this dimension because we have chosen to do so. In other words, our thoughts and feelings became denser and denser, and therefore our bodies became also denser. This makes sense to me, since it explains why Lemurians and early Atlanteans lived in "higher" realms.
As the Rosicrucians and Maia say, density is not "right" or "wrong". It is simply a path of evolution. But what happens next? We become denser and then lighter, and then what?? The helix begins once again?? So, have there been multiple "creations" and "universes"?
Thoth:From the perspective of evolution it is always forward motion, even when it appears otherwise. The wheel is never re-created. From the place of the "ALL" there is no wheel.
More simply put, while cycles are in place to aid in the "evolution" of the universe, cycles are temporal and very localized to what humans and many of their kindred beings perceive and work with and within. When the perception that the Many have of the spiral of evolution and thus cycles - each point above another point on the same spiral being a more evolved cycle of the previous one-  reaches a certain point of over-saturation in consciousness, the spiral becomes a torus - like a doughnut with a hole in the center - and then all being has no beginning and no end and thus no cycles either.
Of course there are individuals incarnate on earth now and in your past who have a larger grasp of living in the torus than the Many, although they have not perfected it. Such individuals are usually yogic masters or others of great illumination.
One can say that there are multiple universes or one universe with multiple arenas of interaction with Being.
Giselle:If there have been creations and universes for all eternity, then what's the whole point of evolution?? Just evolving and evolving. . . forever?
Thoth:I believe your question is indirectly answered above. Evolution is a sub-system of perceptual reality, and not the mainspring getting there. One could argue that turning from a spiral to a torus in Being is "evolution" but actually it is not, since the torus is already there. The Many simply choose not to perceive it yet. "Choice" is not a pawn of evolution although it knows how to play the game.
Giselle:The fundamental question: what is "eternity"? Is Creation an "eternal movement," such as Aristotle said? Or can we speak of an eternal fixed Spirit?
Thoth:Eternity is the IT beyond all categories and systems. The Lemurians called it the "ii" - the Sacred Nothing. Creation is an act of finding that Sacred Nothing that already IS. There is no “eternal fixed Spirit” because there are infinite ways to approach it, to know it, to BE it. So, from the evolutionary perspective, even God is evolving. . . and yet beyond the perception of evolution everything already IS. To the human mind this is, of course a paradox. To Divinity it is the formula of omni-being.
Marieah:what is the relevance to the New Earth Star of thethree serpent aspects of the goddessyou spoke of through Maia ten years ago?
Thoth:the three serpents become ONE as the helix tree of the Old Earth uncoils and reforms through the wave forms represented by the Blue and Red serpents (see article New Tree of Life / Serpent Rope and the Alpha-Omega Metatronic Spiral this issue) the third serpent is the power generated between the Red and the Blue. . . the Violet Flame Serpent of Transmuted Primal Energy. The three serpents of “conception, gestation and birth” then become the CHILD itself The Violet Flame of the New Earth.
Marieah:are the bee, the spider and the dove other aspects of the goddess? How many aspects do each of us need to connect with and anchor as we move into the energy of the New Earth Star?
Thoth:All “Living Symbols” of nature (including stones and crystals) are aspects of the goddess - the Mother. Each is drawn to different of Her energy-symbols at the appropriate times of their life. A symbol (sacred geometry) which incorporates them all is theROSE MYSTICA. The Rose Mystica you might say, is the Flower of Life for the New Earth Star.
Marieah:Do the seven veils relate to the Temple of Salomae and the progressive lifting of the veils over the third eye?
Thoth:Yes. They also relate to the SEVEN FLAMES of Numis’OM - see article The Council of the Seventh Flame and the Duat Path this issue.
PLEASE NOTE:if you wish to ask questions of Thoth relating to anything you read in this publication, or about planetary and cosmic happenings that you would like more clarity on, pleasesubmit your questionsto us. We will attune to Thoth and will print his responses to those questions he selects to answer in the following issue of Numis'OM ~ Eye of Metatron. We cannot promise that all questions will be answered, but we will do our best to accommodate those with the greatest universal scope and importance. We will give you credit for the questions as well unless you request anonymity.

Shiva Lingham at San Marga Monestary on Kaua'iphoto by Maia Christianne Nartoomid
Activation of the LemurianTemple-Node on Kaua'i

The Mu / Kaua'i temple-node Venusian template for the whole unfolding of the"Lotus" realityinto the primal earth (ie "evolution of species"). The Venus temple-node is the touch-point for that original unfolding. It does not contain the whole property - just the original trigger. As these two realities blended, for a period of time there was a balance between the two. The Venus node on Kaua'i holds the "memory" of that balance.

The Foundation Stone of Yephyra

In the 1990's Thoth revealed to me a symbolic Foundation Stone which he called the Yephyra.

Description of the YEPHYRA Logos:  A cube with a triangle containing an eye in the center.  The triangle is circumscribed by three energy lines moving from three spheres.  Surrounding the cube are twelve yod flames.
In the ancient aloii, or First Language of Mankind, 'Yephyra' meant 'to set aflame;' 'to burn from within;' 'to impassion with Spirit;' 'to Perfect;' and the 'Perfected Work.'  In choosing this Logos, Thoth has also given us the accompanying words: 'The Perfected Work We Shall Attain.'
Within the Mur-Atlan (Lemurian and Atlantean) cultures, the Foundation Stone of the temple was called the Yephyra.  In mystical Christianity, the Foundation Stone is a metaphor for the anchoring of the Spiritual Hierarchy in the Earth, and was exemplified in the service of the Apostle Peter, who was the 'Petra,' 'Cephas,' or Rock of the Cosmic Church in the Earth.
In theNew Age Bible Interpretation -- Old Testament, Volume II., Corinne Heline  expands upon the deeper esoteric meaning of the 'Foundation Stone,' when she writes:
In the majestic symbolism of Masonry there is none of greater mystic significance than the Foundation Stone, or Corner Stone.  This is representative of the spiritual perfection of the true indwelling Self, the Virgin Spirit, which is one with God.
. . .the 'fiery Stone,' inscribed upon with the Great Name of God, which is the Foundation of the created world.  Note that the cube, when projected upon a plane, forms the Latin cross, or 'measure of a man.'
The cube then, is a version of the cross. Thoth shows me now, how the Foundation Stone and the Galactic Cross are energetically one and the same!

Abraham and Moses promulgated its truth in their inner schools.  Upon this knowledge Enoch constructed his Arch and Solomon his Temple. . . Every Mystery School in the world is and has been centered in this esoteric thesis.
The triangle containing the Mystic Eye is well-known from the US dollar bill.  It is the All-seeing Eye of Truth.  Below is a passage from a medieval text now lost from this world, but still registered with the Akashic Record and visible to my inner eye regarding this eye.
None can escape its gaze, for it is Absolute and Uncompromising.
About the triangle are three spheres, which represent the three aspects of alchemical integration for Spirit with Matter:  Mutable, Immutable and Coherent; the latter meaning 'to be,' rather than to involve or engage in order to become.  Like with Jonathan Livingstone Seagull, alchemical coherency erases the time component and creates the instant 'being.'  Ancient master hierophants often wore a tattoo of the three spheres upon their forehead.  Thoth Hermes was born with birthmarks of the three spheres on his brow.  One who wore thetetchetor three spheres, was a master of the three forms of Spirit-Matter integration.
The 'energy' lines connecting the three spheres in the Logos symbol, are intended to represent the higher-form energy universe, existing beyond the third dimension, yet impressing upon it.

The Master Builders - Their Legacy

The Order of the Master Builders was first established long before the Adamic generations on  earth. They came from the Blue Star Rigel through the portal of Venus, earth's guardian planet. The Master Builders are from the genetic clan of the 'Sun Bow,' their symbol being a lion, a creature of their world, later to be genetically re-produced in Atlantis. Crest in the Stone Retreatphoto courtesy of William Buehler
Etheric Retreats of Thoth

First, a definition of what is meant by "Etheric Retreat" in this context: a place where portals exist into inter-dimensional fields which are guided by a Master Being - in this case, Thoth.
Thoth has informed me through the years that he has two Retreats in the earth. The first was established by him over 10,000 years ago. This is the one in the caverns under Lake Titicaca, Peru. The second is within Crestone Peak, aka Challenger Peak (re-named in honor of the space shuttle crew aboard the Challenger) which Thoth calls "Crest in the Stone" of the Sangre de Cristo Mountain range at Crestone, in the San Luis Valley of Colorado (where we lived for seven years.) This latter Retreat was established by him in 1994. At that time, he distinguished the two Retreats by saying that the one at Titicaca was more for inner earth inhabitants and the one in Mount Crestone was for the surface earth.
The Crestone Retreat is a portal for persons to pass through in astral or guided meditation. It has no physical structure on this plane of reality other than the mountain itself. The Titicaca Retreat is quite different. There are several physical entrances to it - coming both from the inner earth and the surface of the planet at Titicaca. While you might say it "caters" to the Interior Dwellers, it is not exclusive to them, and in the ancient past was entered by surface dwellers far more frequently than it is today. The catacomb of caverns are partly natural and partly man-made. Most of the complex existed long before it became Thoth's Retreat. It was originally used and added to by the aformentioned being, "AraMu Meru." This "cosmic being" Thoth informs me, created the incredible Titicaca complex was called "Asuala" by the People of MU who came with AraMu Meru to this region, and later by the priests and priestesses of the Atlantean-Inca.
It was transferred to the being we call "Thoth" by the Hierarchy when he was in his "Thoth Raismes" embodiment (prior to that he had been Toth-Mus-Zurud). However, the "Cosmic Being" of Thoth Raismes / Toth-Mus-Zurud was also one of the seven "layered" souls of AraMu Meru!
When I say that there are several physical entrances to Asuala, I do not mean that one can simply walk right into it. Firstly, they are well-concealed, not only physically, but through energy fields. Once a person were to actually see the portal (meaning he/she was vibrationally attuned to that protective energy field), they would then walk down a cavern tunnel a short way before encountering the first "signal". These signals are devices in the wall - like signs in stone with symbols upon them (see image on left). If the traveller is vibrationally attuned to the first "sign", he/she will know which tunnel to take from there, as there are several at each signal station. If he/she is not attuned, then that individual will simply feel strongly urged to retrace their steps or simply have no idea where to proceed from there.
Once a person passes through all the signal stations they come to "the" true entrance to Asuala. All doorways and passages to Thoth's Titicaca Retreat lead to this one entrance. In front of the entrance is an object difficult to describe, you see more-or-less what it looks like in the image to the right.
It is a living "plant" created by throught energy, not unlike certain new life forms of Numis'OM. However, this one was "designed" to emit an elixir-like substance, that when brreathed and tasted (very heavy ether, so it is absorbed into all senses), prepares the individual for entry into a higher vibrational space - a kind of pre-dimensional shifting space.

Once past the entrance into Asula, there are guardians and guides to greet you and take you to various parts of the Retreat. Each "chamber" is of a slightly different vibrational state. On the left we see the Asula Meditation Crystal, you can use it for attunement.
Some visitors are ready at a certain stage in their time at the Retreat to go into the Aramu Temple of Thoth in Numis'OM for a period of time - a direct portal is now open in both Retreats to Aramu. One may visit both in the astral Dreamtime, but Crest in the Stone is more easily accessible to that mode of experience. Thoth makes "appearances" in both Retreats at times. It is difficult to explain his role there. These Retreats are encompassed within his energy field, which is enormus, compared to a normal person's. Thoth may appear in his "Thoth Raismes" form, which he maintains still in the Inner Earth, or he may appear in his surface-earth embodiment as Thoth Amii - a being who walks the earth much as does Babaji.

The Stone of God mentioned in “The Island of Thirty Circles” is one half of the largest single pieces of the Lapis Exlis. The other half would become known as the Emerald Table of Thoth. It was once a larger piece that was split in two.
The Emerald Tablets were created alchemically by Thoth to contain the whole Enochian hologram he brought to earth in his Being and was therefore within his DNA. The tablets were then injected into the meteor "table."
I personally find it of interest that when I was guided by Thoth last month (April, 2007) to create the image of him standing before the Emerald Table, and to include it and further information on the Emerald Table in this issue of Numis’OM, I did not realize that this question was related to the Emerald Table! If you are interested in pursuing this topic, I suggest you read "The Vault of Orion"

New Earth World Treeby Maia Christianne NartoomidOR-0028STD
New Earth World Tree

The artwork above e is my symbolic artistic representation of the New Earth World Tree. The New Earth Star is a World System II (our current “Old Earth” is in the last stages of a World System I). World Systems II are still in duality, but in a much more balanced movement than are the World Systems I. As the New Earth Star continues to developed.
In Numis’OM we will find that the duality is like a vibrational DANCE in which each “partner” easily integrates and sustains the other. In my New Earth World Tree art, you can see that the male is in a supine position, integrated with the earth - passive and receptive - what we identify as a feminine quality. Yet he is also foundational - the “ground beneath our feet.”
The ability to manifest so much more easily in Numis’OM will allow the masculine energy to become more supple and less demanding, since demands on it’s own sheer strength of survival will be almost non-existent.
The female is floating above him, receiving from the energy ethers and stellar geometries. She sends these signals down into his ever-present “earth body.” She is the TREE rooted in the male-earth-foundation.
When the masculine is released from his current role of supplying, protecting and building sustainable environments, he will adapt to the role of a more supple, what we identify as “feminine” receptivity. Yet he will still be the foundation, as the female draws the etheric power into and out of the “form” through his “earth body.” Her ROOTS grow in his fertile soil and his ability to re-vitalize and sustain come from the power surging through her, filtering what is needed for the New Earth.
This is a greatly simplified picture, but that portion of which I was guided to express in my New Earth World Tree.

The Mermaid Coveart by Maia Christianne Nartoomidwater animation by Simeon NartoomidOR-0029STD
The New Avalon

What I am calling “New Avalon” is a reality world of Numis’OM which has been duplicated from the “Old Avalon” dimension here in this world. Yet, it is not exact. It’s primary difference (and this is an important one) is that it is not caught in the past - in holding ancient keys and codes, as is our Old Earth Avalon. It is taking the “base line” of the Old Avalon and upgrading it as the Numis’OM worlds move forward. Like the Old, the New Avalon has unicorns, dragons, mermaids (and mermen), griffins, etc... all energy forms which have assumed the “roles” our planetary mythos assigned to them. BUT the New Avalon is changing these attributes, slowly but surely, and allowing them to become more advanced in free-flowing imagery.
The “avalonic” astral realms of the Old Earth (our current earth), in which some souls venture after leaving their bodies behind (what we tend to call “death”) also contains the Old Avalon energy imaging.  In Yogananda’s “Autobiography of a Yogi” he writes of his encounter with his guru, Sri Yukteswar, after the latter’s “death.” He appeared to Yogananda at that time in the flesh, and told him of his experiences on many different astral planes of earth he had visited. In one instance, he spoke of mermaids in one of these realms. Yet earth’s astral planes are all part of the Old Earth. In the New Avalon, these mythic energy forms will work new wonders, and as they do they will change us and themselves.
Old or New, what is meant by “Avalon” in this context? Thoth defines it as an etheric dimension (within a specific electro-magnetic zone of earth) that is saturated with the Higher Nature elements or “devas.” It is that state of being in which the “High Devas” or organizers of Nature reside and extend themselves into other dimensions of earth through commands of life (via DNA) to the species.
Further, Avalon became infused with the human element when the veils between Avalon and this realm were more loosely defined. When the gates closed between the realms (except for a very few), some humans chose to stay on the other side. These were the ones who had mixed their blood with the faerie beings - the devas who took form more closely resembling us (in DNA). From this “mix” there came the Sidhe and some other faerie-human races. Much mythos comes to life in Avalon due to the thought forms of the human injection into that realm. The energy beings such as unicorns, dragons and mer-people are REAL, but the forms they choose to take are morphed from the human mythic design.
In the New Avalon this mythos is opening like a flower to new dimensions of being, and thus the beings and creatures of New Avalon are eternally engaged in an evolving process.

Opharby Maia Christianne Nartoomid
Ophar:an Intentional Community of Numis’OM

In this volume of Numis’OM I decided to spotlight what we might call an “intentional community” of Numis’OM - one that is already forming, composed of souls who have left the body on this side and are now dwelling in Numis’OM.
Before I continue concerning Ophar...
Souls that are currently inhabiting Numis’OM after the “death” of their physical bodies here, in the Old Earth, will receive an infusion of the energy particles from the planetary ascension when that time comes. Until then, they create their subtle-physical from the rich ethers of the forming Numis’OM itself.
Now returning to the subject of the intentional communities in the New Earth Star...
Souls of Numis’OM are drawn together by certain commonalities as they are here in the Old Earth. Yet, in the New Earth these commonalities are far more of essence, of purpose in Spirit, and not so caught up in the dross of personalities and lower wants and needs. In Numis’OM the “gathering” is instinctive. Souls just find themselves where they need to be. There is no logical decision-making or even emotional process involved.
So what are these commonalities which gather the souls in the collective? The major impetus is the coming together of souls for specific spiritual directives their soul is seeking,  under the guidance of Master Intelligences. Usually, these souls have been together many times in various levels of experience.
The community is a place to expand consciousness by being in the presence of radiant energy fields perpetuated therein... some from crystals and sacred geometry and other from Master Illuminaries. Of course, ultimately none of these “things” are necessary to the truly awakened soul, but there are many, many levels of “awakening.”  Numis’OM is a first stage arena for souls of the Old Earth, and then there are sub-stages within it. Thus, intentional communities such as Ophar are there for souls who find that quickening of Spirit in this manner of gathering.
Ophar is a community within the Temple (energy field) of Thoth, but it also radiates the Light of the Masters and Angelics with whom Thoth aligns his presence: the Archangels Mikael (Michael) and Metatron, among them.
Each wall, building and fountain - every symbol upon them and the placement of the structures in these “temple-cities” are perfectly aligned to the spiritual intent therein. So are the substances of stone, crystal and vegetation. Animals are present that assist individuals and groups. These animals, including birds, are devas of exceptional spiritual presence and sensitivity to what is needed by that individual and group and how they may support them in the process.
Sometimes Masters come among those gathered in the form of children - for their purity is so exceptional that they radiate the glow and appearance of a child.
Sometimes they appear with wizened age, as humans associate wisdom with age. Mostly, however, they appear in their early 30's and in what humans associate with the “prime of youth, power and beauty.”
Such associations among the souls of the New Earth Star will eventually fall away, and then there will be no need to “see” beings a certain way, or to appear one’s self in a specific form.
But that comes upon the soul much later than Numis’OM; although the last phases of Numis’OM come much closer to the experience of pure essence unadorned.
In the “Doma” the souls sing together as a pure energy from the higher throat chakra, joining their voices with great celestial harmonics. Individual singers sometimes perform. These songs / chants are filled with creative, flowing SPIRIT... lifting, swirling, clearing and re-ordering the consciousness of not only the singers, but the world in which they abide.
Light Languages permeate the experience shining brightly and vividly in holograms before the gathering. From these Symbols stream forth the angelic verses of Creation.
Ophar is especially keen for this type of energy generation. It also contains a vast holographic version of the akashic records, through which individuals may find deeper understanding of the “Higher Akashic,” for the lower akashic is no more for them.
The crystal capstone atop the Doma of Ophar issuuvyaor what Thoth has referred to in the past to me as “Golden Jasmine,” as this crystal gives off a fragrance similar to that of the flower by the same name.
In the days of the current or Old Earth, when Thoth and the other Solar Lords were among us, the Golden Jasmine crystal was brought up from the Interior Earth (inner earth) having been formed of the original creative fire of the planet.
Later, when certain devic beings became “unicorns” of the inner earth and of Avalon, they often produced the Golden Jasmine as a “sap” from their horns, to crystallize in time. In Numis’OM the Golden Jasmine is created in this way - given forth from the unicornic devas – not usually in tiny drops from horns, but in a larger manifested quantity.
There is also a specially faceted Golden Jasmine crystal in the Temple of Mira, within Ophar. It is a Moon Temple, where souls may come to receive the deep liquid elixir of the New Earth planet.
Various symbols will appear inside this crystal - here I have depicted one in Sanskrit, as it is one of the Light Languages familiar to us here, in the Old Earth.

The Lion's Gate Star Mapby Maia Christianne Nartoomid
The Lion’s Gate

The Attasic Universe is the Unified Field of full Christ Awareness - it is beyond all duality, the true “Holy Home” of all souls.
The New Earth Star is not developing in the Attasic, as World II Systems are still in some form of duality. However, the last stage of the New Earth Star will be like the top star of the Christmas Tree, just touching the ripples of the Attasic! Through that gate souls will gather into the Attasic, in the no-time of complete Oneness. The welcoming “Golden Star” of Mazuriel is the home star of all souls in World II Systems.
What Thoth calls the "Lion’s Gate" is in our constellation of Leo. It is composed of three of it’s stars” Denebola, Regulus (the lion’s heart) and Algieba (a binary system consisting of two stars).
The actual portal to Mazuriel in the Attasic is Denebola, yet Regulus is the “engine” the powers the field which links Denebola in this universe with Mazuriel in the Attasic. The binary system of Algieba is the “third eye” - the point where the akashic of Mazuriel flows into this universe, to guide and inspire Souls onward into Mazuriel’s embrace. As a binary, it also gives balance to the three-fold Star Gate.
Reference links:
In Numis’OM (and throughout the evolving stages of the New Earth Star) the Lion’s Gate is present as a “companion.” Through it, the Hierarchies of Mazuriel guide the process of all higher World System I and all World System II evolution. Yet, it need be understood that in Mazuriel - an Attasic non-dualistic star, there are no hierarchies! So why the seeming contradiction? Because the “Hierarchies of Mazuriel” do not abide within Mazuriel, and thus not within the Attasic. They dwell in the “ripples” to be found just between these two universal states. The “ripples” Thoth calls the zuvuya.
I thought this word seemed familiar, so I googled it and came up with the book  “Surfers of the Zuvuya” by Jose Arguelles  (which I have not read). Carl Elkins, Ph.D states that the Zuvuya is a Mayan word which is “a cosmic wave of energy that both defines and connects us all.”
Here is a rather extensive article entitled "Zuvuya: a Study of Aeonics" that I also found.
However, getting back to Thoth’s view, the Zuvuya is a ripple or wave-effect caused by the two planes of duality and non-duality touching and yet not able (or intended) to merge at that point, thus creating the ripples of inter-connectivity with the ESSENCE of RETURN.
A few specifics to fill in the complete Thothian Cosmology:
The place in this universe where it began - or rather burst through from the Attasic, is in the Vault of Orion within the constellation of Orion. It is here that we find the Eye of Ra, exposed by the Universal Tear.
The Eye of Ra is the point where all this universe's ley lines converge. It is a pin-point of "leakage" into and from the next universe. From the Eye of Ra (also called the "Heliomar" by Thoth) is emitted the pristine, creation-substance into this universe. The double-dynamic of the "Eye" is a blinking effect that is a "flashing double-diamond," responding to the quasar-like pulsing of the touching of the two universes.
The Eye of Ra is inter-dimensional, so our most powerful telescopes cannot see it. Yet it is visible on certain dimensional levels.
The Eye of Ra in Orion and the Lion’s Gate in Leo are intimately linked on the inner-planes. Their point of linkage is yet in another space-place: the star of Sirius in Canis Majoris - the Great Dog.
The Lion-Headed Sun Lords guardian the Eye of Ra through the temple-capstone of Telos.Aarkhara.
The Lion’s Gate is the pointing of “feeding” the light codes between our universe and the Attasic, through it’s Golden Star of Mazuriel. The Gate/Vault of Orion is where we return-connect to the Metatronic Spiral or full Light spectrum. Yet beyond the Metatron is the Attasic, where the ONE is beyond “Light” as we understand it.

Seal of the Scarabby Maia Christianne NartoomidARSY-0030STD
The Scarab Initiations

The Scarab began by that name in Egypt, but are more ancient in time, taking much of their sacred knowledge from The Atahula Book of Mu. Yet, let us begin in Egypt, where this wisdom was organized into a specific series of “initiations,” based on thenine energy bodies, relating to the body of the scarab.
The basis for these initiations was ultimately ascension of the vehicle, the body, the hosting merkabah of the soul. This form of “ascending” was not intended to transport one permanently to another realm, but for the intention of traveling through the dimensions to eventually return to share the gained enlightenment with others. Once enough people had been through the Scarab Initiations, they would become Immortals and the whole earth and its souls would begin the process of ascension into the New Earth Star.
The Scarab Initiations were composed (in that form) by Thoth Rasimes, yet he had no illusions that these initiations would process in an orderly fashion through the ages. Able to see through the veil into the future, he knew the road would be a long and arduous one, and that the Scarab Initiations would become lost in time. So why did he put them into motion?
Because Thoth, as an Illumined “Solar Lord” and Immortal himself could see, know, and understand all the intricate connections this “motion” would create throughout time and space - one action setting off a series of small “quakes” through time - responses so small they may seem inconsequential, yet they result in powerful human and planetary changes by the time they reach ages way into the future.
The Scarab Initiations continued in Egypt for centuries, but were eventually withdrawn as the Amun Priesthood came into power. They were revived again with Akhenaten, who had access to many of Thoth’s books (Thoth never wrote a book - his akashic scribes “read” and then wrote down his fire-inscriptions which he had placed into Amenti - Thoth’s Hall of Records).
After the death of Akhenaten, the sacred text of the Scarab was sequestered once again, but it also traveled. It was sent into hiding in distant lands, according to Thoth's original plan, which the secret Order of the Scarab continued to fulfill.
The Scarab Initiations were kept in the secret catacombs of the Library of Alexandria (which still exist) and were taught byHypatiato her inner initiates.
The Order of the Scarab placed copies of these sacred scrolls into the hands of the Grand Masters of Constantinople, the Moorish scholars of Spain and the Temples of India and Druid universities of the British Isles, among other far-reaching lands.
The Scarab Initiations are sealed in the akashic and available through that means only to those ready to receive them (which regrettably, I am not).
However, Thoth guided me to create the “Seal of the Scarab” (image above). You can use this to get in touch with the nine energy bodies and the scarab ritual (the center scarab being the 9th) by seeing yourself as the center scarab in the geometric of the Seal and then visualizing, and if possible physically posturing to some extent (if only symbolic) the positions of the scarab for each of those energy bodies, as described in our Spirit Mythos article,The Nine Energy Bodies.

Be creative and let Spirit guide you with each energy body / scarab co-ordinate / sacred name.

Even though you are enacting the ritual on only the first level of perception, it can still be as powerful as you accept it to be - for yourself and for the offering you make of yourself to the Spiritual Soul of earth.

Yeshua in the New Earthby Maia Christianne NartoomidAB-0040STD
Christ in the Old and New Earth

InThe Second Coming of ChristParamahansa Yogananda writes of Jesus’ time in India, Nepal and Tibet. He reveals that ancient texts in the Himis monastery of Tibet tell of “Issa” (Jesus / Yeshua / I’shoa), the enlightened one who spent several years among them. He writes of the various persons who saw this record of Issa having lived and studied in their country. Among them was Nicholas Notovitch in 1887. In 1922 Swami Abhedananda visited the Himis monastery and confirmed the details that Notovitch had written about in his book "The Unknown Life of Jesus Christ." Also in the 1920s, Nicholas Roerich saw as well as copied verses that were the same in content as those published by Notovitch.
Col. James Churchward, who wrote the “Mu” books in the 1930's was also privileged to be shown ancient texts in India and Tibet. In these texts were symbols and fragmented histories of the continent of Mu (Lemuria), and also an accounting of Issa having read and studied the Mu history there in Tibet.
An “old Rishi” told the Colonel that the words spoken by Jesus / Issa on the cross that have been handed down to us in biblical literature as “Eli, Eli, lama sabactha ni” was actually pure “Mu” language and should be “Hele, hele, lamat zabac ta ni.” (Hele--I faint. Hele--I faint; lamat zabac ta ni–darkness is coming over my face.)
Churchward continues saying that a Don Antonio Batres Jaurequi, a prominent Maya scholar of Guatamala in his book, History of Central America says that the last words of Jesus on the cross were in Maya and should be read “Hele, Hele, lamah sabac ta ni”. The translation in English, according to Jaurequi, is “Now I am fainting; the darkness covers my face.”
I find all this quite interesting as around 1980 I was making a tape recording of something I had written about Yeshua on the cross (The Mission). In it, there was a dramatic pause after the words, “and the head bowed”. When I played the tape back, in that space I heard a male voice speaking in an unknown (to me) language. The inflection sounded as if he were speaking something sacred, as if you were listening to a Rumi reading. While it only lasted about 6 seconds, I was able to catch some of the words. One was “Christu”, but other words seemed quite different – and different from each other – like words from several languages put together. At least one or two of the words sounded very Mayan. At least that was my impression.
From the akashic record of Thoth I have had insights of Yeshua’s stay in Tibet, India and Egypt... as well as China and Great Britain. I have asked of Thoth how Yeshua could have possibly traveled to all those places from the age of around 14 to 30, when travel was so arduous, dangerous and took so long. He explained to me that after Yeshua had spent several years in Tibet, he then went to Egypt to receive his Solar Initiation at Heliopolis (the ancient city of On). From there, he returned to Tibet / India / Nepal for some more years. However, by that time he was able to transport his body vehicle at will instantly to other locations on the earth. Thus he “journeyed” to China, Great Britain and some other locations in this manner.
From my unpublished manuscript Christ in the Earth:
Into the burning twilight of the universe, from the golden ebbing of one horizon, there shall come the single moment of comprehension that abides with the truth of all things, that rises above the sun in exaltation, alive in the glories of it’s own manifestation, infinite in beauty. Within this holiness of thought the plan of ages will uncover from the depths of darkness into the dwelling of the light, the resounding brightness that shall ring out through the lands, singing in silent music with eyes of the new day.
This brightness shall take form and substance through the consummation of power and glory, drawing from all ages that have fallen away and all time that has not yet seen birth. Through the strength of all that is or ever shall be there shall become a star born of all things that hold to God, yet not one point of light shall be dimmed to glorify it, for it shall be the servant of the night and the heralder of the new day. The star will bring the restoration of life for those who lift their eyes to see it, for it will shine on the living God of Truth, he that calls the earth his own and the heaven his father.
There will be those that shall bear witness of the child that lies in the light, his heart one with the pulsing source. There shall be those who witness for all mankind...the Krystu’atu (vehicle - body of Christ) shall birth under the star and shall birth under the witness of mankind; and shall die also under their witness...
All this shall come into being as surely as souls gather themselves together in darkness. The star will fade from the sight of mankind, and the voice of what has happened will echo through their words, which will be shaped in the style of men; and mankind will bury the Krystu as they bury their dead, for they had seen him die. They shall glorify his name yet cast his raiments aside and say “It is finished”.
Yet the universe shall still burn with the Krystu’anat (Christ Glory) and there shall continue to be moments that draw from all things and listen to truths; and as these things shall not cease, despite the dusk of mankind’s own choosing, the horizon of Krystu’aton (the Christ Sun King - the Logos sealed into the earth) awaits. ~ Kalhaba, scribe to the Emperor of Mu
Maia:What of the “Krystu” in the New Earth?
Thoth:When we speak of the “Christ” we do not seek this power within a religion. It is a universal frequency that was embodied to it’s fullest in the Earth within the incarnation of I’shoa / Yeshua or by his Greek name, Jesus. This power is part of a whole which includes the Buddhic frequency. These two together - the Christic and the Buddhic - form a Serpent of Light, the tail being the Buddah, who sends the charge of the sacred earth up through into the head of the serpent - the Christ, which is embodied in the World of the Greater Cosmos. The body of the Serpent of Light undulate with these two harmonious wave-forms, which are present in the DNA of all humanity - indeed, to some degree in all LIFE on earth. (note: Thoth is not addressing realities beyond “earth” in this answer, but that is not to imply that the “Christ” and the “Buddah” powers do not extend beyond this planet in other forms and identities.)
Maia:Will I’shoa appear to those who resonate with the “Christ” in the I’shoa embodiment in the New Earth - most specifically, in Numis’OM?
Thoth:He will, as will the Buddha, Mohammed and other spiritual icons of Mastery. However, those finding themselves in Numis’OM will have released the bonds of the more superficial “religion” associated with the historical figures and will see and understand them in a more expanded light. Thus, in Numis’OM - that first stage of souls accepting the New Earth Star, so these beings will infuse their “followers” with the true “doctrine” which is not a doctrine at all, but a truth of the life on the Old Earth of these beings: why it was, and how it was, and the greater purpose of that life incarnation. Once this enlightenment is received, these Masters will then reveal the pure essence they extend to the inhabitants of the New Earth Star.
See also my short story entitledThe Mission.

Islands in the Stream ~ Early Earthby Maia Christianne NartoomidOR-0009STD
The Unwinding Spiral - Our ReturnSagittarius and the Milky Way

Using the latest state-of-the-art technology, scientist have discovered that out solar system is not from the Milky Way, but is instead was born in the Sagittarius Dwarf galaxy! By looking at the cosmos through infrared light, scientist can see how the "decaying and dying spiral of the Sagittarius Dwarf wraps around and passes through our Milky Way."
Virginia and Massachusetts university teams are creating a "NEW STAR MAP showing our Solar System to be at the exact nexus crossroads were two galaxies are actually joining."
If our solar system originated in the Milky Way, we should be "oriented to the galaxy’s ecliptic, with the planets aligned around our Sun in much the same angle as our Sun aligns with the Milky Way."  However, this is not the case. We are positioned at an odd angle from the rest of the Milky Way - something that has been puzzling scientists for a long time.
Our solar system has become captured by the Milky Way out of the unwinding spiral of the Sagittarius Dwarf Galaxy!

Venus, Melchizedek and the Heaven Houses

In the double issue ofThe Source,  VOL. 02-03, 1985I wrote about the Lemurian Heaven Houses. To quote from this previous material (I have re-worded it a bit so that the sentence structure is more understandable):

From Venus, Earth’s guardian planet, the Lemurians established a means of a specific spiritual receipt in the Supreme Temple. . . The Hierarchies of the Living Lights (star-suns) then sent the emissary Melchizedek to Earth through the portal of Venus. It was in the Supreme Temple that he established the Order of Melchizedek.Surrounding the Supreme Temple was an outer circle of chambers, the whole composing the "Hall of the Heaven Houses," representing the celestial zodiac.Within each Heaven House was established one Venusian oracle priestess seven Earth priests, who carried out the revelations of the oracle priestess.
The article continues the story as to how a number of the priests became dissatisfied with their roles and overthrew the oracle priestesses (long after Melchizedek’s departure). Melchizedek was sent to restore balance between the male and female, that was already eroding in that early age. With the corruption of the Supreme Temple  that held the Eternal Flame of Venus, the planet of balanced LOVE, so the decline in the separation of the sexes continued.
It was ironically repeated in another Melchizedek Temple complex in Atlantis centuries later - this one was defiled as well. Neither complex was brought down by males alone. Certain female Earth priestesses (not Venusian oracles) played their role as well. Indeed, it was a "role," as such seeming corruption has it’s place in the awakening and strengthening of the human Spirit.
The 12 Heaven Houses represented the 12 signs of the zodiac, and thus theMazzaroth. The Supreme Temple and it’s Eternal Flame contained the vibration of 13 Heavens - theMazaloth.
Melchizedek also brought to Earth theArchangel Crystal, which contains the Light codes for releasing and transforming the "trapped energies" of Earth within Sirius. However, this crystal is only an outer sign of the crystalline Holy Light of our own DNA.
The Hierarchy that sent Melchizedek to Earth to establish the Order of Melchizedek, holds the vibration in their Being of the star-sun Sirius, which contains the node of healing for the Earth. It is the balance point between Orion and the Pleiades - creating a three-fold Creation matrix for Earth.
In order for LP-40 (Light Principle 40 - the Ascension of Earth) to take place, Sirius must releas the trapped energy that bled from the Earth’s formation when it originally formed on the node of the two merging galaxies: the Sagittarius Dwarf and the Milky Way.
As the first stage of the New Earth is now forming in the form of Numis’OM, there are those souls both now in Numis’OM and here in the current Earth, who are combining energies to help this action of release take place.

Dynamics of the 44:44 StarGate
