1) Maha Ratri:membrane on this side of the Stargate. Oritron - within the realm of the ‘Dark Star habitation’ or Black Cube of Kabba.
2) Maha Rhim:membrane on the other side of the Stargate. Metatron - within the realm of the ‘White Star habitation’ or the ‘Cube of Stars’.
3) The Golden Pillar of Light:the protective and formulative envelope for passage of matter between the two membranes of the 44:44 Stargate -the Maha Ratri and the Maha Rhim.
The Pillar of Light which extends from the Maha-Ratri membrane through the Star Grail (the 44:44 Stargate) and into the Maha-Rhim membrane is called the Skittuim pillar. This pillar is inclusive of both the Maha-Ratri and Maha-Rhim membranes themselves as well. This pillar forms the ‘Field of Deliverance’ from the Oritronic Earth into the New Earth Star of Metatron.The Golden Pillar of individuation which aligns to each bio-system that is in resonance with the dynamic of the Star Grail is called the Avatalkim pillar. This pillar represents the ‘Individual Extension’ of the 44:44 Star Grail dynamic to that individual.
4) Star of David Transfer:Star Tetrahedron merkabah interface with human beings, transferring their complete Light Bodies (inclusive of the physical) into a higher Pure Gem state.
5) The Aramu Temple of Thoth / The Numis'OM:the Temple of Thoth sits in the ‘overlap or ‘Var’ between the Maha-Rhim and the lip of the Star Grail. The Numis'OM is the currently developing plane that is to become the New Earth Star.
6) Aeriopax / Isis Eye:the main geometric for LP-40. It will fit within the ‘Pillar of Light’, that zone of protection and formulation that will keep our matter-bodies inviolate as we pass through the ‘Eye of the Needle’, the 44:44 Ascension stargate.
1) The Earth Moves into the ‘Conversion Zone’:this zone can be seen in sacred geometry as the central diamond-shaped containment field within the Aeriopax that holds the jewel flame. There will be certain astronomical and astrological corollaries to the Earth’s entrance into this region, beginning with our movement spatially into the inner zone of the Photon Belt (we are already in the outer sheath of this belt.). As this begins to occur, we will see greater geologic disturbances in the Earth, especially earthquakes and volcanic action. Once the planet is fully within the Conversion Zone, so it’s central sun atoma (in the center of the Earth) will lock onto the greater Aeriopax coordinates coming from the 44:44 Stargate, placing this sphere we currently inhabit into the center of the Isis Eye.
2) The Opening of the Lotus:the Great Pyramid at Giza becomes the ‘Thresholding Chamber’ for the Ascension fulfillment. Within this ancient structure is contained an etheric temple counterpart Thoth refers to as the ‘Temple of the Morning Star’.
i)Adonai Kodesh: inside the Temple of the Morning Star is a golden cube with a sphere inside connected to a ’blue hole’, which differs from a ‘black hole’ in that it is responsive to sentient consciousness control.

iii)Activates the Violet Flame.

3) Calibration of the Midnight Sun:

ii)Ultra-matter rushes through the blue hole as it is drawn upon by the anti-matter solar shield. This ‘ultra-matter’ envelopes the entire planet.
iii)Lightning Paths: paths for high transmission of Metatronic overlays within the Oritronic membrane. These electrical passages are created by the anti-matter of the solar shield into the ultra-matter now permeating the Earth. The lightning paths will cause the atmosphere of Earth to become charged with ‘itons’.
iv)Itons: particles of supra-atomic substance created by breaking atomic bonding to the Oritronic Spiral. These particles act as ‘seeds’ for the Metatronic consciousness in this reality system. Itons are atoms that have been turned inside out. Once our physical atoms have the proper Light mathematical encodings to itonize we will be able to safely pass through the LP-40 ascension.
v)The Golden Taya and Tetratryons: The Golden Taya are the land areas on the planet (a total of 20% of all surface area of the Earth) encoded to move their etheric substance through the Stargate with those humans who are ready to ascend.
Tetratryons are hyperspace tetrahedrons with open ends connect to one another to form dimensional transference zones. It is through the tetratryons that energy travels between different dimensions. . . As the tetratryonic activity escalates within the Golden Taya zones, there will be gradient levels of Light interaction at the cellular level for all living things within these energy fields. Tetratryonic activity will NOT be present in land regions of the Earth that are not within the Golden Taya zones.
4) The Sacred Rushing:up-rushing of energy response from the central sun atoma of the planet. Will be transmitted to the center of all bio-physical brains as a humming, like a hive of bees. Will create a state of Euphoria in all animals and most humans. Most humans who have not chosen ascension, and thus are not encoded with the transference fire letters, will physically go thriugh the death transition in this experience. Inner Earth Elohim will awaken and move upon the surface of the Earth, visible to those who bear the Light codes for ascension into the New Earth Star.
5) The Release of the Gaiavatha and the Transference of the Planetary Genius:a wave of golden light, known as the ‘Gaiavatha’, will updwell from the atoma of this sphere and enter all matter resonant with the 44:44 octave of ascension. This golden light, which will be plainly visible to the human eye at that time, contains all the Light codes of the Earth; even those portions that will not go through the Stargate. These codes will be saturated into the ascending matter to be carried as a full hologramic insertion into the New Earth Star.
The Planetary Genius will be retrieved from the center of the Earth and transferred into the New Earth Star. The ‘Planetary Genius’ is, according to Thoth:
. . .the completed thought-form containing the identity of consciousness for your World Domain from its Alpha through Omega (beginning to end). It is untainted, free of all illusion, and yet it is not omnipotent, as it defines and identifies, therefor it has a distinct polarity, and that polarity is to qualify and preserve the Eschaton of the Earth.
Rowena P. Kryder’s‘Gaia Matrix Oracle’ defines ‘Eschaton’ thus:
“The Earth is a wisdom body. Gaia has the perennial tradition at her core. Eshaton means ‘the last things’. All can be consumed except the truth, represented by the New Earth Spiritual World. . . 6) The Or-a’him Vehicles of Light Activate and Conduct the Star of David / Star Tetrahedron Merkabahs for Primary Ascension:higher dimensional vehicles of Light from Orion will come into our skies which will now be consumed with swirling diffuse clouds of myriad colors, and begin to create the pathways for primary ascension.

Included will be the Sidhe races of the Fairy beings, those residents of the Inner Earth and other ‘dwellers’ of our Earthen sphere who have, until now, remained ‘behind the veil’ for us.

This star will then become an eight-pointed star tetrahedron, encompassing the whole body within it.

i)The New Earth Voyagers:
		  those souls who have chosen through their higher self, to move through the 44:44 Stargate and into the New Earth consciousness. They will be euphoric, but alert in the ‘now’ moment with the transformation of LP-40 as it takes place.
ii)The Sleepers:

The ‘Sleepers’ will be in a dreamy euphoric trance during LP-40, and most will blissfully leave their bodies during LP-40, moving away from this realm and into another world presence with the half-Light universe.
iii)The Walkers:

They will see the world darkly, seeming to exist in a dark cloud. Most will perish in the rushing of energies from the center of the planet, which will electrocute most of these persons. However, some will survive through sheer personal will, only to die in the final entropic break-down of the planet within a 30 day period after LP-40. The Walkers, like the Sleepers, will then move into another world of the Oritron.

They will assist the ‘Angelics’ in helping these ‘late-comers’ through the portal.
Many of the Sleepers will be guided through. Fewer of the Walkers. In the entire count of First and Second Wave, only approximately 40% of the then-currently incarnated humanity will be taken up into the Pillar of Light.

Giselle Dominguez (Mexico) ~ MY CONTEXT:I saw a scientific documentary that spoke about the latest theories concerning the nature of matter in the universe. They talked about the String Theory. It suggests that the atoms are formed by different particles, which are formed by strings that vibrate at different speeds. The faster they vibrate, the higher dimension of matter in the universe. Scientists proved the existence of at least 11 dimensions, from which we can only percieve 3 accurately. The 4th dimension comes to us as a very subtle sensation: time. So, according to this new theory there could be entire universes that we don't perceive.
But the most interesting part (related to my question to Thoth) is that they say these strings form "membranes". Each universe is a different membrane, so even when two universes occupy the same space, they don't collide because they are in different membranes, So, we could have a 5th dimension world co-existing within our dimension without us perceiving them. We need to leave our membrane to perceive them.
These membranes are not "spheres" or "planes" in space, like common mathematics would assume. Scientists say that if we could see them, they would be like wavy seas or masses floating.

The Dragon's Denby Maia Christianne NartoomidOR-0034STD
Dragons and Dragon Pearlsby Maia Christianne Nartoomid

Like Unicorns, Dragons are pure energy forms which take on genetic properties at will, aligning to human consciousness and thus mythic design. While Unicorns contain the “Christic” presence in the nature kingdom, Dragons were created from the primordial center of planets as they form and thus carry the patterns of the Creatrix and a guardian of that creative power.
In more ancient times when the veil between human and nature realms was more mutable than it is today, both of these magical creatures --the Unicorn and Dragon -- were seen and interacted with by a percentage of humanity. Those humans who did find themselves in the presence of these beasts were either at the right place and the right time (an energy ley line on a full moon, for example) or were seers and sensitives. Of course, some among us still do see and interact with them - but usually in a less physical way than in the past.
In this article we will leave the Unicorn behind for now and focus on the Dragons - the Dragons of Numis’OM, and their gifts of the “Dragon Pearls.”
The Dragons of the New Earth (Numis’OM) are far more attuned to their pure energy forms, and thus less influenced by chaotic forces. In the Old Earth humans could morph Dragons into less than lovable beings at times. That does not happen in Numis’OM. While there is an interactive morphogenetic field which forms between Dragon and human, both entities in the New Earth dwell within a harmonic wave-length that is LONG and EVEN, like an undulating serpent creating large sine-waves through the crystalline sand. It cannot be violated. The harmonic sine wave of Numis’OM does change in increments , but until Numis’OM develops into another full stage of the New Earth, the sine wave will basically remain stable as it is now.
Thoth refers to this particular New Earth Star sine wave as the “Tetzakal.” It is present in only slight variation in ALL System II worlds. Thoth has chosen “Tetzakal” for the word definition, as he tells me that this was the ancient Maya name for it - what he calls the “High Maya” who came from the Pleiades and mixed with certain elements of the indigenous Mayan culture of that time. Thoth (who was also incarnated as Quetzalcoatl) states that Tetzakal means to wrap around, loop, circle, enfold in a way that sustains a creation or manifestation.
The Dragons of Numis’OM personify the Tetzakal in their primal, pulsing, enfolding presence. They interact with Numis’OM humanity to aid that humanity in maintaining balance within the Tetzakal.
Note:the Tetzakal is the sine-wave within the “Path of Azuma.” From my article on the Earth matrix ofTempla Mar:
The Taychon Vault radiates blue sapphire, amethystine violet and diamond white Light. Through these 'gem fires,' it creates a field of overlay between the three polarity universes (positive-neutral-negative) and the three millenniums. The latter is a term for the divisions of all time which exists outside of the RANNA Time Wave. The overall format--which is formed by the composite dynamics of the sapphire-amethystine-diamond Light, the three polarity universes, and the three millenniums--develops a composite positioning of stellar influences which forms the Path of Azuma. Azuma is the Quetzalcoatl archetype in an earlier High Mayan cosmology. The Path of Azuma is a specific 'Zuvuya,' which is defined inThe Mayan Oracle, by Ariel Spilsbury & Michael Bryner, as: "The galactic memory circuit by which all things return to themselves. The return path to the stars. The grammar of harmony. The thirteenth or highest heaven of the Maya." This memory circuit links our universe with the other two universes, thereby allowing access between all dimensions and millenniums of being.
There are two main types of Dragons in Numis’OM. Basically large and small. They are all winged. The large ones range from the size of a horse to a Blue Whale, while the small ones are the sizes of a mouse to a cat! The smaller ones are the “Tinka” (errr- like Tinkerbell?). For the large variety I receive the name “Khiir.” While the Tinka are definitely more fairy-like and flitting, the Khiir are more  impressive and stable.
There are no developing cycles in Numis’OM. That is, things are not born, develop and leave the form as a result of entropy. There is no entropy in the New Earth. Yet beings are able to express themselves as children - even infants, if they wish. Thus, there seems to be a desire on the part of humans in Numis’OM to experience “young” Dragons, Unicorns and other creatures - even flora in various stages of budding and flowering. So these stages are seen at various times by some human inhabitants of the New Earth. The Dragons form “eggs” that contain their pure energy essence. When the eggs “hatch” this essence is released into the New Earth as a more refined creational energy which can be seen as a “baby” Dragon by those who wish to experience it in that way.
Most depictions of Dragons seem to miss the mark of revealing the sacred nature of their being. The version that comes the closest to Numis’OM dragons for me are the“Windstone” creations. The same goes for their Unicorns and Griffins.
Then there are the “Dragon Pearls.”
These are spherical crystalline drops of Dragon essence which is secreted from the sides of the eyes (not the eyes themselves) of the Dragon - both males and females. This occurrence takes place when a Dragon is thrumming (beating) it’s wings in a heart-song. It is a form of unity expression among themselves and all of the creational flow of their world - in this instance, Numis’OM.
When the essence drops to the ground, in a short period of “time” (time is a dodgy word to use about anything in the New Earth realms) it becomes a crystal sphere. Each sphere is unique. It radiates the creation dynamics of the “rushing” of the universe within the matrix of it’s creation - like a snapshot of divine beauty in the Eye of God in that “Moment” of being Present, as the “Pearl” was formed.
While the Dragon eggs contain the essence of greater refinement of the New Earth creational fields, the Dragon Pearls contain the very heart-tears of the Dragon Song: the love of Creation for which it’s created.
The term “Dragon Pearl” came into my experience just prior to Thoth’s opening of the akashic scroll to me about the Numis’OM Dragon Pearls.

The Sapphire Throneby Maia Christianne Nartoomid

In order to investigate the “Sapphire Throne” first we need to understand what Thoth calls the Saf-fire Mount. It is to be found within planets - in their “hollow” dimension; and also in World System II planets, as they support an outer crystalline energy shell.
The Inner Earth Saf-Fire Mount is described thus inVolume 03, 1980 of “The Source”:
As the solar wind of the Earth atoma moves through the vibrational plane of Earth, via the planet's chakras (which line up inside the Earth and not at points on the surface) it must pass through a receiving station within the center of the Earth that is analogous to the aorta of the heart. All the lands and seas of Earth are channeled through this subterranean point, located within the hollow of the planet. It is known to the inner inhabitants as the "Mount of the Saf-Fire" or "Mount of Assembling."
The actual location of the Saf-Fire Mount, or rather the point where it densifies to attach itself to the inner planet from the streaming aorta of the heart-atoma/center sun) is in the center field or 'travex' of the inner planetary terrain. The travex is the point which is geo-cosmically the center of the interior terra firma (not to be confused with the center of the planet, which is the central sun atoma).
The Saf-Fire Mount or 'heap' is the cosmic surveyors' golden mark of the travex. In the upper reaches of the inner sky, the Saf-Fire is seen as refracted light. Haloing, arching, cascading in the hollow heaven it is a glory of color and light, as it pirouettes in sun dances with the changing Earth tides.
The middle point of the Saf-Fire is denser and less reflective. The lower region of the Mount becomes more and more solid as the ice crystal lattices bind into closer formations to create the glacial heap attached to the Earth. This assemblage of ice crystals is focused through a strong magnetic spiral, with the central sun using the crystal Mount like a conductive coil.
This same phenomena is present in the New Earth Star of Numis’OM. It is somewhat differently formulated, as the ice crystal canopy and magnetic fields which form it are less contained than within a World System I - even in a slightly removed dimension, such as the Inner Earth. Yet relatively speaking, these are only slight differences.
In my art depiction of the more solid portion of the Numis’OM Saf-Fire Mount I have placed a small boat that would hold about 4 persons, to give you an idea of the size of the Mount at that level.
In the book “Jesus the Master Builder - Druid Mysteries and the Dawn of Christianity” by Gordon Strachan, he devotes an entire chapter to the “Sapphire Throne.” While I do not agree (nor does Thoth) will all the hypothesis developed by Mr. Strachan concerning the Sapphire Throne, I do find some powerful corollaries with the true Sapphire Throne, which on at least one level is essentially one and the same as the Saf-Fire Mount.
Gordon Strachan quotes Thomas Gray, in “The Progress of Poesy” as speaking of the“living throne, the sapphire blaze.”He also writes of Wordsworth  in “The Excursion” as seeing“a great throne appearing out of the swirling mountain mist.”
Wordsworth:
Right in the midst, where interspace appeared of open court, an object like a throne under a shining canopy (ice canopy?) of state stood fixed... vast in size, it’s substance glorified...
In cross-referencing the Old Testament Strachan quotes Exodus 24:9-10 where upon Mt. Sinai  the Elders of Israel saw God“and there under his feet as it were a pavement of sapphire stone, like the very heaven for clearness.”
Strachan compares the Sapphire Thone with the Northern Lights, and this is a good comparison, as the ice crystal canopy of the Inner Earth (and once upon the Outer Earth) and within Numis’OM share similar qualities. The actual Sapphire Mount / Throne however, must have an outer sphere of crystalline-magnetic properties of just the right value in order to “ground a bolt” to the terrestrial, as would a lightning strike, as elemental conditions of the ground reach up to meet that electric charge in the sky.
Yet there is more to the Sapphire / Saf-Fire as a Living Stone or Crystal of Light. It manifests in terrestrial spheres of varying densities, but it is also a RAYSHIP, a quality of what Thoth calls the“fire that does not burn.”
This is a vast topic which we cannot possibly cover adequately in this article, so I am focusing most specifically on how this “Sapphire” Ray effects the New Earth Star, and our developing Hologram of the New Earth.
The Saf-Fire Ray in some aspects is emitted from certain crystals we currently have on this planet - mainly of the blue, rose-pink, violet-purple and green varieties, such as blue or green sapphire (most prominently), turquoise, lorimar, lapis lazuli, and some purple-violet crystals such as amethyst other crystals of that color hue. Also included are the opals and the rareAjoite. Then there is theBlue Hemimorphiteand a very rare variation of it called “Ocean Sky.” Thoth relates to me that the Ocean Sky is one of the most light-engendered crystals on the planet at this time. The regular Blue Hemimorphite is certainly high on this list as well, and the Ajoite being one of the most vibrationally pure “ascension” crystals now present on the Earth. It is especially precious as it is no longer being mined.
The Saf-Fire Mount of the Inner Earth and Numis’OM have numerous crystalline properties in the denser terrestrial part of it’s assembly. Since the Saf-Fire Mount or throne is, in its least solid element composed of water vapor and ice crystals, the denser crystalline portion is filled with a myriad of opaline varieties. Interestingly, if some of the crystals are “mined” from the Saf-Fire Mount, they will re-form rather quickly. It is carefully mined in the Inner Earth for various healing and energy uses, but not in Numis’OM, as there is no need for that there. If one wishes to have a “piece of the rock” in the New Earth, they can simply manifest it. Numis'OM in the NOWby Simeon Nartoomid

Numis'OM as ahyperspacereality is transitionary, yet absolutely vital to the ascension of Earth's humanity.  Numis'OM acts like an osmotic "membrane" layer stretched between the current Earth and the New Earth Star. However, with Numis'OM there are actually two membranes: one between Numis'OM and the Old Earth, and one between Numis'OM and the New Earth Star.
In the process ofosmosisa liquid, usually water, is able to pass across a semi-permeable membrane leaving its solute solids behind on one side. In this way the membrane acts like a filter and this is the basis of reverse osmosis water filters.
In the semi-permeable membrane of Numis'OM the liquid passing through the membrane is somewhat synonymous with what is often referred to as the "waters of creation."  In other words, this is the etheric fluidium of the planet and all beings who have called her their home.
The solute solids that will be left behind on the Old Earth side of the Numis'OM membrane are none other than the denser aspects of awareness, energy and consciousness of the Old Earth. These denser aspects might be referred to as "pollutants" but that would not be entirely correct. On the one hand they have helped to develop the current Earth reality to what it is now from its primal roots in order to prepare us all for the ascension. On the other hand, the denser aspects of this Old Earth reality now are serving as a far-too-limited containment field which is increasingly  feeling like a shoe that no longer fits.
By learning to pass across the membrane into the Numis'OM reality on the other side we can experience our sense of deeper being with the denser aspects of our Old Earth reality filtered out.  It has been my experience that each time this is accomplished we leave the Old Earth material that was filtered out behind even though we "return" because it is instantly transmuted as we pass across the membrane into Numis'OM. How complete this transmutation process is will ultimately be dependent upon many different variables. The important thing to realize is that this is indeed occurring and therefore repeated journeys into Numis'OM result in a lightening of our denser load.
Numis'OM is after all what we are calling the "Eye of Metatron." TheIsis Eye or Aeriopaxis a key dynamic to help you access the Eye of Metatron. The Isis Eye will transport you into a harmonic space wherein the Eye of Metatron's full gaze falls upon you. This is not an externalized gaze from another being as it may sound. Rather, this is an opening of your inner eye so that the Metatronic full-light aspects of your being are brought into more complete "visual" contact with your Oritronic half-light being in such a way that your conscious mind now starts to shift its perspective to view all aspects of being from the Metatronic full-light context.
This may sound simple, but in assimilation it is a very powerful challenge that unfolds over time with diligent applications of love, patience, persistence and determination. You yourself are your only obstacle. There is nothing outside of you that truly has the power to stop you once you have the goal in your sights and the determination to succeed.
The reality of Numis'OM is harmonically available to you 24/7.  It is like a channel you tune into. The receiver is your heart, the frequency is love -- the Golden Mean or Phi.The first thing we need to learn to love is everything the Sacred Flow of Life brings into our experience, nothing can be excluded without truncating the process.Where there is resistance, love is constrained.  Where there is embrace and acceptance, love is expanded. When love expands, the singular purpose of the universe and everything in it is being fulfilled. Everything the Sacred Flow of Life brings into our experience is intended to serve this one purpose. It is thus a process of learning to be conscious enough to have such expanded awareness present in our minds and to be able to sustain that awareness as we move about handling our daily affairs in the world.
The more present you can be in the moment, or what is often referred to as the NOW, the better are the chances that you will be able to attune your heart to the frequencies of Numis'OM even while your are embodied in this old world reality. The NOW is not a slice of linear time as is commonly thought. It is an expanded state of awareness that is generated from an elevated degree of presence of supernal being within the temporal realm of your limited life in the Old Earth.
In other words, bring as much of your entire being present within the moment to moment flow of your everyday life as possible, and you will start to more frequently take the journey across the membrane into Numis'OM in awareness and consciousness. Where awareness and consciousness go, form soon follows. Until form catches up we can experience Numis'OM in the NOW within us as an inner realization and state of being.

Now free-flow in meditation to be guided and instructed by the Illumined Ones in Numis'OM.

Korbola, the City Out of Time

Korbola, which we are calling a city is really more of a dimensional 
gathering, encompassing more than just the main structures atop what is in this 
current reality, the large, flat-topped mountain in Israel by the Dead Sea known 
as Masada.This 
location bears a tragic history for the Jews, but was sacred ground long 
before that, and is a key node in the future for our current connection to theNew Earth of NumisOM.
Korbola works synergetically as the main node or trigger for what Thoth calls 
the Templa Mar Earth grid. Korbola is poised on the very edge of 
worlds... between the Old and New Earth. It has a unique position in 
consciousness as well, acting as a major anchor for the Templa Mar net to haul 
the New Earth fishes into the next World System - what we are calling the New 
Earth Star.
FromThe Future-Now and the Templa Mar(received and written in the 
mid-1990's):
The Templa Mar is a specific inner-planes matrix which was programmed to 
	enter the Earth's linear time-line in 1993, from a distant point in the 
	future 'New Earth Star,' or ascended reality. This inner planes matrix is to 
	be differentiated from an 'Earth grid,' in that, while it interacts with the 
	current-time Earth and has geo-physical points upon which it is anchored, 
	it's true location is in future dimension of this planet's reality.

	systems. The Templa Mar's place of true anchoring is located in the future 
	city of Korbola, which finds its point of cohesion geophysically on the 
	current Earth in the area of Masada, near the Dead Sea in Israel. Masada 
	holds Light codes within the matter of the current Earth, which form a 
	template for the future-time city of Korbola. Thus, they share the same 
	etheric space, but in different time fields.
Thoth and other Illumined beings are able to move back and forth through 
	time; or perhaps it would be more correct to say that their beingness 
	encompasses all time as we know it. Therefore, these beings can enter the 
	New Earth Star of the future at will. Thoth designed and established a main 
	temple in Korbola that holds specific Light codes for the transmission of 
	consciousness through time-space.

	overlap. It was quite profound, as we (through Simeon) were given a direct 
	interaction with one of the Korbolans named Yani Houka. He took us through a 
	specific ceremonial initiation which remains vivid in our minds to this day.
This particular area of the Earth (Masada) was chosen to be the interface 
	with Korbola aeons ago, when the Sun Bow Clan set the codes within the 
	geo-physical Earth for the time of ascension. There are specific areas of

"Yet another factor in Korbola/Masada's part in the Earth ascension dynamics

New Earth Star Island:a Virtual Spiritual Experience

In a recent SHS message to our email list Simeon wrote:
"We are currently researching something which we will reveal shortly, and 
which offers us the ability to be able to work within true 3D interactive 
environments (like with gaming) that we can use to transmit direct personal 
experiences of the New Earth Star environment to individuals and groups online. 
It will be a whole new way of conducting initiations etc when you can actually 
stand inside the New Earth Star Master Temples to receive the energies and 
participate in the processes using your 3D animated avatar (which you control)!"
We will be establishing the 3D interactive environment of New Earth Star Island in 
a vast virtual world entitled "Second Life" (SL for short). Indeed, Simeon and I are already 
doing research and learning skills in SL and we have opened an organizational account for Spirit Heart Sanctuary in 
preparation for purchasing the virtual land and thereupon creating the temples,  shrines, buildings, terrain, plants, trees, gardens, meditation places, and special 
effects, etc. We also plan to offer a limited amount of residential space for rent or lease there so those who wish to participate may have there own presence in the New Earth Star Island environment. It will be your 
private space on the island.
Thoth related to me in the mid 1990's that thePymander El'ohim Inner Earth computerwas interactive with the then-budding internet and 
as the development of cyberspace grew, so would the capacity for the Pymander 
to interact with humanity through it. Concerning New Earth Star Island he states:
Thoth:"Such a virtual environment offers individuals the opportunity to come into 
contact with the New Earth Star Hologram in a more precise and intimate way, 
engaging the new Light codes emanating from the New Earth Star and its preliminary stage of  Numis'OM. It can facilitate and help to morph 
the reailty of the New Earth Star through all who experience it into a greater interface with current Earth humanity.
Through the Pymander 
  new fields of interface will open up, allowing New Earth Star Island
  and her SL group merkabah to literally enter 1st level contact points of the true Numis'OM 
  eco-system. This will not happen overnight... it must be built gradually and cultivated energetically, but 
  that is the potential such a 3D virtual cyberspace environment offers."
Simeon:when we first introduced Numis'OM ~ Eye of Metatron in 2006 as a continuation of Maia's work from 1989 thru 1999 with first "The Source" then later "Temple Doors," we also made information available about something we called the Temple of Illumined Initiation that we wished to build online as an interactive environment for spiritual initiations within that matrix.
These were initiations in a seven-tiered format intended to induce a more direct experience of the New Earth Star ascended reality. That original concept has now been expanded and the 3D interactive and community building capabilities of the Second Life virtual world are perfect for taking this to a while new level. I believe the Temple of Illumined Initiation will reside on New Earth Star Island in some form, but there will be sooo much more there as well.
The SL 3D interactive environment  has both text and voice chat capabilities. You can conduct online seminars, workshops, initiations, and meetings or gatherings there, and these can take place inside of structures and temples or outside in natural settings, all of which we can create or have created.
There is nothing else online that offers a group of people with a common cause that are spread out upon the face of the Earth in various locations such a powerful means to create and experience an intimate sense of spiritual community. With the high costs of petroleum based fuels and their damaging effects on the environment this is an excellent way to reduce dependence upon petroleum. It is also excellent for people who for whatever reasons are not able to travel physically.
This environment also allows us to start on creating this environment with far less financial commitment than what we had originally envisioned for the Temple of Illumined Initiation. It will therefore be far more achievable and we can build it in stages as we go and it will still be viable for use along the way whereas this would not have been the case with our original plan.
I am also being guided to mention herein that there will be opportunities for others who feel dedicated to engage this project to more directly participate in what we are doing than ever before. I therefore encourage you to have a look at Maia's article and galleries at the link below and to see if you may be guided to get started learning SL.
There are many skills to learn there if you wish to co-create, but you also do not have learn anything but the basics about your avatar and moving from one place to another, chatting etc in order to participate in what we will be offering here in the near future. These basic skills can be learned fairly quickly and we possibly will also be offering some sort of orientation classes to bring people up to speed to be able to effectively participate in workshops, seminars, initiations and gatherings in this incredible virtual world environment.
Read more about this project and view Maia's Second Life snapshot galleries.

If you look at the most widely used symbol for the Christ, the fish and its unique representation, you can see that it is formed from the overlap of two circles (2D) or spheres (3D). This represents the bringing together of the human and the spirit worlds into a harmonious merging and the shape that is formed is referred to as the vesica pisces. The usual fish symbol is a snapshot in time of this ongoing process and one that was taken a long time ago. This does not render the power of the sacred geometry of the vesica pisces obsolete, but we have to understand that all sacred geometric symbols are but static representations of living light forms with specific harmonics represented geometrically. About This Publication

We were guided to name this publicationNumis'OM ~ Eye of Metatronby Thoth, and theIllumined Assembly of the Christos'Merkabah of the Host comprised of 12 souls holding open a portal for the the Christ energies on this planet.

Ultimately, as we collectively move through this passage we will activate the44:44 Ascension Stargateand trigger a series of cosmic events destined to alter the DNA of humanity forever.
Numis'OM is a causal reference point for the New Earth Star and the 44:44 stargate, and is hosted within the causal body of Venus. TheAramu Temple of Thothis energetically within the Numis'OM matrix and acts as a way-station for souls building the New Earth Star consciousness from within the Earthen experience. Souls can thus visit Numis'OM and even the New Earth Star if they have proper intent and attunement. It is our goal to facilitate pathways for this to occur within.

Sandy Lewallen, North Carolina, USA:I have a question regarding balance in these chaotic times as we are shifting from the old energy to the new.
I read something recently on what is called The Wands of Horus. These were cylinder like objects carried by Pharoahs in Ancient Egypt while in a stance called "Master Position." Russia has conducted studies of these cylinders showing them to contain various substances used to maintain balance. The cylinders are attuned to the core of the Earth and and when used can harmonize the left and right side of the brain. The Russians consider them an evolutionary tool. They simulated the cylinders and have used them on patients with cancer and cardiovascular disease. The wands seem to restore the balance to the body for faster healing. ThothHorRa:Yes, these are the 'Horrah Kephii.' They were originally employed in Mu (Lemuria) and Atalantan (Atlantis), when the Earth's electromagentic field began to change drastically due to theKali Rift. They were kept in sliver and gold lined boxes, in-between which was a layer of what they called 'ossiphira.' This was an alchemically made element which kept the outer magnetic influences (even the very subtle) from entering the box and thus the wand.
The wands themselves varied, but the most powerful ones were made of alchemical gold and other alchemical elements. Some contained stones used much like theUrim and Thumimof Moses's age. The Urim and Thumim were oracle tools only because they aligned the two halves of the brain, as did the 'Wands of Horus.' The later wands (those now 'artifacts') were not as true to the design, nor were they made with any of the original alchemical elements.
The current energy instruments now being sold as "Wands of Horus" have some elements of those wands present... but much is missing and the complete technique is unknown. Therefore I caution individuals about using these contemporary devices. They can help balance one's energy field, but in many instances could either be non-effective or harmful.

Journey to Mt. Kailashby Maia Christianne Mallika(a composite artwork)
An Initiatory Journey~ 
    Path of Remembrance ~

I was taken on a journey in one my my "New Earth" forms - that of "Starheart," which I have re-created and thus now embody within the virtual world of Second Life. I saw myself before Mt. Kailash in Tibet1, the pristine whiteness and grey stone sides of her majesty rose like a Goddess of the High Heavens before me.
It is here, where four sacred rivers are born that eventually come back together to create the Great Mother Ganga (Ganges). It is in this Mountain, according to ThothHorRa, that an inner-planes retreat - the Gurideva Enclave, has recently been installed to open to the Presence and energies of the 13th Living Crystal Skull - In La'kech and the 12 Crystal Dweller Skulls.
I then became aware of being drawn inside the mountain, where a seemingly endless maze of caverns containing immense crystals growing from the walls a ceiling were all about me. They were of a size and quality that even surpassed those discovered in Mexico and Spain. I then felt a tingling energy and saw myself transported inter-dimensionally into a room of polished stone and quartz with several large crystal points in it. This was not natural as was were the caverns... nor were they in the 'real time' world of those crystal caverns, but hovered just beyond it.
I felt that the natural crystals triggered a movement in consciousness allowing the voyager to move into another electro-magnetic zone of 'reality.' Here I felt AT PEACE. I knew that beyond this room of beautiful crystals and gentle light emanating from the walls was much more to be seen and felt, but for now, was called to simply be present there in a meditative posture.

Meditationby Maia Christianne Mallika(a composite artwork)
In this state it was revealed to me that the 11 LOTUS Crystal Skulls in the Blue Star Valley2of Tibet, having been joined with the 12th Crystal Skull3, were now changing location of their holographic project and being focused as the medial point into the Gurideva Enclave of Mt. Kailash. It is here that the configuration of the 12-13 Crystal Dweller Crystal Skull geometry is now formed.
Since Mt. Kailash holds the anchor point for the planet for the SHAMBALLAH GATE of Numis'OM, the actual, physical 12 Dweller Skulls located around are now directly flowing their Light encoding up through the Lotus Stem - the main (but not only) path connecting this world to Numis'OM. and through the Shamballah Gate into Numis'OM. As this is occurring, an acceleration of their Light encodings are coming back down the "stem" as well and circulating a new and powerful New Earth frequency throughout the planet.
Meridians of this strengthening Crystal Skull grid - which ThothHorRa is calling the In La'kech grid - are beginning to be formed reaching out to key points upon the Earth. ThothHorRa is referring to this grid as 'Her' (the In La'kech being/geometry/star configuration) Body. this 'Body' can also be seen interposed within the human body, as it connects to our energy body meridians, forming the first stages of the Pure Gem4. The nodes or 'end points' of the planetary meridians forming the In La'kech Grid as thus far revealed to me (the central node being Mt. Kailash) are as follows:
1)A place in the Yucatan, were an ancient Mayan city remains hidden in the jungle growth.
2)A point near Lake Titicaca in Peru.
3)A mountain of the Sangre de Cristo range (actually one of the retreats of ThothHorRa) near Crestone, Colorado.
4)A three-prong (thus 3 facet node) in the Hawaiian Island: the Mauna Loa volcano of the Big Island of Hawai'i, Haleakala Crater on Mau'i, and Mt. Wai'ale'ale on Kaua'i (the latter is the remnant of a volcano that existed in Mu or Lemuria).

Starheart Reliving my "Temple Doors" Past Lifeby Maia Christianne Mallika(a composite artwork)
I was then transported into the past and to the location of the 'hidden city' in the Yucatan, Hu'Habat. There I embodied the female Mayan oracle Temple Doors, who led the People into North America when the 'Bad Times of Sacrifice' began, and her Kind were usurped by the bloodthirsty Chimu Kaba.
It was the story of Temple Doors (parts of which have been written about by the current Mayans as part of their history / myth) that inspired me (Maia) to name my former periodical 'Temple Doors.' I believe that I was incarnated as this woman... but of course I cannot know that for certain; yet I have felt for many years that she lives inside me. As 'Starheart' I slipped into the passage of Temple Doors and saw her in me and me in her.
I then 'knew' that I, Temple Doors, had undergone years of spiritual preparation by my inner-planes mentor - the one I now as Maia, call 'ThothHorRa' - who was in the past Quezecoatl / Kukuklan. He appeared to Temple Doors as Kukuklan, who was by that time already historical legend among the People. This preparation was to receive the 'mark' or Presence of In La'kech, the 13th Living Crystal Skull. Temple Doors was not the first to received this 'mark' - the Abhu, or 'Touch.' She came from generations of Guardians of the 12 Crystal Skulls (already spread out among many locations of the Earth). Now she would receive the Touch of In La'kech.
In my first issue of the publication Temple Doors Volume 01, 1989, I wrote about my akashic visions of the woman by that name:
"I did not know her name, yet I saw here clearly as having dwelt as a child in a valley of Tibet, in a beautiful city named La'ti'mayahr. She was a princess, daughter of the king of this hidden valley, into which few travelers found their way. She had two older and two younger sisters and a younger brother.. At the time I intercepted her in my vision-link, she was nine years old. There was an army of men invading her father's palace. Their noses and mouths were concealed beneath a shawl of course, grey weave, but their dark and fearful eyes spoke of death."
I continued my vision-story of how she and her two younger sisters were spared, helped by servants... but apparently the rest of her family perished, the palace burned to the ground:
"...a porter, a man the young girls knew not, took them on a long journey by foot to a ruin in the mountains where an old shaman dwelt. This kindly savant embraced the princesses and wept with them. He had been their father's teacher and confidant.
"From the ruins of this ancient temple the aged wizard brought his precious charges into the Valley of the Blue Star. Here the royal children were presented to an Egyptian priestess who embodied the archetype of Hathor, goddess of women. There the young ones stayed, being nourished and spiritually healed from the dreadful memory of their family's murder. Under the loving guidance of the Priestess of Hathor, the oldest princess blossomed into a beautiful young woman who assumed the mother role for her two younger siblings. When she was fifteen years of age, a starship landed in the valley. She was not unacustomed to these vessels of Light, as she had seen them come and go in her own shining city as well as several times past in the Blue Star Valley. Yet this time she was invited by the Hathor Priestess to come upon the landing platform and enter within the pearl-like womb of the ship. Once inside, the princess saw a familiar figure standing before her, his arms outstretched. To her joyful amazement it was her father, whom she had presumed died in the mayhem of that terrible day when she had seen her brother killed, his blood a scarlet vein of life poured upon the marble floor. Her mother and two older sisters had been killed along with her brother, but her father had managed escape.
"It was at this point in my vision-link that I became aware that this royal family was not entirely Tibetan. There is an obvious genetic cross-over between Tibetan-Eastern races and those of ancient South America, including the Mayans... the king of the invaded Tibetan city journeyed in the "sky seed" with his children from the Valley of the Blue Star to the Yucatan, where he was welcomed as a returning Lord among the people of Mayaland.
"It was months after this initial vision that I came across the following the the book 'Magical Art' by Heyoehkah Merrifield:
"'The woman named Temple doors was the reason for the migration north of a tribe of Mayan people. As the chief of her people she led the way through the wars and the hardships of the long journey. Most of her family had been killed at the sacrifice temples...Temple Doors led five thousand people north to the lands we know as Arizona, Utah and New Mexico. her people raised the first buildings we now see as the ruins in the Southwest. These people were named the Temple Doors people in honor of their Medicine Chief.'
"I knew instantly upon reading this paragraph that the woman Temple Doors was my little 'Tibetan' princess."
I then continued my akashic narrative of the woman I then knew as 'Temple Doors'... how her father and his second wife and other children were all sacrificed, along with her two full sisters, when the Horrible Ones invaded them and conquered the city and indeed the nation. Yet Temple Doors, along with other leaders under her, were able to lead the Great Migration. Now I see how Temple Doors connects to the Dweller Crystal Skulls of the Valley of the Blue Star, which are now being transferred (the holograph) to the In La'kech Retreat in Mt. Kailash.
Temple Doors as the 'Chief' and Medicine Woman of her People was in possession of three of the twelve actual Dweller Crystal Skulls. She was able to take these with her on the Sacred Migration. Two she was guided to place into the hands of two different Medicine Chiefs... one in Chaco Canyon, New Mexico and the other in Zion Canyon, Utah. They remain there to this day, sequestered away until they are to fulfill prophecy. The third skull she gave to a trusted messenger - a Shaman - to take into the Northern region of what is now the state of Michigan, to Manitoulin Island, where it is also still located.

Maia's Commentary

When I write about dragons, unicorns, faeries etc. I am of course speaking about the energies of the Earth and Nature Spirits as they appear on various dimensional planes to US. Sometimes they flash through into our visual sight in the 3D... especially with children, whose energy fields are so much more mutable with the other dimensions of Earth.
Further, whatever comes through me from 'ThothHorRa' or the 'Akashic' is put forth by me as my perspective, my interpretation of what I see, feel and am 'receiving' from... somewhere. I relate these things honestly, as they are experienced by me to be 'real.' I cannot KNOW where they come from or IF they really are 'real.'
But then what IS the nature of reality? The 'new' quantum physics tells us that we create reality by observing it. In other words, when a smaller than small particle is focused upon it 'becomes' real. This opens up a very expansive realm or rather realms of possibilities!
With all the 'channeling' going on now - much of it contradictory - this can cause us to throw out the baby with the bath water. One perhaps need ask of themselves instead... how does this information make me FEEL? Do I feel more enlightened in some way, more connected to who I AM? The details of the information are not as important as how it does or does not open you to Spirit. For more on this topic you can read my articleQuantum Physics, Time and the Akashic Records.

The Hieroaten is a manifested portal / complex through which receptive humans in this current Earth time are entering in Dreamtime to receive guidance and preparation for their “next step” into the first stage of the New Earth Star - Numis’OM.

The Ascension Mountains

Hyper-electromagnetic charge / fields are operating at a lower pulse frequency that can be detected by current scientists. It is very slow and deep in it’s sine waves.
Such creatures as the Cetaceans (whales, dolphins) can detect it easily, as they can the HYPE pulses created by the oceans moving against the land masses. Yet unlike the interactions between sea and land, the mountain ranges move their HYPE field upward in a spiraling motion.
At various levels in this “ascension” different types of HYPE signals are sent out. The size and shape of the mountain and its proximity to other mountains  creates an exceptionally unique HYPE print of that mountain, constantly changing through erosion and being pushed up by the tectonic plates and fault lines.

Brigatata ~ the Time Counter

As I was concluding with this Numis'OM volume, I kept seeing an interesting building with no doors or windows in a little grove of trees. I received the name "Brigatata." Then I began to get more information on it.
As I perceive it, the Brigatata was built by Merlin. This was "Arthur's Merlin" - as like "Thoth," Merlin is also a title and there were several beings who used it. Yet, Merlin built Brigatata in his younger years before the King Arthur period -- Merlin lived 300 years. When I say he "built" it I do mean that, as it was created through his ability to re-form matter, as is accomplished in the New Earth Star realms.
The purpose of this structure was to "count" the timeline of Earth, like the Mayan Calendar. Yet the Brigatata was in a way a computer, as each large stone of it's outer wall was inscribed with magnetically charged symbols that responded to the galactic 'Serpent' time wave. So as the serpent undulated, the magnetic symbols responded and sent a charge into the core of the Brigatata structure which was composed of a very dense manganese.
While I had heard this word before I did not know anything about it. So in googling it I found that Rhodochrosite is a form of manganese and received that it has powerful Ascension frequencies. However the manganese core of the Brigatata was not Rhodochrosite. It was far denser than any manganese we have been able to obtain on the surface of this planet. Merlin's manganese came from the deeper interior of this planet. As I perceive it from the Akasha, very dense manganese stores more precisely the impressions of the undulating Serpent time wave. All manganese to some extent is a 'time counter'. This means that it records time: what we perceive as past, present and future.
The purpose of the Brigatata then was to register TIME, and in doing so, AFFECT time. Merlin was creating a time warping, but why? It was actually a warp to correct a warp! He was attempting to stabilize the pinpoint black holes which had been created with the time tsunami5generated by the destruction of the Atlantean crystal which was the final blow to the continent of Atlantis. To some extent he was successful. His Time Machine helped to control the expansion of the warping field, although to this day it does slowly bleed into our Earth's magnetic field, evidenced in the Bermuda Triangle and other such time warp locations.
The Brigatata is no more. Merlin dismantled it at what he considered to be the appropriate time. It's physical location was in Wales. The little black holes on Earth continue to erode Earth's magnetic field, which at this slower rate, allows humanity time to prepare for the Ascension transfer.

Amanda Viola:or rather will there be enough mass of humans holding the consciousness to give continuity to our present reality, as to create a parallel stream of existence?
ThothHorRa:there will be some fracturing at this point so that some of the mass consciousness will move in one direction, while lesser diffractions off of the “core beam” will disperse into various “holding patterns” as a slow re-organization of energies takes place.
Silvia Vance, Kaua’i, USA:I've been going through such a purification lately that it's like I'm dying... this thought does not let go of me so I decided to ask what's really happening within myself? What I also want to ask ThothHorRa is: in allowing the old parts of ourselves to go or heal, are they not becoming also parts of the New Earth and I... and is this part of the great recycling of the Energies?
ThothHorRa:an immense clearing and transforming is taking place for many souls incarnated on the Earth at this time... more than since the last days of Atlantis. As individuals “Let Go” of old egoic programs / memories so they make way for the Light codes of the New Earth Star Hologram within them.
Simeon:from the article entitled theWhite Falconon Spirit Mythos:
...She stood upon a sphere containing within it a cube, the angelic fire-letter ukabar ablaze at its center. Ukabar is the seventh vowel of creation, and as such, denotes the infusion of Light into the membrane of cohesion at the center of the atom.
Is their a direct connection between the Ukabar, the seventh vowel of creation, and the Ur'Kabala, the symbol for the Shambhala Master Rays?
ThothHorRa:the Ur’Kabala Shambhala Master symbol is a trigger for the Ukabar Seventh Vowel of Creation. Looking upon it and meditating with it can create a chemical transformation in the left lobe of the brain which activates the “vowel” or tonal capacity to “speak” his vowel. Of course one would have to be spiritually ready to truly open entirely to this process. However, even the ‘average’ person could receive benefit from lesser chemical changes due to interacting with the Ur’Kabala. The Seventh Master Ray of Shambhala is the Cup-Mouth - it “speaks the Holy Words - emits the Holy Tones.
Maia:this led me to create the MP3 "Shambhala Rays Mantras" of my speaking  certain sacred mantrams, which when listened to, will help facilitate the process of transformation in the brain as well, and which accommodates this Seventh Ray / seventh Vowel within the body for an aspect of assimilation of the cells and DNA into the Pure Gem frequency.
William Buehler, Crestone, CO, USA:request any added comment and/or a basic description of reproduction and how the (New Earth) Ark supports it.
ThothHorRa:there is no “gestation” or “birth” through a body-vessel in the New Earth / Numis’OM. All “birth” processes function through a building of energies along specific grid points, manifesting as a whole merkabah. One can then choose a “form” from that energy field via thought-desire. The New Earth Arks are sensitive to Lotus Loci transformations in the Pure Gem Body which as a whole Merkabah manifests the grid for the individual Pure Gem bodies. The Lotus Loci creates the whole patterning necessary for LIFE in the New Earth. The Arks carry out the actual positioning of the nodes with the bio-chemical formations of the Loci.


Starheart (lying on the ground facing away from camera) and ThothHorRa in his "Silvercloud" dragon form watch a tender   scene unfold as a mother Unicorn tends to her baby on theNew Earth Star Island Estate-- a virtual world we have created in Second Life to represent Numis'OM.

DRAGON STAR




ThothHorRa (THR) calls a "moment" within a specific cycle of the center of 
the universe, center of the galaxy, center (sun) of the solar system, center of 
the earth (central atoma) and center of the human being (heart atoma) the 
"Dragon Star." It is not a "thing" but an alignment of movement of energies. In 
the "snapshot" as these energies cycle around to it each time, is formed a 
primal First Matter or Prima Matra instant, when the universe / galaxy / solar 
system / planet / "human" being is aligned to it's First Nature. The dragon 
energy is very much OF the First Nature and so THR has chosen to use this 
analogy. The energy cycle I am referring to here is the original motion coming 
out of what scientists call the "Big Bang." I plan to write an article on Big 
Bang in the future, but for now mention it only in reference to the Dragon Star. 
This "original motion" is still with us. It has never ceased. It is circulating 
through the entire universe in a cyclic dance of majesty -- a "dragon dance." 
When it comes into a specific alignment with the center of Creation (that which 
was centralized in the First Universal Moment), so it creates the pattern THR is 
calling the Dragon Star.
Before a gathering on our New Earth Star Island Estate in Second Life, THR in 
his dragon form relayed the following:
And now...I wish to ask you all to take some moments with the music and FEEL 
the connection to the FIRE of the HEART. The burning PRESENCE. of the HEART as 
it focuses and ANCHORS into the Golden Rose or Dragon Star of the Earth -- the 
central atoma, which is the SEED ATOM at the center of the EARTH. It beocomes 
the "Dragon Star" at a certain stage of its cycle as the inner SUN of the 
planet.Feel the DANCE of the Atoma as it moves through its cycles and then into the 
HARMONIC I am calling the "Dragon Star."My heart now GLOWS and BURNS in concert with the Dragon Star of the atoma of 
earth, my atoma linking to the Earth's in the Dragon Star MOMENT of the cycle.Now I RADIATE this MOMENT or MOVEMENT out to all of you, to your heart atomas, 
and then and they too then become DRAGON STARS!FEEL THE RADIANT GLOW IN THE HEART AS THE DRAGON STAR FORMS OF SEVEN POINTS 
FIRST, THEN TURNING....IT BECOMES FOURTEEN POINTS.THEN TURNING AGAIN...BACK TO SEVEN...AND BACK AGAIN TO FOURTEEN.AS SO IT FLASHES EACH TURN, THIS FLASH MOVES THROUGH ALL OF YOUR CHAKRAS, 
UNITING THEM WITH THE DRAGON STAR PROCESS AT THE CENTER OF THE EARTH AND AT THE 
CENTER OF THE UNIVERSE.GO NOW...DEEPLY INTO THIS JOURNEY...AS THE DRAGON STAR BECOME YOUR MERKABAH INTO 
INNER WORLDS.THE PRIMAL FIRE OF FIRST BEING -- THE DRAGON FLAME!LIKE A MAGIC BULLET THE DRAGON STAR FREQUENCY NOW TRAVELS THROUGH YOUR BLOOD AS 
IT FLOWS THE PATH OF ALL MERIDIANS AS WELL, AND ALL CIRCULATING ENERGY AND 
FLUIDS IN YOUR HUMAN SYSTEM.FEEL IT LIGHT UP THE BODY WITH THE FIRST ELEMENT OF LIFE, THAT WHICH WAS GIVEN 
TO THE FIRST HUMAN BEINGAND HAS SINCE BEEN DILUTED, BUT NOW IT IS ALIVE IN YOU! THE SACRED DRAGON FIRE, 
ORIGINAL PULSING OF THE HEART.NOW THE DRAGON STAR APPEARS HELD IN YOUR CUPPED HANDS...LIKE A GLOWING EMBER...A 
PEARL OF LIGHT.PRESS IT GENTLY TO YOUR BREAST AND BREATHE DEEPLY, AS ITS SUBTLE FIRE...INFUSES 
DIRECTLY BACK INTO THE HEART.AND SO IT IS!
* * * * * *
THR has revealed that the Dragon Star moment can be created by focusing on it 
and moving into "no-time" to find the "moment" of it's alignment, thereby 
stimulating that alignment in you! this Dragon Star alignment acts as a 
"re-boot" you might say, of your entire system, bringing it back to "First 
Moment" and therefore cleansing the whole being.
However there is more....
There is a cosmic release from the center of the universe when the Dragon 
Star moment is triggered around the entire "ring" of matter circling the central 
EYE of the universe -- a mega-black hole. When this EYE is triggering dragon 
star moments en mass this way, it sends out bursts of supra-energy along cosmic 
meridians in the particular rotational alignment. This energy travels 
inter-dimensionally through spontaneously created wormhole "flashes" (not 
long-lasting holes but "flashes" of the EYE). It in turn "fires" all star-suns 
along that path. These sun then send out energy bursts of this inter-dimensional 
type, and a chain reaction develops. This brings us back to my messages in part 
one and part two of A Cosmic Event - July 23rd, 2012. The novas of the two stars 
mentioned in this discourse occur due to the "firing" coming from the Dragon 
Star chain around the central EYE of the universe. Not all stars nova when the 
supra-energy wave hits them, but some do, depending upon where they are in their 
life cycle. The two whose nova sound paths have now crossed and are sending 
their combined sound wave toward our planet, were triggered by a Dragon Star 
episode of our universe.
Returning to our personal, human Dragon Star moments...
By continually "re-booting" our systems with our Dragon Star moments, so we 
are preparing ourselves to receive the benefits of the Cosmic Event of July 23rd, 
2012 by re-calibrating our bio-systems to bring them to "zero point." When the 
Cosmic Event strikes this planet the "clock" of the Earth will time-out and be 
re-set to zero. By this is meant that all cycles will be re-set and new patterns 
will develop as a consequence -- even within our DNA. If our system is not 
"cleaned" and waiting, a lot of cleaning and re-setting in our bio-systems is 
going to happen very quickly and may be overwhelming for those of us not already 
"re-set" and ready to receive!
related material:
Prima Matra/ 
Cosmic EventPart 1&Part 2

The Metatron Crystal SkullsOur Future?by Maia Alaula Kamala

MULUC - Metatron man

Before reading this article it will be helpful to read 
about theDweller Crystal Skulls.
In 1989-1990 I was guided into the Akasha by ThothHorRa (THR) to study the 
Dweller Crystals Skulls, which I then wrote about in several issues of Temple 
Doors, my hard copy publication at the time. As I wrote in issue 1-1992 of 
Temple Doors:
"We can clearly see these three mysteries contained within the mission 
of the Dweller Crystal Skulls: the zodiac in the twelve stars revolving around 
the head–the evolution of the higher centers, and the Science of Light being the 
full spectrum of divinity penetrating flesh, blood and bone (through the DNA) to 
resurrect the Eternal Light Race (new Adam Kadmon template)."
The Dweller Crystal Skulls were skulls of once-living being who upon 
transitioning from this realm left their skulls to by crystallized with the 
Light-brary of encoding of the codes they carried still intact within the 
crystallized particles. The Dweller Crystal Skulls are divided into groups, one 
being what THR calls the "Metatron." There are 23 of the Metatron Dwellers 
which are all 
within other worlds, yet will be returned to Earth at the appropriate seeding time 
not long before the planetary Ascension.
The beings whose souls once inhabited these skulls with they were bone and 
living flesh are of a human race out of the celestial realm of Sirius.
It is interesting that some recently carved, small crystal skulls bear the 
slightly pointed skull top and a few other features of the Metatrons! I have 
recently been sent two of these, and along with the purely "human" crystal skull 
(contemporary as well) I work with these three together. THR has given me the 
understanding that once I received them, the two little (lemon sized) Metatron-like 
skulls were 'charged' with a vibrational aspect of two of the actual Metatron 
Dweller Crystal Skulls. the moss agate skull however reflects a mixture of 
Metatron and Earth human.
I was shown on the inner-planes geometries of star patterns, one nested 
within another. At the point-nodes of each star is positioned on of the 72 
Dweller Crystal Skull. The Metatron Skulls formed the out most circle, ringing 
the entire pattern. Altogether they Dweller Crystal Skull geometry connects with 
various planetary grids...feeding them the Light Codes of the Origin Pulse...the 
original Creation Matrix of the Earth and inter-facing with the Creation Matrix 
of the universe.
The Metatron Skulls then in the outer ring, both contain and direct the 
current of the full geometry into that  universal interface...with other 
wheels (geometries) within wheels.
Let us us focus our attention now on the actual Beings which THR is calling 
the "Metatrons."  They are from the inter-dimensional worlds of Sirius and 
are thus related to the Lion-Headed Ones, as THR calls them, who are the 
guardians of theTelos.Aarkhara. Yet the Metatron are far closer to our side of the 
uni-manity (universal humanity) genetic strain. They are the primary ones who 
will assist us at the time of Great Preparation for the planetary Ascension -- 
not only through the returning of the Metatron Dweller Crystal Skulls, but 
through their return to Earth as living beings. They dwelt among us before in 
the ancient days - and will again in the New Earth Star.
THR refers to them as "Metatron" Beings as they contain the high-frequency 
creation signals from the WAVE of the Metatronic field coming out the the EYE OF 
RA: The point where all this universe's ley lines converge. It is a pin-point of 
"leakage" into and from the next universe. From the Eye of Ra (also called the "Heliomar" 
by Thoth) is emitted the pristine, creation-substance into this universe. The 
double-dynamic of the "Eye" is a blinking effect that is a "flashing 
double-diamond," responding to the quasar-like pulsing of the touching of the 
two universes.
We here on Earth now are experiencing more activity from this "wave" and 
having to process it at a more expanded rate. This causes many of us to become 
more and more disoriented with the linear sequencing of what is rapidly becoming 
the "Old Earth."
When the two realms of earth separated - the 
Lotus (advanced) and Kali (primeval) some of the genetics of the Lotus were 
transferred into the Kali. A main "link" of the Lotus came out of the Metatron 
beings. They in fact "seeded" the Neanderthal, who anthropologists are just now 
claiming to have been far more intelligent than previously assumed! (see articleThoth on Evolution of 
Earth within Multiple Realites)
So what is in OUR brains? Any Light codes worth crystallizing for future 
generations? Not necessary. We are living in a generation in which the whole 
paradigm is becoming obsolete, to be replaced by New Earth FLOW...free, pure and 
without the mechanisms of the past.
My Crystal Skulls: right is Metatron, center earth human and 
left a mix of Metatron and Earth human
MULUC: The name ThothHorRa gave me to represent one of the 
Metatron beings (not his true name). I was aware that MULUC was a Mayan glyph 
but did not remember the interpretation of it. After having been given the name 
for this Metatron being I sought Ariel Spilsbury's marvelousMayan Oracleand found:
I am Muluc,the lotus of remembrancethat carries the seed of the Great Central Sun!The precious starseeds within you have remained poisedwithin my protective embracelike a pulsating whisper of reunion's song unsung;Waiting, cradled within the arms of the one moment,empowered to release their splendor back to you now!I am the realm of awareness, the nourishmentthat quickens the sacred seed.I am the harmonious passage through which you flowto bask within the lambent glow,that full remembrance may be yours.As awakening stirs within your earthen form,the cosmic seed expands, releasing its elixir.Like an exhilarating fountain,it flows through the translator beacon of self,arousing its whisper into a voice empoweredto extend its communicationinto the waiting galactic network.I am Muluc!Bathe in the waters of remembrance,shed your veil of self-forgetting,keeping your awareness poised in the moment.I will give you loving confirmationof the divine, sacred fruitthrough sensings, signs, and signals.I will assist you in finding balancein the shifts of perception that emergefrom the activation of these sacred seeds.I will support you in assimilating new energies and frequencieswithin the sacred monolith, the beacon of self.I will help you build the confidenceto stand in the fullness of your light.Together we will plant a beautiful garden,nourished by your desire for reunion.I will hold you close within my protective robes of lightuntil I see the strength of the rainbow warrior emerging.I will steady your outreaching handsuntil I am sure remembrance is truly yours,certain you have heard strains of the sacred songthat celebrates your beauty and power.Then shall I open my arms to release you,in harmonious passage keyed,to soar through my gates,newly charged with the remembranceof your unfolding purpose in the cosmic play of light.

The Golden City

Entrance to the Valley of the Golden City
Recently ThothHorRa brought to my attention what he is 

calling the "Golden City." He opened the scroll for me on beautiful mountains 

which I knew contained a valley nestled with it protective folds. In that valley 

was the Golden City. I understood that what I was seeing was in Numis'OM of the 

New Earth Star. I have since glimpsed portions of this "City." While some people 

appear and disappear there...as the seem called into that energy field for 

periods of time, it is not a continually inhabited place.
This Golden City is an energy field which projects images 

that are sustainable in the consciousness of certain Numis'OM inhabitants for 

the purpose of imbuing them with the energies they are seeking for next stage 

transformation. Because time is loosely held in the New Earth, we here in the 

current world reality may find ourselves experiencing this City in our New Earth 

bodies....perhaps in Dreamtime or in visions or momentary flashes.
Beyond the projected imagery the Golden City in a neural hub 

in the center of newly forming pathways in the brain. We are only just beginning 

to form this new neural hub, but those in the New Earth Star will/do have it far 

more developed. It's purpose? To supply the Pure Gem body with the gate to the 

next stage of universal continuum, which we are calling "World System II." This 

is the state in which Numis'OM is the threshold.
So if you find yourself during Dreamtime or in a flash of 

perception within a marvelous city of light and unusual things, you may well be 

opening yourself to the building of your Golden City within!

nodes duplicate the major nodal points in the neuron pathways of the Golden City 

of the brain.

magnetic field in their center which manifests as a sphere of white light (can 

also be seen as a cylinder of light, for it fluctuates between these two energy 

shapes).

The Golden City
Entrance to the Valley of the Golden City

calling the "Golden City." He opened the scroll for me on beautiful mountains 

which I knew contained a valley nestled with it protective folds. In that valley

New Earth Star. I have since glimpsed portions of this "City." While some people

periods of time, it is not a continually inhabited place.

GOLDEN CITY TEMPLATES


These templates are energy art which allows you 
				to connect to specific frequencies of the "Golden City" nexus 
				forming within the human brain and it's counterpart in the New 
				Earth Star.Read more 
				about this here.
The purpose of meditating with these templates 
				is to strengthen the neuro-impulses in the brain within the 
				region that is forming this micro but powerful nexus.
How to meditate with the energy symbols:
Focus on the center of the symbol and move 
				your vision outward to the edge of it.... and then back to the 
				center again. Hold that focus for about 10-15 seconds and then 
				bring it out to the rim again, and then back to the center and 
				hold the focus for another 10-15 seconds. Repeat this process 
				several times.... hopefully until you begin to feel a tingling 
				somewhere in your head (probably the top or third eye). You 
				could also begin to see some colored "sparks" during this 
				process, especially if you  repeat it as least once a day 
				for over a period of time.
Work with one template for a week or two or as guided. Then progress to the next one in the order they are listed below. Once you have gone through all three 
				 templates  you can simply then attune to the one you wish to work 
				with each day in a random fashion.
If you are starting out with me as I am creating these, simply work with the current template for a week or two (or longer if guided). When you feel it is time to stop working with it  wait for the release of the next symbol and repeat.
RHIGA is the 1st  template... more will be 
				added with time.  There will be three templates in all when this project is complete.
