Alternate Realites, Jules Verne and the 
Ultimate Tea Party!


Prologue: This article mentions the virtual reality of "Second Life" 
(SL) in which I am actively engaged. We have our New EarthStar Island Estate (NESIE) 
in SL and I hold weekly spiritual gatherings there with people from around the 
world.
ThothHorRa (THR) has often brought to my attention the existence of 
"alternate realities" existing in "electro-magnetic zones" of the Earth. I have 
thus explored it more fully in my Akashic travels. Recently at one of our NESIE 
Gatherings in SL, THR discussed this topic with us. Below are portions of this 
transcript.
ThothHorRa 
	Khandr: NAMASTE.I discuss with you this gathering the 
	existence of various alternate realities within Earth's electro-magnetic 
	zones
These "alternate realities 
	are related to but not the same as the more diffuse "astral planes" to which 
	most souls move after their incarnation the alternate realities of the 
	electro-magnetic zones are actual ALTS shall we say of your own current 
	incarnation. (note: "ALTS" referred to here are "alternative avatars" as 
	many people in Second Life have more than one avatar which they can choose 
	to "embody.")
These 
	are "alternate" choices" your being is making of "existence" formats within 
	the electro-magnetic zones of Earth.
The EM zonesI speak of are beyond the 
	lesser wave forms. They are of a supra-nature and are the commanding forces 
	of the lesser electro-magnetic fields. The supra-EMs operate as whole 
	systemic functions...that is they effect the WHOLE planet and not just 
	specific locations. they do create pathways or zones within their wholistic 
	field. [12:19]  These pathways are "bends" in space-time.
One EM zone which is mis-functioning shall we 
	say, is the Bermuda Triangle. It is like a dying star, imploding at it's 
	center and becoming very unstable.
Now 
	we discuss the system itself and how your ALTS (alternate reality personas) 
	are operating within them as aspects of your incarnating nature Truthfully, SOULS 
	are Pure Essence. They do not enter 
	a body They stream into 
	it like this SL music. They do not think, 
	choose, accept or deny.SOULS are pure 
	essence. Yet individual 
	living beings are "streaming" 
	their souls - and in that 
	stream so the identity forms from the 
	particles of elements it encounters. The Elemental Body intelligence 
	then forms within the elemental vehicle of the physical body. While I use 
	the word "intelligence" here, the Elemental Body is largely instinctual and 
	very basic.
Also this streaming is 
	getting caught in the EM and is then 
	creating whorls - patterns like a magnet 
	causes when influencing particles These whorls 
	then begin to migrate into various EM 
	zones which align to 
	their unique composition of particles and thus the 
	"personality" and "character" which is being created through the DNA 
	guides the "life" 
	of the particles These particles then find themselves forming another EM "being" out of the first. 
	This then is how 
	the EM ALTS are created.
In the NEW EARTH 
	there will be / are more fluid zones which form instantly out of THOUGHT and there will be 
	/ are 
	no astral planes, for that layer 
	will be absorbed by the intense radiance of the New Earth Star.
Yet now in your 
	current embodiments you are all in the 
	process of collecting the ALTS and experiencing them more vividly as a part of 
	YOU and then 
	integrating them. For this 
	integration is necessary in what we are calling the "Ascension" into the New 
	Earth."
--- end of THR transmission
I (Maia) 
	had my own bit of "alternate awareness" experience lately. I have 
	always had a strong draw toward Jules Verne and his visions of the future 
	(from the time perspective in which he lived). The stories themselves I have 
	not found all that interesting, but rather the backgrounds to them. In 
	exploring this further within the Akasha it was revealed to me that indeed 
	Verne was drawing from the Akasha as well...upon an alternate reality 
	similar to our own and yet with distinct differences as well. I feel that I 
	am drawn to it because one of my "alternates" is within that reality.
Not knowing my feelings about the Jules Verne 
	sagas, a friend in Second Life gave me two "Verne-Like" ships! A large one 
	and then a little one which was already named "Nessie."  Virtual 
	realities such as Second Life allow you to experience in a more up close and 
	personal manner your deeper longings, dreams and fantasies. This can be 
	healthy or unhealthy depending on your choices. For me, SL offers me the 
	opportunity to explore in animated 3D what I could only see inside my head 
	before.
So now as I stepped into my large skyship 
	which I named Nautilus II, I felt a powerful surge...as if I was consciously 
	connecting to and living one of my alternate realities. I can only say 
	here...and with deep gravity...WOW!

Maia as 
	"Starheart" aboard the Naulitus II, ready to start all engines and FLY!
As 
	sound of the engines ignited under my control the feeling was eerie. A time 
	warp in my brain. How many of us have felt that unicorn beneath us or known 
	that just around the bend our crystal cave awaited? Not a child's fantasy 
	(really there is no such thing, is there? Childrenknow) but a very 
	real and palatable feeling racing through us.

Flying 
	around NESIE in Nessie
So the question remains...how do we integrate these realites? 
	Or are we really meant to just yet? THR states:"...in your current embodiments you are all in the process of collecting the 
	ALTS and experiencing them more vividly as a part of YOU and then 
	integrating them."This would indicate that at least for most of us, we 
	are still in the stage of experiencing more fully our alternate expressions 
	in the many EM zones of Earth. Yet integration is soon upon us. We need to 
	be prepared to bring all these wonderful selves together into one shining 
	being. Of course they already ARE together...it is a matter of opening the 
	gate within so we can truly feel that; and right now we are still getting to 
	know at least some of the parts of us, in various ways.
So let us have one fantastic tea party with 
	all of our "selves"...yes, invite the whole crew even though perhaps only a 
	handful show up. The others are just shy, hanging around the door somewhere. 
	Sitting down at the table with Self is a good way to begin your day.
Read more about Second Life 
and NESIE.

QUANTUM STARLIGHT STREAMING RE-CALIBRATION
SL/NESIE Group working with QSSR
Recently in a gathering with Second Life on our New Earth Star Island Estate 
(NESIE), ThothHorRa elaborated on something he is calling "Quantum Starlight 
Streaming" or QSS. From the transcript of this gathering I quote below.
Starheart (Maia):A few days ago as I was doing my morning healing on 
myself all of a sudden I felt /saw these laser streams coming down through my 
body. They were LIGHT but kind of liquid light and they were linear like a line 
of them...and they were many-colored. Some were red, others green, then blue, 
purple, etc and some were pure white light. They had number sequences pouring 
out of them (this has since changed to flame letters of Light Language). I felt 
the difference in my body and a charge of energy moving through me.So now ThothHorRa is wishing to speaking on this...
ThothHorRa:I have suggested calling it QUANTUM STAR STREAMING as it is a streaming or 
pouring in of highly refined star light into the body. Actually it is always 
happening for everyone, however, when you focus upon it and ask for 
"re-calibration" it clears the circuitry for a new round of infusion.
The DNA is connected to a universal grid of quantum light calibration that is 
neither "here" nor "there" and yet everywhere. DNA manifests directly from that 
grid and it can change in an INSTANT. So why is it not doing so?  It 
IS...on subtle yet important levels. These subtle levels contain major triggers 
for future changes of far more consequence as Earth moves forever deeper into 
creating it's New Earth Hologram. The "streaming" of quantum star light  is 
becoming a greater definition, enhancing more quickly the entire human body 
landscape beginning with the smallest crystalline structure in the DNA.By calling upon the QSS (Quantum Star Streaming) you are directly and 
consciously accessing the Quantum Field Grid. You are sending the message:I 
SEE YOU...RESPOND!The entire universe is "scripted" to respond to code. DNA 
is the essential code breaker, sender and receiver in the human realm. It is 
alsocomposed of Starlightjust as is everything else in and about you.The numbers in the Star Steams Maia-Star was seeing  is how her brain 
interpreted the numerical vibration...into her understanding of it. This is the 
high-frequency level of encoding coming into the DNA. If one line were to change 
a number by just one decimal the whole human form would change drastically. Yet 
the Quantum Field or Grid keeps the QSS from wobbling - from any distortion in 
the stream. However when the field begins to change (as it is now) so the 
streaming changes. This is intended, for the Greater Plan is always about 
CHANGE.Let us now imagine each of you - how the Quantum star streaming looks to your 
senses as it pours into your DNA. Take some moments...see feel and call upon the 
star streaming. Say I SEE YOU - RESPOND. LET THE RE-CALIBRATION BEGIN!Feel the liquid light trace geometries of your DNA...deep in the core of the 
structure...filling and refreshing the codes therein. The code of the DNA that 
give the HEART it's intelligence (for the heart is the supreme instrument of 
intelligent coherence in the body).Feel this code being RECEIVED by the heart...UPDATING its function and 
coherency.
(a period of time lapses)Now...bring yourself  BACK to here and now...but know that the streaming 
never stops until your body ceases life on this plane, and even then it's 
template is stored in your ethereal body for future assimilation within 
incarnation.(end of THR transmission)
The following is excerpted from our Network Healing gathering on NESIE (with 
some additional information added):
Starheart-Maia:I am going to briefly talk about the Quantum Starlight 
Streaming or QSS. These are starlight codes...YOUR codes which come from the 
starlight of your bodies that was created when the "Big Bag" banged. When your 
bodies are created in ANY life time on ANY planet or dimension it has the same 
star codes. This of keeps track of ALL of you, so to speak. When in the QSS 
re-calibration mode your being calls upon this streaming to bring ALL into 
re-calibration...to CENTER...to the zero point. Everything that is of the 
elements has the QSS streaming and can thus be re-calibrated in this manner - 
including your garden, and even the energies in your home.When you call upon your QSS to re-calibrate you are calling upon your over-soul 
 to stream the zero point or first "bang" output into your body. It is like 
saying "okay this is where the streaming starts. This is my zero point. 
Re-calibrate all to this reference."
Our starlight drifts with the decay of 
atoms, moving through the time line like dandelion fluff on the breeze. 
Re-calibration brings it back to zero point...as least in that moment. Of course 
it will immediately start to drift again, but it gives you a moment to reference 
your zero point, which sends a tone or signal out to your entire body that is 
reminding all your cells exactly WHO and WHAT you are and where you are intended 
to go!
(end of transcript excerpts)
There are many ways you can activate QSS 
Re-calibration (QSSR). One is as given above, calling upon it with a cue of some 
kind, such as "QSS Re-calibrate now." You can also add a "target" which would be 
a template of some kind - a grid to help focus the energy. this could be a 
crystal which you program with intention to be your target, or several crystals 
in a particular pattern (as you feel so guided) to cue you into the QSSR. It can 
also be an energy-art, such as a mandala, etc.
You can do QSSR on water, food and even your 
garden. With food and water QSSR it just before eating or drinking. For a 
garden, set some QSSR programmed crystals within it and then call upon 
re-calibration for it several times a day. You don't have to be AT the location 
for this to work.
QSSR for another person
You can send QSSR to another person 
but...there is a specific difference in doing this. First you ask the BEING of 
that person for permission to aidthemin QSSR. This request can be made 
silently through the inner planes or verbally to them. You then proceed with 
their QSSR with the intention that ONLY if the BEING of this other person is 
engaged in the process is it viable. In other words it can be silently sent to 
someone who would not consciously co-operate but their greater BEING would!
In Groups
QSSR can be especially powerful in groups of 
people all intending and focusing re-calibration together. What occurs then is 
that not only is the individual in the group re-calibrating but thegroupis as well! As a unit of ENERGY. This group process can be done in person or in 
a conference call, in a virtual reality set-up, etc.
How Far?
How far could we take this? THR has said that 
we can even send it to whole nations! To do that one would need to "ask 
permission" to assist the mass consciousness of that nation - not each 
individual within it. I am seriously considering facilitating some QSSR 
conference calls for groups and nations.
In Conclusion

the star fields within the body - the entire body, all energy bodies included. 
This brings the whole elemental and energy being back to zero point, to that 
contact zone where you are free of "static" and have a blessed moment to

now what I AM and what my program IS!"

The GLO'RII'A - New Earth Ark of the Mother

Starheart (Maia) sits of the Glory Seat of the New Ark of the 
Mother
In the early morning hours of November 8th, 2009 - which was the beginning of 
the 6th Day or 12 Heaven in the Mayan Calendar - I awoke to see in my mind an 
incredible sight. It was a series of circular platforms rotating with a “Seat” 
on the top platform. Light was moving through it from below and above. The whole 
platform system was made of gold, with marvelous golden lotus buds beaming rays 
of light upward. The seat was crafted of golden lotus petals. It was far grander 
than the one you see here, but this one which I have created in the virtual 
world of Second Life has the basic structure and movement of the object I 
witnessed. In my waking dream I heard the incredible tone coming from it: MAAAAA. 
It was like the chorus of a thousand angelic voices all blending together in 
perfection.As I became more conscious the scene and harmonic dissipated and faded into 
oblivion. I longed for it to return! I had just been contemplating sitting in 
that SEAT when all of it left me.I then “knew” that what I was seeing was the GLO’RII’A New Earth Ark of the 
Mother. It could change its outer form for different purposes but the basic 
schematic remained the same; and that is what you are seeing here...the basic 
pattern of it, with the rotating platforms.It was revealed to me that it’s true dwelling place is within the “Golden City” 
of the human brain. Which is now being built within us, and as a visual 
counter-part being created also in the New Earth Star realm.The Glo’Rii’A New Earth Ark is the key Ark of alignment for our energy systems 
in transporting us into the New Earth vibration. It offers us a path (in the 
genetic DNA) to true Presence. What I saw and is manifested in the New Earth 
realm is an outer expression of this inner world creation evolving in our brains 
and DNA.
I felt compelled to re-create at least the basic system visually in some way. 
Since the whole devise was rotating at two different levels I decided to build 
it in the virtual world of Second Life and then have a friend there video it for 
me. We will now have monthly "Glo'Rii'A Encantations" there.
Process with Glo'Rii'A being performed in Second Life

The video is very short but I feel it is effective energetically 
to bring the Presence forth. Unfortunately the disks do not appear to be moving 
in this film, although theyareactually slowly rotating. The incredible 
music was composed and performed byBruce 
Mitchell. I asked her 
to attune to what I had heard on the inner-planes and she did! It is amazingly 
similar.

music for meditation and activation

The Academy of ON(Semik Ra'Hanok)

Maia's rendition of the Logo of Semik Ra'Hanok

Some 10,000 plus years ago whenThoth Raismes of Aphraabided 
in Egyptos he had constructed according to sacred pattern, the Semik Ra'Hanok 
which we will call here the Academy of On, for it was often generalized as the 
great learning center of the city of On (An / Divine Light), much later to be 
named Heliopolis (City of the Sun) by the Greeks.
This "academy" was much more than simply a place of learning. 
Yes, Thoth and certain initiate teachers under him did hold discourses and 
discussion on various topics. Semik Ra'Hanok means "the becoming of the Pillar 
of Light (or fire)." Thus on entered this place to become that vessel or pillar 
of LIGHT. Some only were able to attend the discourses and achieve a measure of 
learned understanding. Many other went on to higher stages of receipt which on 
the outer was evidenced by being able to change the body vessel through 
molecular re-organzation...this for transporting it to other locations and even 
other dimensions. Yet these were not parlor tricks but a result of deep inner 
spiritualization of all aspects of the Being.
Semik Ra'Hanok was not just one structure but a complex 
containing various buildings, open plazas and large sculptures which one could 
enter and receive energy for different levels of awakening.
At the center of the complex was the Temple of Transformation. 
This was a large pyramid-shaped building. It was not a "pyramid" in the sense of 
the ones with which we are familiar on Giza and other areas of Egypt which we 
now find there. It was a building with rooms, stairs and hallways, but in the 
shape of a pyramid. However some of the chambers were quite transendental in 
nature and purpose. Others were rooms for high-level instruction and initiation.
Thoth Raismes came to the Academy periodically, but for the 
most part it was operated by a council of master teachers under him. His 
guidance was of course paramount.
Thoth designed the logo for the Academy, which is pictured in 
my own rendition above. A triangle rests on a T-square. These much later will 
become masonic symbols, but Thoth first initiated them in esoteric symbology. 
The triangle representing unification and further delineation of the Three-Fold 
Creatrix of the universe, which in a later era would be seen as "Father, Son and 
Holy Ghost, but cosmically as the Three-Fold Creatix is three white light holes 
(not black holes) which pour out the divine light for creating and organizing 
universes. The feather in the center of the triangle was the symbol for 
inscription of Light Language into the Greater Akashic.
The T-Square for Thoth was the foundation or leveling place 
where all came together as a foundational formation in the Earth.  It is 
the anchor. The interlocking serpents within this symbol were to represent the 
creative power itself...found in all things and in Earth's nature as a dual 
couplet of continual perpetuation. As one plays against the tension of the 
other, so the it takes on the tension and the "other" relaxes. Then this process 
is reversed.
Altogether this symbol was the defining synergy of universal 
continuity and unification.
It has been shown to me that Semik Ra'Hanok 
now exists in Numis'OM of the New Earth Star. It is not identical to the ancient 
version, as transformation occurs in the passage into New Earth vibration. It is 
now even more into the greater levels of harmonic than it was in Egyptos.
I feel I was guided by ThothHorRa (Thoth in 
his New Earth embodiment) to establish a "New Earth Academy of ON" on a sky 
platform above the New Earth Star Island Estate (NESIE) in the virtual world of 
Second Life. While it is not to be compared with THE Academy of ON of the 
ancient or New Earth versions, this one is under that umbrella of Light and for 
our current and mortal purposes allows those of us in the NESIE Community to 
experience some of the energetic connections. In January of 2010 we will 
officially begin holding instruction on various spiritual topics, not only given 
by myself but other members of the community as well.
On another note:in December of 2009 I gave a class discourse on 
Symbology at the Moon Temple of Moon Valley Sanctuary (another spiritual 
organization in Second Life) and recorded it.This first discourse is  available to everyone. In the future I plan 
to record many more classes in the NESIE Academy and these will be 
available here as part of your 44:44 Ascension Portal subscription. They may possibly also be placed for sale in the Spirit Store for non-subscribers.
Click hereto see photographs I have taken of the New Earth Academy of 
ON above NESIE.

Inter-Dimensional Healingby Maia Christianne Mallika


When we think of the term “inter-dimensional” we tend to associate it with a 
supra-state of being occupied by Angels, Ultra Beings and a few rare human yogis 
and sages. Yet WE are inter-dimensional beings - every one of us! Most of 
humanity simply is not aware in the moment of that truth... truly aware. Within 
our atomic structure and DNA micro-energy streamings are constantly moving in 
and out and through other states or dimensions than the one we perceive we 
inhabit. What THR (ThothHorRa) calls the “magna-soul” or over-soul projects into 
various dimensional zones of Earth and sometimes energetically associated 
planets, while we live and breath this incarnation in what we know as the “here 
and now.”
So why it is we are not experiencing these things - this “Other” of 
our selves? Because the wavelength of our perception does not have enough 
bandwidth to support it. The reason for this is that our awareness is not 
expanded to the degree of supporting the expanded bandwidth! We have created a 
world orientated consensual reality that is like a bubble containing our 
awareness and thus bandwidth. It is a membrane that absorbs the bandwidth of 
energy levels. Think of a point of energy in the center of a bubble. The energy 
point expands, sending out it’s energy in an expanding bandwidth until it 
reaches the barrier of the bubble. This energy then spreads out on surface of 
the bubble, so that the whole bubble absorbs the energy waves. This stabilizes 
the energy and keeps it central to the internal properties of it’s domain (the 
world construct we inhabit). Without this stabilization we would all promptly 
lose our minds as we simply would not be able to handle an ever-expanding 
bandwidth!
The big question is then: why can’t we handle it? Some few humans on 
  this planet would seem able to, such as yogis and sages. The answer is simple. 
  They switch the channel. They are able to move into a state of pure awareness 
  that does not require “bandwidth” or rather a conduit through which their energy 
  must travel. They instead move into the medium of Zero Point Energy (ZPE), a state of 
  perpetual STILLNESS where all simply IS - operating outside of polarities. 
This is what THR calls the "Attasic Universe." From that stillpoint ALL dimensions are 
  accessible for truly then, ALL IS ONE. From this place they can still interact 
  with moving energy, but they are not of that energy.So let us come back to humanity as inter-dimensional beings. Okay so we ARE but 
  most are not accessing it. I did not say ‘cannot’ but are not. The secret to 
  tapping into our inter-dimensional being is to first realize that we do not have 
  to consume the whole seven-course meal at once. We can sit at the table and eat 
  just a little of what we need at the time. In other words there are degrees of 
  access to our on-going state of inter-dimensional being. In fact we already do 
  this. Our minds and the organism of the brain which the mind uses to “channel” 
  into the body could not operate in it’s marvelous complexity without 
  inter-dimensional awareness. We just don’t realize we are thinking 
  inter-dimensionally...that is on more than one dimension at a time...but indeed 
  we are.
Now when we train ourselves to feel this, to recognize that our 
  mind-brain complex and thus our thinking is inter-dimensional, then we begin to 
  become more aware of our whole inter-dimensional state as it operates within the 
  human body (which is only a portion of the whole inter-dimensional beings we 
  are). When we become more connected to the human body’s inter-dimensional 
  exchange of information - between dimensions of it’s own continuity as a living 
  organism - then we can truly heal ourselves and open the door to help others 
  heal themselves in a direct Source-to-Source application of quantum physics.
People in this Age are already developing techniques and means to stimulate our 
awareness connection to the inter-dimensional human body... to aid us in 
“switching the channel” at least within the human condition. Some are calling it 
“re-programming” and to some extent it is... but true re-connection of awareness 
to our inter-dimensional being goes beyond “programming’ to embrace a full 
spectrum of quantum leaps in consciousness. In the New Earth Star realm of 
Numis’OM the AUUM Network Healers are currently aiding this world’s humanity 
through what they call “reflectivity.” They reflect their full spectrum 
awareness (and thus inter-dimensionality) upon individual human beings who are 
receptive to receive it.
Now these receptive humans do not then become fully 
  aware, but the DO carry a level of that awareness as a reflective aura within 
  them that they can then use to “see” a true part of their Nature wherein the 
  path to full spectrum awareness abides within them. This is a form of 
  inter-dimensional healing...whether it is facilitated by the AUUM, a friend or 
  practioner or coming from a powerful inner awakening trigger through 
  circumstance in the individual’s life, such as a near-death experience.The Master Isho'a (Jesus) had achieved the zenith of inter-dimensional awareness 
  in a human being. Yet he was able to be and to interact with other humans on a 
  very simple and intrinsic level. This was because abiding in multiple dimensions 
  is our natural state. Thus people were drawn to Isho'a as a human being for they 
  felt that natural state so fully within his awareness and it was calling them to 
  recognize their natural dimensionality.Becoming more aware is a natural progression for humanity - just as is our 
  planet moving through it’s stages of progression as it’s whole body slows down 
  and eventually ‘dies’ to this current pattern of conformity. Like the Earth and 
  as part of it, we will then arise Phoenix-Born, into a greater Heaven of our 
  inter-dimensional experience. Yet in the NOW we have at hand what we need for a 
  preview of and a movement toward abiding fully in our natural state as an 
  inter-dimensional being. The ancients of Mu (Lemuria) called it Tanghasangii, 
  meaning abiding in the sacred nature.
All of mypersonalized energy art(Merkabah Logos, Healing Mandalas and Ark Name 
template) is attuned to aiding one in moving into the Zero Point Energy zone 
within their being...on some level of their experience.
Thememunite 
crystalsare the actual transducers of inter-dimensional energy.

the bubble, so that the whole bubble absorbs the energy waves. This stabilizes 
the energy and keeps it central to the internal properties of it’s domain (the 
world construct we inhabit). Without this stabilization we would all promptly 
lose our minds as we simply would not be able to handle an ever-expanding 
bandwidth!
The big question is then: why can’t we handle it? Some few humans on 
  this planet would seem able to, such as yogis and sages. The answer is simple. 
  They switch the channel. They are able to move into a state of pure awareness 
  that does not require “bandwidth” or rather a conduit through which their energy 
  must travel. They instead move into the medium of Zero Point Energy (ZPE), a state of 
  perpetual STILLNESS where all simply IS - operating outside of polarities. 
This is what THR calls the "Attasic Universe." From that stillpoint ALL dimensions are 
  accessible for truly then, ALL IS ONE. From this place they can still interact 
  with moving energy, but they are not of that energy.So let us come back to humanity as inter-dimensional beings. Okay so we ARE but 
  most are not accessing it. I did not say ‘cannot’ but are not. The secret to 
  tapping into our inter-dimensional being is to first realize that we do not have 
  to consume the whole seven-course meal at once. We can sit at the table and eat 
  just a little of what we need at the time. In other words there are degrees of 
  access to our on-going state of inter-dimensional being. In fact we already do 
  this. Our minds and the organism of the brain which the mind uses to “channel” 
  into the body could not operate in it’s marvelous complexity without 
  inter-dimensional awareness. We just don’t realize we are thinking 
  inter-dimensionally...that is on more than one dimension at a time...but indeed 
  we are.
Now when we train ourselves to feel this, to recognize that our 
  mind-brain complex and thus our thinking is inter-dimensional, then we begin to 
  become more aware of our whole inter-dimensional state as it operates within the 
  human body (which is only a portion of the whole inter-dimensional beings we 
  are). When we become more connected to the human body’s inter-dimensional 
  exchange of information - between dimensions of it’s own continuity as a living 
  organism - then we can truly heal ourselves and open the door to help others 
  heal themselves in a direct Source-to-Source application of quantum physics.
People in this Age are already developing techniques and means to stimulate our 
awareness connection to the inter-dimensional human body... to aid us in 
“switching the channel” at least within the human condition. Some are calling it 
“re-programming” and to some extent it is... but true re-connection of awareness 
to our inter-dimensional being goes beyond “programming’ to embrace a full 
spectrum of quantum leaps in consciousness. In the New Earth Star realm of 
Numis’OM the AUUM Network Healers are currently aiding this world’s humanity 
through what they call “reflectivity.” They reflect their full spectrum 
awareness (and thus inter-dimensionality) upon individual human beings who are 
receptive to receive it.
Now these receptive humans do not then become fully 
  aware, but the DO carry a level of that awareness as a reflective aura within 
  them that they can then use to “see” a true part of their Nature wherein the 
  path to full spectrum awareness abides within them. This is a form of 
  inter-dimensional healing...whether it is facilitated by the AUUM, a friend or 
  practioner or coming from a powerful inner awakening trigger through 
  circumstance in the individual’s life, such as a near-death experience.The Master Isho'a (Jesus) had achieved the zenith of inter-dimensional awareness 
  in a human being. Yet he was able to be and to interact with other humans on a 
  very simple and intrinsic level. This was because abiding in multiple dimensions 
  is our natural state. Thus people were drawn to Isho'a as a human being for they 
  felt that natural state so fully within his awareness and it was calling them to 
  recognize their natural dimensionality.Becoming more aware is a natural progression for humanity - just as is our 
  planet moving through it’s stages of progression as it’s whole body slows down 
  and eventually ‘dies’ to this current pattern of conformity. Like the Earth and 
  as part of it, we will then arise Phoenix-Born, into a greater Heaven of our 
  inter-dimensional experience. Yet in the NOW we have at hand what we need for a 
  preview of and a movement toward abiding fully in our natural state as an 
  inter-dimensional being. The ancients of Mu (Lemuria) called it Tanghasangii, 
  meaning abiding in the sacred nature.
All of mypersonalized energy art(Merkabah Logos, Healing Mandalas and Ark Name 
template) is attuned to aiding one in moving into the Zero Point Energy zone 
within their being...on some level of their experience.

crystalsare the actual transducers of inter-dimensional energy.

The Mem-Star Merkabah

Memunite Crystals, and Universal Membranes



Before reading this article I suggest you 
readMemunite Crystals.

The memunite 
crystalline particles are the smallest and most "instant" elements of the 
universe. By "instant" I mean that they were created the very instant the 
universe came into being through what the scientists call the "Big Bang." They 
are the pure streaming of the Christos. The word "Christos" is not used in the 
context to denote a religious belief, but as a sacred streaming from the HEART 
of SOURCE which we all contain in our being to some extent, and the Master 
I'shoa (Jesus) incarnated more fully than any other human being on Earth up to 
this time.

In the mid 
1990's my inner-planes mentor ThothHorRa (THR) began referring to the "universal 
membranes." He did not give me information in detail, nor at the time did I seek 
it from my akashic insights. Up to that point I had never heard of universal 
membranes or "M Theory." I had heard about "String Theory" but never really read 
anything definitive on it. THR had told me years before that there were many 
universes. It is not my intention with this article to delve into the M Theory 
but I will place some reference links at the end for those who wish to pursue it 
further. In brief, from Wikipedia:

"In 
theoretical physics, M-theory is a new limit of string theory in which 11 
dimensions of spacetime may be identified. Because the dimensionality exceeds 
the dimensionality of five superstring theories in 10 dimensions, it was 
originally believed that the 11-dimensional theory is more fundamental and 
unifies all string theories (and supersedes them). However, in a more modern 
understanding, it is another, sixth possible description of physics of the full 
theory that is still called "string theory." Though a full description of the 
theory is not yet known, the low-entropy dynamics are known to be supergravity 
interacting with 2- and 5-dimensional membranes."

According to 
THR and my akashic insights there are an infinite number of dimensions, but the 
"11" fits the pattern of one level of "nesting" mem-star merkabahs (MSM). MSM 
are conglomerates of memunite crystalline particles which are drawn together 
through a type of gravity as yet undiscovered which I will call here "wave-form 
gravity" as it oscillates like a current across the skin of the universal 
membranes, causing those membrane skins themselves to move in wave-like 
patterns.

Each particle 
of the memunite is charged with a specific code that "calls" it to nest with 
other memunite particles containing the same code. This code information is 
transferred through the wave-form gravity field running along the skin of the 
universal membranes. The memunites therefore form in conglomerates on the skin 
of the membranes. These conglomerates create mem-stars like marvelous 
snowflakes. the mem-stars in turn "nest" with other mem-stars through the 
oscillations of the wave-form gravity field.

Now here is the true beauty 
of it...

When a certain 
"magic number" sequence of mem-stars (each carry DNA-like string patterns, ie 
numeric bandings) come together in a nest they "light up" like a Christmas Tree 
and send a burst of radiant LOVE-LIGHT throughout the entire skin of the 
membrane! So these little mem-stars are bursting forth from their nestings this 
sacred LIGHT here, there and everywhere.

EVERYTHING is 
composed of membranes with the mem-stars lighting up in burst patterns upon it. 
WE are composed of this starry stuff! Our auras emanate from these bursts of mem-light. We do not see them in bursts because the time between the "burstings" 
is too minute for our senses, but auras do pulse from the micro-bursts of the 
mem-stars.

The MSMs 
respond also to our thoughts and feelings...the energy information we send to 
them...of which we are a part. We ARE the MSMs and they are US. When we have 
negative thoughts and feelings we slow the "burstings" of light in our mem-star 
merkabahs. When we attune to the MSMs through being in touch with out CORE - 
that is, becoming more heart-coherent - then we allow the MEM's full range of 
their pulse-potential along the membranes of our composition. Remember there is 
no separation from "our" membranes and those of the most distant star! So what 
signals we send out through membranes within us, OF us are received throughout 
the universe!

The next time 
you "meditate" FEEL that connectiveness and visualize the mem-star merkabahs 
firing off their light on the surface of the membranes composing your energy 
bodies. This will help keep the pathways clear to allow full potential of the 
MSMs to fill your Being.

There is a 
vocalization you can use also to help clear the pathways of the MSM connection: 
AUUM-AHHH-UUU.

Maia / Starheart in her Na'vi Avatar
New Earth Star and Pandoraby Maia Alaula Kamala

Since the mid-1980's I have been writing about the New Earth 

Star: our ascended future reality - yet also co-existing with our present Earth. 

When I recently (1/10) watched the motion picture AVATAR I was stunned by the 

world Pandora's similarity to Numis'OM, the first stage of the New Earth Star 

world experience. The producer of the movie, James Cameron was shown Pandora in 

a dream over 10 years ago.
The Nav'i cat-beings of Pandora DO exist in Numis'OM. 

ThothHorRa calls them the "Kuri." They are a Sirian race originally stemming from a larger gene-pool of Sirians, feline in nature, mixed with human genetics to one degree or 

another. Several of the Sirian Races are in Numis'OM.
The glowing plants of Pandora are like the ones in Numis'OM. 

The inter-connectedness of the roots of the trees with ALL LIFE of Pandora the 

same as in the New Earth.
TheLotus Lociof Numis'OM are seen in Pandora as the "Seeds 

of the Tree." In Pandora they are small and white. In the New Earth some are 

small and some are white, but most are large and colorful.
In the move AVATAR there are violent animals and even the 

Na'vi kill to eat, but in Numis'OM there is no need for that, as it is a world 

of pure manifestation.
Here is a brief slideshow of some of my past art images reflecting Numis'OM which reveal a veryPandora-like world.
Nothing has to date affected audiences as has the movie 

AVATAR. There are many who are even saying they found themselves depressed 

having to leave it behind in the theatre - wishing to stay on Pandora! Of course 

beautiful fantasies tend to effect people in that way as we long to escape our 

everyday challenges. Yet I believe there is far more to it than that, and 

Pandora expresses it more dynamically before us than anything previously has 

been able to. "Fantasy" comes from the "imagination" which is a state of being 

in which we tap into other realms of very real experience. Some of what we 

receive is distorted by our own fears and desires, but much of it reveals other 

states of being. Minus the box-office violence Pandora IS the New Earth Star and 

thus it is calling people in a powerful way to connect to their New Earth 

"beings" NOW (for all "future" is merely a limit we place on on cognitive 

awareness). Those who feel that must leave it behind when the theatre lights 

come on are experiencing the deep feelings of separation they have from their 

pure awareness.
The Na'vi /Kuri of Numis'OM
"Na'vi" is an actual name in the Old Language of Earth, 

meaningto ripen upon the vine."Kuri" means much the same:to become 

full in Grace.What then, do the Kuri of Numis'OM do...what sacred path do 

they hold open in the New Earth? According to my akashic insights they create a 

living link between the Earth and Humanity. Just as in the motion picture AVATAR 

they are the extended roots of the Mother Tree. They move through passages 

between the forming Numis'OM and our current Earth realm...touching into our 

Nature Elementals and nourishing them into transforming through the New Earth 

codes and frequencies in their (Kuri's) DNA. They have been with us a long 

while. They speak to us in rhythms of the sub-conscious where we are ebbing and 

flowing with the Divine Mother in the Earth.
Some of us - human beings of Earth - are Kuri in our "future" 

New Earth bodies (or at least one of our New Earth bodies). Many more resonate 

with the Na'vi / Kuri as they hold that bridging element between where we are 

now and where we are going, in a very pure and natural energy form. They are 

very much AT-ONE with the Lotus Loci (Seeds of the Mother Tree)and literally 

dwell among them in Numis'OM.

ThothHorRa Infusion with the "Seeds of the Tree"(as 

given to those gathered on NESIE in Second Life on 1/17/10)
ThothHorRa Khandr: ANU KA ~|~ Welcome AllLet us take a few moments of silence and go to the HEART.As in the motion picture AVATAR so in the NEW EARTH of Numis'OM the Lotus Loci 

(Seeds of the Mother Tree) are present. Yet they are also forming within the DNA 

of the human being in this current earth reality.This process is coming about 

through a bridging of Light Codes between the current Earth and New Earth, 

through the New Earth Hologram continuing to unfold.And what creates this Hologram? YOU do...all of earths kind. Despite all the 

travail...wars and greed upon Her surface GAIA is still calling you to Her 

shore. Because of this calling so the Children of the Mother respond. Even in 

the midst of raising the sword or throwing the stone...so the Children pause 

within and lift up their eyes to HER and say YES I choose you! They then fall 

back to their dreaming in the world..the things they create of the shards of the 

past that continue to then create THEM in the false dream.The Lotus Loci / Seeds of the Tree are the beings we all ARE in first form. That 

embryo of LIFE in the midst of the SEED is US...all of us. They harken now to a 

new form...a new path opening before you. OLD and yet NEW, for all is ONE.BID THEM WELCOME NOW IN YOUR MIDST....just as you see these little images descending upon you now (virtual Seeds of 

the Tree descending up the gathered avatars - see Seed Tree image above).Hold in your senses that they DO dwell within you...seeds...many seeds carrying 

the codes of your NEW BIRTHING. So now let us take some moments while I guide 

you through an infusion of the SEEDS OF THE TREE.[ThothHorRa Khandr: See yourself in an open field of luminous flowers all around 

the sky is crystals blue with pale rose and violets swirling gently through it. 

The air is scented with delicate heavenly aroma. Breathe deeply...relax and let 

GO of everything but the ESSENCE OF YOU.In the midst of the field of flowers all alive and glowing in LOVE so a SEED is 

planted from your heart into the rich soil. Do so now...PLANT THE SEED. As you 

bend to the sweet Earth waves of love come from HER to YOU and you know you are 

ONE with HER.You stand back now and watch as the Seed unfolds and sprouts before your eyes 

and the TREE GROWS like a dance upon the winds, graceful, taking LIFE by the 

hand and leading it upward into the sky.Growing, growing...expanding, always the motion upward like the eagle upon wing, 

and your SOUL flies upward with it, spiraling among the unfolding branches. It 

dances with the leafing beauty as the Trees seeks the sky.Ahhh such FREEDOM, PEACE and Eloquence...no lost moment here...all perfectly 

poised to be fullness and completion.The Tree now reaches its full height and mature glory before you as you now land 

at its roots and look up...up into the face of the MOTHER in this form of Her 

expression...and she smiles upon you...and her smile is the MILK of LIFE, the 

sweet sap of her Tree dripping like honey upon your tongue. As you TASTE of it 

you are able to speak the Language of the Trees who are the Keepers of her 

MUSIC.And the Words and the Music fill you. They cascade over your tongue and you sing 

Her SONG. Your body takes hold of Her breath and you DANCE her DANCE. You lift 

up once again and her branches enfold you, tender green leaves shelter you.You know now...You know her Language deep in your heart and you will never forget again. In all 

you say you will speak it and in all you do you will dance it; and in all your 

ARE you will BE it.I inscribe her symbols upon you now...in my very heart of hearts that reaches 

across the universe...so I speak her words to you and give you the key to her 

rhythm. For as one being does this for another so we find it to be true in every 

HEART the universe over.ANUWYE KU'ESHUE TOPARII KUME...It is so accomplished.Take another DEEP BREATHE of the SWEETNESS and the return to the "now" amongst 

us.Awaken to the new day!AND  SO IT IS.

Crysulims - The New Earth MerkabahsOur Starships Home!

art by Maia
The woman stood surrounded by the abundance of nature. she felt fresh, 
clean, re-born. Her senses were alive and clearer than she had ever known them 
to be....in any incarnation she had ever experienced, and now she was fully 
aware of them all. Yet all that was compressed in but a mere moment in time. She 
was entirely present in the expanded "Now" of this New Earth she stood upon. Yes 
she "stood" but...there was no sense of weight, only a marvelous feeling of 
connection, as if her body was growing right out of the soil and yet at the same 
time flying high above in the crystalline sky of the "New World." In the 
distance she heard birds singing, but the sound was fuller - with greater 
expression, for now she knew their language.
It was time, she could sense it. Her whole body responded as if it longed 
to expand even further, out into the lavender-blue sky. She lifted her arms and 
sang...singing the song of her Soul, which was a sound so revealing her heart 
burst into pure LIGHT and her joy knew no bounds. THIS was the I AM of her 
totality! Not as a "she" or "he" but as the very pureness of BEING.
As she continued to bring forth this glorious sound from within her, her 
heart became more and more radiant until her whole body glowed and was 
iridescent and with the transparency of a butterfly's wing. Traces of silken 
threads - pure honey-light, floating in the air, streamed gently from her body. 
The threads began to coalesce, coming together to from a beautiful, weaving 
pattern of color around her. This was her cocoon-merkabah, the crysulim which 
would continue to nurture her until her body was completely transformed into its 
"pure gem" state.
So as we first "appear" in the New Earth we will undergo the transformation 
within our crysulims. This will take place in stages, where the need to create 
the crysulim comes upon us and we stay within it for a period of "time" (time 
being present but as a much more dimensional experience). We will then take back 
the threads and go into other experiences, living our new lives...to return 
again into the crysulim later for another cycle of development and nourishment.
Imagine now if you will, the sensation of creating and being nourished for a 
time in your crysulim. It is spun from the radiance of the heart when this organ 
become fully active as a generator of LIGHT. We now live with hearts that are in 
the "hold" mode...pumping away to keep the engine running. When our hearts 
become "alive" and radiant they are at full capacity and capable of completely 
restructuring our body by turning on all the necessary codons of the DNA to make 
this happen.
FEEL how it would be to experience this...to open up and BE - all the senses, 
all the potential realized right NOW! Let out of the box. You can now fly free! 
Right now in this moment and repeatedly, you can go through this exercise of 
imagination and each time you do, you will bring the "future" into the present 
just a little bit more. This will allow you to recalibrate your starlight 
patterns and expand them, offering you greater potential for health and a sense 
of joy and well-being.
Radiant Heart(click image to enlarge)
